# Trident Documentation - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/#trident-documentation)

Trident Documentation[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/#trident-documentation "Permanent link")

========================================================================================================

Fuzzing is a technique to test the robustness of a program by providing it with random inputs.

Trident is a Manually Guided Fuzzing framework for Solana. It lets you to execute instructions of your Solana programs with random data and observe the changes in the state of the program.

Getting started[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/#getting-started "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [Installation](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/installation/)
     - Install the Trident Fuzz Testing Framework
*   [Start Fuzzing](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/)
     - Focus on security and start fuzzing immediately

Advanced fuzzing customization[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/#advanced-fuzzing-customization "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Explore the various features Trident provides.

*   [Transaction Hooks](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/)
     - Create and manipulate transactions with different methods
*   [Multi-Instruction Transactions](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/multi-instruction-transactions/)
     - Compose fuzzed transactions with multiple instructions
*   [Trident Manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/)
     - Customize your fuzz tests with different configurations
*   [Code Coverage](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/code-coverage/)
     - Track and display fuzz test code coverage
*   [Dashboard](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/)
     - A web-based interface for visualizing fuzzing session results
*   [Regression Testing](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/)
     - Track and compare fuzzing session results

API & Macros Reference[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/#api-macros-reference "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Check out the API and macro reference for Trident.

*   [Trident API & Macros](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/)
    

Trident Examples[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/#trident-examples "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Check out examples to learn how to use Trident.

*   [Trident Examples](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-examples/trident-examples/)
    

TridentSVM[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/#tridentsvm "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Check out the TridentSVM, lightweight fuzzing execution and account storage environment.

*   [TridentSVM](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-svm/)
    

What is Fuzzing ?[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/#what-is-fuzzing "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

_"Fuzz testing is an automated technique that provides generated random, invalid, or unexpected input data to your program. This helps discover unknown bugs and vulnerabilities, potentially preventing zero-day exploits."_

\--:--\--:--

Back to top

# Changelog - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/CHANGELOG/#changelog)

Changelog[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/CHANGELOG/#changelog "Permanent link")

=================================================================================================

All notable changes to this project will be documented in this file.

The format is based on [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.0.0/)
, and this project adheres to [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html)
 (SemVer).

**Note**: Version 0 of Semantic Versioning is handled differently from version 1 and above. The minor version will be incremented upon a breaking change and the patch version will be incremented for features.

\[dev\] - Unreleased[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/CHANGELOG/#dev-unreleased "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

**Removed**

**Changed**

\[0.11.1\] - 2025-10-21[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/CHANGELOG/#0111-2025-10-21 "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

**Removed**

*   Removed lld linker ([394](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/394)
    )

**Changed**

\[0.11.0\] - 2025-08-14[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/CHANGELOG/#0110-2025-08-14 "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   Add server for displaying content of fuzzing artifacts ([347](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/347)
    )
*   Add fuzz artifacts directory to the fuzz test folder ([343](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/343)
    )
*   Added state monitoring support for fuzzing metrics ([341](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/341)
    )
*   Added dashboard support for fuzzing metrics ([340](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/340)
    )
*   Code coverage tracking support enabled and configured via Trident.toml. Coverage data can be visualized using the VS Code extension [330](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/330)
    
*   Added features to enable syscalls in fuzzing ([329](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/329)
    )
*   Add `--skip-build` flag to only initialize fuzz test without building the project ([325](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/325)
    )
*   Add support for space, lamports and owner to TridentAccounts macro ([320](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/320)
    )

**Removed**

**Changed**

*   FuzzTest fields are now aggregated into Trident struct ([339](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/339)
    )
*   Add support for reproducible fuzzing with thread-specific seeds ([332](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/332)
    )
*   Move Trident.toml into trident-tests folder ([328](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/328)
    )
*   Conversion from AFL and Honggfuzz into Manually Guided Fuzzing ([324](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/324)
    )
*   Update template generation to use tera ([326](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/326)
    )

\[0.10.0\] - 2025-03-13[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/CHANGELOG/#0100-2025-03-13 "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   TransactionSelector allows to select and execute random transaction with hooks and without hooks ([297](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/297)
    )
*   Added "random\_tail" attribute to TridentFlowExecutor macro to allow random tail generation ([296](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/296)
    )
*   Added support for seeds constraint for accounts structs ([284](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/284)
    )
*   Additional methods accessing the AccountsStorage and creating corresponding accounts are now optional ("token","vote", "stake") ([279](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/279)
    )
*   Derive macros now use own syn parser for better extensibility and UX ([275](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/275)
    )
*   Program ID inside test\_fuzz.rs file is now automatically filled in is present in the program IDL ([272](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/272)
    )
*   Added additional attributes to TridentAccounts, mut and signer ([268](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/268)
    )
*   Users can now specify a program for which they want to add or initialize a fuzz test using `--program-name` flag ([273](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/273)
    )
*   Allow custom test name specification in fuzz test creation with `--test-name` flag ([274](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/274)
    )

**Removed**

*   The DisplayIx macro is now removed, Debug trait was implemented for instruction inputs ([281](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/281)
    )

**Changed**

*   FuzzTestExecutor and FlowExecutor are grouped together and FuzzTest has client as generic instead of TridentSVM ([294](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/294)
    )
*   Changed Transaction sequence logic ([289](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/289)
    )
*   AccountsStorages are simplified, no types are required to define ([276](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/276)
    )
*   Trident Architecture changes containing multiple features and improvements (details in the PR)([267](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/267)
    )
*   get or create token account methods fixed for native token accounts ([262](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/262)
    )

\[0.9.1\] - 2025-02-03[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/CHANGELOG/#091-2025-02-03 "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   added warp to time manipulation ([259](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/259)
    )
*   added methods to check if account storage is empty ([258](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/258)
    )
*   added support for post-instruction behavior ([257](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/257)
    )

**Removed**

**Changed**

\[0.9.0\] - 2025-01-15[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/CHANGELOG/#090-2025-01-15 "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   added support for composite accounts ([245](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/245)
    )
*   Trident SVM + AFL (see the PR for more details) ([234](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/234)
    )

**Removed**

*   removed fuzz\_iteration from test\_fuzz.rs ([243](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/243)
    )

**Changed**

*   renamed Config to TridentConfig ([246](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/246)
    )
*   errors are simplified and transaction error contains only transaction error ([244](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/244)
    )

\[0.8.1\] - 2024-11-14[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/CHANGELOG/#081-2024-11-14 "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Removed**

*   removed unnecessary deserialization with AccountsSnapshots, to deserialize data implementation AccountDeserialize can be used ([221](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/221)
    )

**Changed**

*   improve AccountsStorage module structure and remove unnecessary methods in FuzzClient ([223](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/223)
    )
*   improve manipulations with AccountsStorages in get\_accounts() function ([219](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/219)
    )

**Added**

*   add pre\_sequence!, middle\_sequence! and post\_sequence! for easier sequence definition ([220](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/220)
    )
*   add/ add support for Clock sysvar manipulations with the client(i.e. warp to slot/epoch and forward in time) ([217](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/217)
    )

\[0.8.0\] - 2024-10-21[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/CHANGELOG/#080-2024-10-21 "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   impr/ allow to specify programs and accounts in the Trident Manifest ([207](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/207)
    )
*   impr/ added get\_program\_id function to the IxOps and FuzzTestExecutor ([199](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/199)
    )

**Changed**

*   impr/ improve init command, modify program manifest automatically, add init force, add howto subcommand ([208](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/208)
    )
*   impr/ allow to derive AccountsSnapshots for empty Account Context ([209](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/209)
    )
*   impr/ fuzz flags are read at start of fuzzing session from Config instead of env variable and transaction dispatch was added to increase FuzzTestExecutor readability ([204](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/204)
    )
*   impr/ allow various instructions to be generated in case of multiple programs in the Anchor workspace ([200](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/200)
    )
*   feat/ option to add account into Fuzz Test environment with base64 data ([197](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/197)
    )
*   impr/ instead of parsing source code and creating our IDL, read anchor IDL ([198](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/196)
    )

**Removed**

*   del/remove integration tests supported by Trident, this feature adds more unnecessary overhead compared to its value ([196](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/198)
    )

**Fixed**

    )
*   fix/snapshot's zeroed account as optional ([#170](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/170)
    )

**Removed**

*   del/remove localnet subcommand ([178](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/178)
    )
*   del/remove unnecessary fuzzing feature as trident is mainly fuzzer ([#176](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/176)
    )
*   del/remove Trident explorer ([#171](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/171)
    )

\[0.5.0\] - 2023-08-28[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/CHANGELOG/#050-2023-08-28 "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   cli: Added trident subcommand `fuzz` to run and debug fuzz tests using honggfuzz-rs.
*   cli: Added trident `--skip-fuzzer` option for `init` subcommand to skip generation of fuzz test templates.
*   client: Added new Cargo feature `fuzzing` that enables optional dependencies related to fuzz testing.

\[0.4.1\] - 2023-08-21[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/CHANGELOG/#041-2023-08-21 "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Changed**

*   Upgrade Solana (`=1.16.6`) and Anchor framework (`=0.28.0`) versions.

**Fixed**

*   Implemented Anchor Client logic was not able to work with newer version of Anchor. Fixed with `async_rpc` and `async` feature.
*   Trident init IDL Parse Error on newer version of Rust, fixed with updated `accounts` token.

\[0.3.0\] - 2022-09-23[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/CHANGELOG/#030-2022-09-23 "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Changed**

*   Upgrade Solana (`~1.10`) and Anchor framework (`~0.25`) versions

**Added**

*   Custom Solana RPC error reporter. If the Solana RPC error is thrown, the error code, message and data (logs) are reported to the output.
*   Custom imports in the `.program_client`. User is able to import custom types and structures into program client. The import part of the code would not be re-generated.

\[0.2.0\] - 2022-07-27[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/CHANGELOG/#020-2022-07-27 "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   Trident is now configurable. This requires `Trident.toml` file to exist in the project's root directory - without this file the execution will fail. To solve this re-run `trident init` or just create an empty `Trident.toml` file in the project's root directory.

Back to top

---

# Commands - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#commands)

Commands[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#commands "Permanent link")

==============================================================================================

Trident CLI supports the following commands:

`trident init`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#trident-init "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Initializes Trident Workspace and generates new Fuzz Test Template. Creates the following structure:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-1) project-root [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-2) ├── trident-tests [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-3) │   ├── fuzz_0 # particular fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-4) │   │   ├── instructions # instructions folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-5) │   │   ├── transactions # transactions folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-6) │   │   ├── test_fuzz.rs # the binary target of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-7) │   │   ├── types.rs # the types of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-8) │   │   └── fuzz_instructions.rs # the definition of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-9) │   ├── fuzz_1 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-10) │   ├── fuzz_X # possible multiple fuzz tests [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-11) │   ├── fuzzing # compilations and crashes folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-12) │   ├── Cargo.toml [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-13) │   └── Trident.toml # Configuration file located in trident-tests directory [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-14) └── ...`

#### Options[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#options "Permanent link")

*   `-f, --force` - Force Trident initialization. Trident dependencies will be updated based on the version of Trident CLI.
*   `-s, --skip-build` - Skip building the program before initializing Trident.
*   `-p, --program-name <FILE>` - Specify the name of the program for which fuzz test will be generated.
*   `-t, --test-name <NAME>` - Name of the fuzz test to initialize.

* * *

`trident how`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#trident-how "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Show the HowTo message about writing fuzz tests.

* * *

`trident fuzz`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#trident-fuzz "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Run fuzz subcommands. With fuzz subcommands you can add new fuzz test template or you can run fuzz test on already initialized one.

**Examples:**

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#__codelineno-1-1) trident fuzz add [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#__codelineno-1-2) trident fuzz run fuzz_0 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#__codelineno-1-3) trident fuzz debug <FUZZ_TARGET> <SEED>`

### `trident fuzz add`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#trident-fuzz-add "Permanent link")

Generate new Fuzz Test template.

#### Options[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#options_1 "Permanent link")

*   `-p, --program-name <FILE>` - Specify the name of the program for which the fuzz test will be generated.
*   `-t, --test-name <NAME>` - Name of the fuzz test to add.
*   `-s, --skip-build` - Skip building the program before adding new fuzz test.

* * *

### `trident fuzz run <fuzz_target>`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#trident-fuzz-run-fuzz_target "Permanent link")

Directory Note

Execute fuzz tests from the `trident-tests` directory.

Solana Logs

In case you want to see the logs of the fuzzed transactions, prefix the command with `TRIDENT_LOG=1`.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#__codelineno-2-1) TRIDENT_LOG=1 trident fuzz run <fuzz_target>`

Runs the specified Fuzz Target using Trident's Manually Guided Fuzzing (e.g., fuzz\_0).

#### Arguments[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#arguments "Permanent link")

*   `<fuzz_target>` - Name of the desired fuzz template to execute (for example fuzz\_0).
*   `[seed]` - Master seed used for fuzzing, if not provided it will be generated randomly.

#### Options[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#options_2 "Permanent link")

*   `-w, --with-exit-code` - Run the fuzzing with exit code, i.e. if it discovers crash the Trident will exit with exit code 1.

* * *

### `trident fuzz debug <fuzz_target> <seed>`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#trident-fuzz-debug-fuzz_target-seed "Permanent link")

Debug crashes by analyzing specific crash files using the provided seed.

#### Arguments[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#arguments_1 "Permanent link")

*   `<fuzz_target>` - Name of the desired fuzz template to execute (for example fuzz\_0).
*   `<seed>` - Master seed of the desired fuzz template to execute.

Debug Output

The debug output includes:

1.  Transaction logs
2.  Instruction data structures
3.  Panic/Crash information

* * *

`trident clean`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#trident-clean "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Clean build target, additionally perform `anchor clean`.

* * *

`trident server`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#trident-server "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Starts the Trident Server, in order to make it easier to visualize the fuzzing dashboard, more info in the [dashboard](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/)
 section.

* * *

`trident compare`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/#trident-compare "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Allows you to compare two fuzzing regression results. More info in the [regression](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/)
 section.

* * *

Back to top

---

# FAQ - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/faq/#faq)

FAQ[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/faq/#faq "Permanent link")

===============================================================================

_Is Trident supported only with Anchor?_

*   Currently yes, Trident under the hood obtains data from the IDL generated by Anchor.

_I created the Fuzz Test, what should I do next?_

*   Start here [Start Fuzzing](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/)
    .

_Is Trident open-source?_

*   Yes, here [Trident](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident)
    .

_I would like to report an Issue with Trident, what should I do?_

*   Create [issue](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/issues)
    .

_Is Trident deployed on Mainnet / Devnet / Testnet?_

*   No, Trident is Fuzz Testing Framework, not Solana Program.

_What type of Fuzzer is Trident?_

*   Currently, we refer to it as _"coverage guided gray box fuzzer"_.

Back to top

---

# Installation - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/installation/#installation)

Installation[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/installation/#installation "Permanent link")

==========================================================================================================

Trident requires the following prerequisites:

Prerequisites

Before proceeding, ensure you have installed:

*   [Rust](https://www.rust-lang.org/tools/install)
     (stable version)
*   [Solana CLI](https://solana.com/docs/intro/installation)
    
*   [Anchor](https://www.anchor-lang.com/docs/installation)
    

Check out [supported versions](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/installation/#supported-versions)
 for version compatibility.

Install Trident[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/installation/#install-trident "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/installation/#__codelineno-0-1) cargo install trident-cli`

You can also use the `version` flag to install a specific version:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/installation/#__codelineno-1-1) cargo install trident-cli --version x.y.z`

Install cargo-llvm-cov[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/installation/#install-cargo-llvm-cov "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To enable code coverage tracking during fuzzing, install [cargo-llvm-cov](https://github.com/taiki-e/cargo-llvm-cov)
:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/installation/#__codelineno-2-1) cargo +stable install cargo-llvm-cov --locked`

Supported versions[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/installation/#supported-versions "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Version Table Legend

*   \= Develop branch
*   \= Released version
*   `-` = Not required/supported

| **Version Type** | **Anchor** | **Solana** | **Rust** | **Honggfuzz** | **AFL** |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Development | `>=0.29.0` | `>=1.17.3` | `1.86` | `-` | `-` |
| **Current (0.11.x)** | `>=0.29.0` | `>=1.17.3` | `1.86` | `-` | `-` |
| **0.10.x** | `>=0.29.0 < 0.31.0` | `>=1.17.3 < 2.1` | `nightly` | `0.5.56` | `0.15.11` |
| **0.9.x** | `>=0.29.0 < 0.31.0` | `>=1.17.3 < 2.1` | `nightly` | `0.5.56` | `0.15.11` |
| **0.8.x** | `0.30.1` | `^1.17.4` | `nightly` | `0.5.56` | `-` |
| **0.7.x** | `>=0.29.*` | `^1.17.4` | `nightly` | `0.5.56` | `-` |
| **0.6.x** | `>=0.29.*` | `^1.17` | `nightly` | `0.5.55` | `-` |
| **0.5.x** | `~0.28.*` | `=1.16.6` | `-` | `-` | `-` |
| **0.4.x** | `~0.27.*` | `>=1.15` | `-` | `-` | `-` |
| **0.3.x** | `~0.25.*` | `>=1.10` | `-` | `-` | `-` |
| **0.2.x** | `~0.24.*` | `>=1.9` | `-` | `-` | `-` |

# Start Fuzzing - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/#start-fuzzing)

Start Fuzzing[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/#start-fuzzing "Permanent link")

======================================================================================================

To start writing fuzz tests, you need to initialize Trident in your Anchor-based workspace.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-0-1) trident init`

If you have already initialized Trident, you can add a new fuzz test using:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-1-1) trident fuzz add`

Trident creates a new fuzz test template in the `trident-tests` directory, with the following structure:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-1) project-root [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-2) ├── trident-tests [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-3) │   ├── fuzz_0 # particular fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-4) │   │   ├── instructions # instructions folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-5) │   │   ├── transactions # transactions folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-6) │   │   ├── test_fuzz.rs # the binary target of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-7) │   │   ├── types.rs # the types of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-8) │   │   └── fuzz_instructions.rs # the definition of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-9) │   ├── fuzz_1 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-10) │   ├── fuzz_X # possible multiple fuzz tests [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-11) │   ├── fuzzing # compilations and crashes folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-12) │   ├── Cargo.toml [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-13) │   └── Trident.toml [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-14) └── ...`

`Instructions` folder contains the `instructions` that can be used in the fuzz test.

`Transactions` folder contains the `transactions` that will be used during the fuzzing, each transaction can contain `one` or `multiple instructions`, based on the developer's choice. By default there is only one instruction in each transaction.

Back to top

---

# Executing the Fuzz Test - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#executing-the-fuzz-test)

Executing the Fuzz Test[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#executing-the-fuzz-test "Permanent link")

==============================================================================================================================================

To execute the fuzz test, navigate to the `trident-tests` directory and run the following command to execute the fuzz test:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-0-1) trident fuzz run <FUZZ_TARGET> <SEED> [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-0-2) # for example: [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-0-3) # trident fuzz run fuzz_0 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-0-4) # seed is optional, if not provided, a random seed will be used`

Directory Note

Execute fuzz tests from the `trident-tests` directory.

Solana Logs

In case you want to see the logs of the fuzzed transactions, prefix the command with `TRIDENT_LOG=1`.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-1-1) TRIDENT_LOG=1 trident fuzz run <fuzz_target> <seed>`

For the output reference and additional options such as debugging the found issues, check out [Commands](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/basics/commands/)
.

For the additional customization through the `trident.toml` file, check out the [Trident Manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/)
 page.

Back to top

---

# Writing fuzz test - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/#writing-fuzz-test)

Writing fuzz test[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/#writing-fuzz-test "Permanent link")

=================================================================================================================================

Trident is Manually Guided fuzzing framework for Solana programs.

In order to start fuzzing, you need to guide the fuzzer by specifying what are the expected inputs to instruction or the expected sequences of instructions to execute.

**Why is this important?**

Letting the fuzzer to generate completely random instruction inputs and completely random sequences of instruction would lead in most case

*   to transaction failures, which would mean the fuzzer is not properly fuzzing the logic within the program; and
*   executing irrelevant random instruction sequences, which would again lead to transaction failures.

Guide the fuzzer[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/#guide-the-fuzzer "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Start with properly configuring different types of instruction inputs:

*   [Instruction Data](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-data/)
    
*   [Instruction Accounts](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/)
    
*   [Fuzzing Flows](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/)
    
*   (Optional) [Remaining Accounts](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/)
    

Back to top

---

# Fuzzing Flows - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#fuzzing-flows)

Fuzzing Flows[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#fuzzing-flows "Permanent link")

=======================================================================================================================================

Before you start fuzzing, you need to guide the fuzzer on which transactions it should execute. This is important because if your program contains a lot of instructions and we let the fuzzer randomly pick from them, most of the time the fuzzer would pick incorrect sequences. This is due to the fact that Solana programs expect some kind of order. For example, DeFi protocols most likely expect something like:

1.  Initialize Config
2.  Initialize User
3.  User deposit
4.  User swap (there might be multiple swaps, with random order, this is achieved with flows)
5.  User withdraw
6.  User account remove
7.  Collect trading fees
8.  ...

For that reason, it is required to slightly guide the fuzzer. The following code shows the default state of the `test_fuzz.rs` file.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-0-1) #[derive(FuzzTestMethods)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-0-2) struct FuzzTest {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-0-3)     /// for fuzzing    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-0-4)     trident: Trident,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-0-5)     /// for storing fuzzing accounts    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-0-6)     fuzz_accounts: FuzzAccounts, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-0-7) } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-0-8)[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-0-9) #[flow_executor] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-0-10) impl FuzzTest {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-0-11)     fn new() -> Self {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-0-12)         Self { [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-0-14)             fuzz_accounts: FuzzAccounts::default(),        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-0-15)         } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-0-31)     fn flow2(&mut self) { [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-0-45) }`

Let's describe the `test_fuzz.rs` file.

The main[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#the-main "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-1-1) fn main() {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-1-2)     FuzzTest::fuzz(1000, 100); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-1-3) }`

This is the starting point of the fuzzing. Here you can specify how many iterations you want to run and how many flows you want to execute in each iteration. Flows are described below.

The `FuzzTest` struct[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#the-fuzztest-struct "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is a struct containing Trident, which contains multiple methods for fuzzing, collecting fuzzing metrics, etc., and FuzzAccounts, which is used to store account IDs and their corresponding Pubkeys (addresses).

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-2-1) #[derive(FuzzTestMethods)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-2-2) struct FuzzTest {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-2-3)     /// for fuzzing    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-2-4)     trident: Trident,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-2-5)     /// for storing fuzzing accounts    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-2-6)     fuzz_accounts: FuzzAccounts, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-2-7) }`

The `impl FuzzTest` block[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#the-impl-fuzztest-block "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This is the main block where you guide the fuzzer to perform the fuzzing.

### The `new` method[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#the-new-method "Permanent link")

The `new` method is called once at the start of the fuzzing. It is used to initialize the fuzzer and the fuzzing accounts to their default state (so empty).

### The `#[init]` method[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#the-init-method "Permanent link")

The `#[init]` method is executed at the start of each iteration. As described above, it is possible to specify the number of iterations and flows, meaning that this `#[init]` method will be executed at the start of each iteration. Within it, you can perform execution of transactions which should initialize something in your program, for example Global Config, User account, Token Accounts, etc.

### The `#[flow]` method[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#the-flow-method "Permanent link")

Methods marked with `#[flow]` are where the fuzzing happens (apart from the fact that the instructions contain random data on their inputs). Methods marked with `#[flow]` are selected randomly from other flows and executed in random order.

As shown in the source code below, the `flow1` and `flow2` methods are marked with `#[flow]`. This means, in each iteration, 100 flow methods will be selected in random order and the logic specified in the methods will be executed. So if we have two flow methods, the random order can be `flow1`, `flow1`, `flow2`, `flow2`, `flow1`, `flow1`, etc., until 100 flows are executed.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-3-1) #[flow_executor] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-3-2) impl FuzzTest { An example[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#an-example "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

As an example:

*   Within the block below, we have 4 flows. The `start` method is executed at the start of each iteration. The `flow1`, `flow2`, `flow3`, and `flow4` methods are executed in random order in each iteration.
*   There will be 1000 iterations and 100 flows executed in each iteration.
*   A random order of `MoveEastTransaction`, `MoveSouthTransaction`, `MoveNorthTransaction`, and `MoveWestTransaction` will be executed in each iteration, due to the fact that they are marked with `#[flow]`.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-4-1) #[flow_executor] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-4-2) impl FuzzTest {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-4-3)     fn new() -> Self {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-4-4)         Self {            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-4-5)             trident: Trident::default(),            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-4-6)             fuzz_accounts: FuzzAccounts::default(),        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-4-7)         }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-4-8)     }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-4-9)     #[init]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-4-10)     fn start(&mut self) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-4-11)         let mut tx = InitializeTransaction::build(&mut self.trident, &mut self.fuzz_accounts); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-4-12)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-4-13)         self.trident            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/#__codelineno-4-14)             .execute_transaction(&mut tx, Some("Initialize")); ---

# Instruction Accounts - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#instruction-accounts)

Instruction Accounts[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#instruction-accounts "Permanent link")

============================================================================================================================================================

Accounts are storage entities on the Solana Blockchain. They may be simple wallets (consisting of regular keypairs) or accounts with more complex address structures, such as Program Derived Addresses (PDAs).

During fuzzing, Trident sends random Accounts to the program's instructions. However, the account addresses are not completely random but are taken from the Fuzz Test's account storage. Trident generates random indexes to the account storage. This approach is crucial, as allowing the fuzzer to generate completely random account addresses would lead to many failed transactions (i.e., nothing would be fuzzed).

Your responsibility is to guide Trident on which storage locations it should retrieve accounts from. Additionally, if particular account types are expected, such as Token Account, Mint Account, etc., your responsibility is to initialize them within the `set_accounts` method.

Setup Instruction Accounts[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#setup-instruction-accounts "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are two ways to guide the fuzzer about which storage locations to retrieve accounts from:

1.  Using the `TridentAccounts` macro
2.  Manually setting the accounts using the `set_accounts` method

### Using the TridentAccounts Macro[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#using-the-tridentaccounts-macro "Permanent link")

The `TridentAccounts` macro is used to derive account handling functionality for instruction accounts (similar to the Context structure in Anchor-based programs).

You can check the [TridentAccounts attributes](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/)
 page to see the attributes that can be used.

Consider the following example:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-0-1) /// Instruction Accounts [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-0-2) #[derive(Arbitrary, Debug, Clone, TridentAccounts)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-0-3) #[instruction_data(InitializeFnInstructionData)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-0-4) #[storage(FuzzAccounts)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-0-5) pub struct InitializeFnInstructionAccounts {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-0-6)     #[account(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-0-7)         mut,        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-0-8)         signer,        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-0-9)         storage = author,        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-0-10)         storage::account_id = (0..1)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-0-11)     )]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-0-12)     pub author: TridentAccount,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-0-13)     #[account(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-0-14)         mut,        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-0-15)         storage::name = hello_world_account,        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-0-16)         storage::account_id = (0..3)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-0-17)         seeds = [b"hello_world_seed"],    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-0-18)     )]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-0-19)     pub hello_world_account: TridentAccount,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-0-20)     #[account(address = "11111111111111111111111111111111", skip_snapshot)]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-0-21)     pub system_program: TridentAccount, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-0-22) }`

The example specifies these attributes:

*   `#[instruction_data(InitializeFnInstructionData)]` - Specifies the instruction data type (helpful if instruction data input is part of PDA seeds)
*   `#[storage(FuzzAccounts)]` - Specifies the account storage type
*   `mut` - Marks the account as mutable
*   `signer` - Marks the account as a transaction signer
*   `storage::name = <target_account_storage>` - Links the account to a storage location for address retrieval
*   `storage::account_id = (0..3)` - Randomly generates an account id from the range of values, this is particularly helpful if you want to try to send different accounts to the instruction
*   `address = "..."` - Sets a constant address for the account
*   `seeds = [b"hello_world_seed"]` - Specifies the seeds for Program Derived Addresses (PDAs)
*   `skip_snapshot` - Excludes the account from snapshot creation

### Manual Accounts Setup[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#manual-accounts-setup "Permanent link")

If you need more control than the `TridentAccounts` macro provides, you can manually set up accounts using the `set_accounts` function:

Precedence of `set_accounts`

The `set_accounts` method takes precedence over the `TridentAccounts` macro attributes. Any behavior defined in the `set_accounts` method will override the behavior defined in the `TridentAccounts` macro.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-1-1) impl InstructionSetters for ExampleInstruction {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-1-2)     type IxAccounts = FuzzAccounts; [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-1-3)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-1-4)     fn set_accounts(&mut self, trident: &mut Trident, fuzz_accounts: &mut Self::IxAccounts) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-1-5)         // Generate random account id        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-1-6)         let account_id = trident.gen_range(0..3); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-1-7)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-1-8)         // Create and store a PDA        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-1-9)         let hello_world_account = fuzz_accounts.hello_world_account.get_or_create(            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-1-10)             account_id,            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-1-11)             trident,            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-1-12)             Some(PdaSeeds::new(&[b"hello_world_seed"], self.get_program_id())),            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-1-13)             None,        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-1-14)         ); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-1-15)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-1-16)         // Set the account address        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-1-17)         self.accounts            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-1-18)             .hello_world_account            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-1-19)             .set_address(hello_world_account);    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-1-20)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/#__codelineno-1-21) }`

In the previous examples:

*   We configured the fuzzer to always keep the `author` account as a `signer` and as `mutable`. It will be stored in the `FuzzAccounts::author` storage, and the account id will be randomly generated from the range of 0 to 1.
*   We configured the fuzzer to always keep the `hello_world_account` as a `mutable` account, which will be stored in the `FuzzAccounts::hello_world_account` storage, and it will be a PDA with an address derived from the `seeds` attribute, and the account id will be randomly generated from the range of 0 to 3.
*   We configured the fuzzer to always keep the `system_program` account as a `constant`. Snapshots of this account before and after the instruction execution will not be taken.

Back to top

# Instruction Data - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-data/#instruction-data)

Instruction Data[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-data/#instruction-data "Permanent link")

================================================================================================================================================

Instructions on Solana can have parameters. Trident lets you to send random data as the instruction parameters.

Manual Data Setup[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-data/#manual-data-setup "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The following example shows how to specify what data should be sent to the instruction. In this case we are guiding the Trident to always generate random number from 0 to `u8::MAX` and use it as the `input` parameter of the instruction.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-data/#__codelineno-0-1) impl InstructionSetters for DepositObligationCollateralV2Instruction {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-data/#__codelineno-0-2)     type IxAccounts = FuzzAccounts; [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-data/#__codelineno-0-3)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-data/#__codelineno-0-4)     fn set_data(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-data/#__codelineno-0-5)         &mut self, trident: &mut Trident, _fuzz_accounts: &mut Self::IxAccounts    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-data/#__codelineno-0-6)     ) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-data/#__codelineno-0-7)         self.data.input = trident.gen_range(0..u8::MAX);    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-data/#__codelineno-0-8)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-data/#__codelineno-0-9) }`

# Remaining Accounts - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#remaining-accounts)

Remaining Accounts[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#remaining-accounts "Permanent link")

======================================================================================================================================================

Some Solana instructions require additional accounts beyond their primary accounts. These are called "remaining accounts" and can be configured using the `set_remaining_accounts` function.

Manual Remaining Accounts Setup[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#manual-remaining-accounts-setup "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Remaining accounts are defined as a struct with the `TridentRemainingAccounts` derive macro. The macro expects remaining accounts as an array of `TridentAccount`, allowing you to specify any number of additional accounts.

Remaining Accounts Configuration

Do not forget to add remaining accounts to the `Instruction` struct. Additionally the field has to be named `remaining_accounts`.

Here's an example of how to set up remaining accounts:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-1) pub struct SomeInstruction {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-2)     pub accounts: SomeInstructionAccounts,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-3)     pub data: SomeInstructionData,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-4)     pub remaining_accounts: SomeInstructionRemainingAccounts, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-5) } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-6)[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-7) #[derive(Arbitrary, Debug, Clone, TridentRemainingAccounts)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-8) pub struct SomeInstructionRemainingAccounts {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-9)     pub remaining_accounts: [TridentAccount; 5], [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-10) } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-11)[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-12) impl InstructionSetters for SomeInstruction {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-13)     type IxAccounts = FuzzAccounts; [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-14)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-15)     fn set_remaining_accounts(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-16)         &mut self,        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-17)         trident: &mut Trident,        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-18)         fuzz_accounts: &mut Self::IxAccounts,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-19)     ) { [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-20)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-21)         // Generate random account id        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-22)         let account_id = trident.gen_range(0..3); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-23)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-24)         // Get the account from storage using the generated index        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-25)         let remaining_account1 = fuzz_accounts            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-26)             .owner            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-27)             .get_or_create(account_id, trident, None, None); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-28)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-29)         // Configure the account meta with:        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-30)         // - Account public key        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-31)         // - is_signer flag (false in this example)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-32)         // - is_writable flag (true in this example)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-33)         self.remaining_accounts.remaining_accounts[0].set_account_meta(            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-34)             remaining_account1,            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-35)             false, // is_signer            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-36)             true // is_writable        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-37)         );    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-38)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-39) }`

*   The `set_remaining_accounts` function works similarly to `set_accounts`
*   Each remaining account can be configured with its own signer and writable permissions
*   You can access remaining accounts using array indexing (e.g., `remaining_accounts[0]`)
*   The number of remaining accounts is fixed at compile time by the array size

Back to top

---

# Regression testing - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#regression-testing)

Regression testing[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#regression-testing "Permanent link")

==============================================================================================================================

Regression testing is the process of re-running tests to ensure that previously working functionality still works after code changes.

Trident allows for regression testing by specifying which accounts should be included in the regression test, generating a JSON file format with all monitored state and providing a subcommand to compare two regression test results.

Regression test setup[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#regression-test-setup "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  First, decide which account(s) should be included in the regression test.
    
2.  Add the accounts for tracking, this can be done as shown in the following code snippet. Check the `add_to_regression` method.
    
    `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-1) #[flow_executor] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-2) impl FuzzTest {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-3)     fn new() -> Self {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-4)         Self {            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-5)             trident: Trident::default(),            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-6)             fuzz_accounts: FuzzAccounts::default(),        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-7)         }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-8)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-9)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-10)     #[init]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-11)     fn start(&mut self) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-12)         let mut ix = InitializeFnTransaction::build(&mut self.trident, &mut self.fuzz_accounts); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-13)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-14)         self.trident.execute_transaction(&mut ix, Some("Init")); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-15)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-16)         // Add the account to the regression test        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-17)         self.trident.add_to_regression(            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-18)             &ix.instruction.accounts.hello_world_account.pubkey(),            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-19)             "hello_world_account",        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-20)         );    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-21)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-22)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-23)     #[flow(weight = 5)]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-24)     fn flow1(&mut self) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-25)         // This flow will be executed 60% of the time        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-26)         let mut ix = InitializeFnTransaction::build(&mut self.trident, &mut self.fuzz_accounts);        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-27)         self.trident.execute_transaction(&mut ix, Some("Flow1"));    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-28)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-29)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-30)     #[flow(weight = 5)]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-31)     fn flow2(&mut self) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-32)         // This flow will be executed 40% of the time        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-33)         let mut ix = InitializeFnTransaction::build(&mut self.trident, &mut self.fuzz_accounts);        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-34)         self.trident.execute_transaction(&mut ix, Some("Flow2"));    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-35)     }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-36)     #[flow(weight = 90)]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-37)     fn flow3(&mut self) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-38)         // This flow will be executed 40% of the time        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-39)         let mut ix = InitializeFnTransaction::build(&mut self.trident, &mut self.fuzz_accounts);        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-40)         self.trident.execute_transaction(&mut ix, Some("Flow3"));    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-41)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-42)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-43)     #[end]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-44)     fn cleanup(&mut self) -> Result<(), FuzzingError> {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-45)         // This method will be called after all flows have been executed        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-46)         Ok(())    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-47)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-48) } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-49)[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-50) fn main() {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-51)     FuzzTest::fuzz(1000, 100); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-52) }`
    
3.  Enable the regression test in the [Trident manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-metrics)
     by setting:
    
    `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-1-1) [fuzz.regression] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-1-2) enabled = true`
    
4.  Run the fuzz test to generate the regression test data.
    
5.  Run the same fuzz test with the same MASTER SEED on a different version of the program.
    
6.  Run the following command to compare the generated JSON files.
    

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-2-1) trident compare <path_to_json_file_1> <path_to_json_file_2>`

Back to top
