# Transaction Methods - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/#transaction-methods)

Transaction Methods[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/#transaction-methods "Permanent link")

============================================================================================================================================================

Trident supports customizing transaction behavior with `Transaction Hooks`.

*   [Pre-Transaction Execution](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/pre-post-execution/)
    : Perform custom logic before transaction execution
*   [Post-Transaction Execution](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/pre-post-execution/)
    : Perform custom logic after transaction execution
*   [Transaction Invariants](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/)
    : Validate transaction-specific invariants
*   [Transaction Error Handling](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/error-handler/)
    : Handle transaction errors
*   [Typed Accounts](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/typed-accounts/)
    : Deserialize accounts into typed data to perform differential analysis

Back to top

---

# Transaction Error Hook - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/error-handler/#transaction-error-hook)

Transaction Error Hook[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/error-handler/#transaction-error-hook "Permanent link")

================================================================================================================================================================================

Trident lets you handle errors that occur during transaction execution.

This feature is helpful when you want to investigate errors and verify if the behavior is as expected.

Error Hook Execution Order

The `transaction_error_handler` method is called only when the transaction has `FAILED`.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/error-handler/#__codelineno-0-1) impl TransactionHooks for ExampleTransaction {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/error-handler/#__codelineno-0-2)     type IxAccounts = FuzzAccounts; [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/error-handler/#__codelineno-0-3)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/error-handler/#__codelineno-0-4)     fn transaction_error_handler(&self, e: TransactionError) -> Result<(), TransactionError> {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/error-handler/#__codelineno-0-5)         // Your custom error handling logic goes here    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/error-handler/#__codelineno-0-6)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/error-handler/#__codelineno-0-7) }`

Example[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/error-handler/#example "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The following example demonstrates:

*   Logging the error
*   Returning Ok to suppress the error

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/error-handler/#__codelineno-1-1) impl TransactionHooks for ExampleTransaction {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/error-handler/#__codelineno-1-2)     type IxAccounts = FuzzAccounts; [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/error-handler/#__codelineno-1-3)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/error-handler/#__codelineno-1-4)     fn transaction_error_handler(&self, e: TransactionError) -> Result<(), TransactionError> {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/error-handler/#__codelineno-1-5)         // Example: Log the error and decide whether to propagate it        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/error-handler/#__codelineno-1-6)         eprintln!("Transaction failed with error: {:?}", e); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/error-handler/#__codelineno-1-7)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/error-handler/#__codelineno-1-8)         // Return Ok to suppress the error, or Err to propagate it        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/error-handler/#__codelineno-1-9)         Ok(())    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/error-handler/#__codelineno-1-10)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/error-handler/#__codelineno-1-11) }`

Back to top

# Transaction Invariant Hook - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#transaction-invariant-hook)

Transaction Invariant Hook[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#transaction-invariant-hook "Permanent link")

==========================================================================================================================================================================================

Transaction invariant checks let you compare account states before and after transaction execution (differential analysis), or verify that accounts are in a specific state after the transaction.

This is useful to validate transaction behavior and ensure accounts are not modified in unexpected ways.

Invariant Check Execution Order

The `transaction_invariant_check` method is called only after the transaction is `SUCCESSFULLY` executed.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#__codelineno-0-1) impl TransactionHooks for ExampleTransaction {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#__codelineno-0-2)     fn transaction_invariant_check(&self) -> Result<(), FuzzingError> {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#__codelineno-0-3)         // Your custom differential analysis goes here    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#__codelineno-0-4)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#__codelineno-0-5) }`

Example[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#example "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The following example demonstrates:

*   Obtaining the owner's balance after the transaction, with `.get_snapshot_after()` (post transaction snapshot)
*   Comparing the balance to the expected balance (500 lamports)

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#__codelineno-1-1) impl TransactionHooks for ExampleTransaction {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#__codelineno-1-2)     fn transaction_invariant_check(&self) -> Result<(), FuzzingError> {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#__codelineno-1-3)         // Obtain the owner's balance after the transaction        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#__codelineno-1-4)         let owner_lamports = self            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#__codelineno-1-5)             .instruction            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#__codelineno-1-6)             .accounts            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#__codelineno-1-7)             .owner            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#__codelineno-1-8)             .get_snapshot_after()            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#__codelineno-1-9)             .lamports(); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#__codelineno-1-10)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#__codelineno-1-11)         // Compare the balance and return error if not valid        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#__codelineno-1-12)         if owner_lamports > 500 {            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#__codelineno-1-13)             return Err(FuzzingError::with_message(                [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#__codelineno-1-14)                 "Owner lamports should be less than 500",            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#__codelineno-1-15)             ));        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#__codelineno-1-16)         }        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#__codelineno-1-17)         Ok(())    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#__codelineno-1-18)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/invariant-check/#__codelineno-1-19) }`

# Multi-Instruction Transactions - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/multi-instruction-transactions/#multi-instruction-transactions)

Multi-Instruction Transactions[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/multi-instruction-transactions/#multi-instruction-transactions "Permanent link")

===============================================================================================================================================================================================

Trident supports fuzzing of multiple instructions within one transaction.

By default, separate folders for `instructions` and `transactions` are created. To create multi-instruction transactions, either modify an existing `transaction` in its corresponding `.rs` file or create a new one.

Instruction Resolution Order

In multi-instruction transactions, instruction hooks are executed in the same order as the instructions are defined in the transaction structure.

Example[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/multi-instruction-transactions/#example "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The following example demonstrates:

*   Creating a multi-instruction transaction
*   Adding the transaction to the `FuzzTransactions` enum

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/multi-instruction-transactions/#__codelineno-0-1) // example_transaction.rs [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/multi-instruction-transactions/#__codelineno-0-2) use crate::fuzz_accounts::FuzzAccounts; [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/multi-instruction-transactions/#__codelineno-0-3) use crate::instructions::*; [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/multi-instruction-transactions/#__codelineno-0-4) use trident_fuzz::fuzzing::*; [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/multi-instruction-transactions/#__codelineno-0-5)[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/multi-instruction-transactions/#__codelineno-0-6) /// Customize transaction behavior by adding more instructions. [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/multi-instruction-transactions/#__codelineno-0-7) /// [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/multi-instruction-transactions/#__codelineno-0-8) /// Docs: https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/multi-instruction-transactions/ [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/multi-instruction-transactions/#__codelineno-0-9) #[derive(Debug, TridentTransaction, Default)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/multi-instruction-transactions/#__codelineno-0-10) pub struct ExampleTransaction {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/multi-instruction-transactions/#__codelineno-0-11)     pub instruction1: ExampleInstruction1, // instruction one    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/multi-instruction-transactions/#__codelineno-0-12)     pub instruction2: ExampleInstruction2, // instruction two [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/multi-instruction-transactions/#__codelineno-0-13) } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/multi-instruction-transactions/#__codelineno-0-14) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/multi-instruction-transactions/#__codelineno-0-15)[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/multi-instruction-transactions/#__codelineno-0-16) impl TransactionHooks for ExampleTransaction {}`

Back to top

# Pre and Post Transaction Hooks - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/pre-post-execution/#pre-and-post-transaction-hooks)

Pre and Post Transaction Hooks[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/pre-post-execution/#pre-and-post-transaction-hooks "Permanent link")

=====================================================================================================================================================================================================

Trident lets you perform specific logic before and after transaction execution with pre\_transaction and post\_transaction methods.

These methods accept a `FuzzClient` parameter, which provides methods to interact with the fuzzing environment. See the [FuzzClient](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/fuzz-client-trait/)
 documentation for details.

Post-Transaction Execution Order

The `post_transaction` method is called only after the transaction is `SUCCESSFULLY` executed.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/pre-post-execution/#__codelineno-0-1) impl TransactionHooks for ExampleTransaction {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/pre-post-execution/#__codelineno-0-2)     fn pre_transaction(&self, client: &mut impl FuzzClient) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/pre-post-execution/#__codelineno-0-3)         // Your custom logic goes here    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/pre-post-execution/#__codelineno-0-4)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/pre-post-execution/#__codelineno-0-5) }`

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/pre-post-execution/#__codelineno-1-1) impl TransactionHooks for ExampleTransaction {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/pre-post-execution/#__codelineno-1-2)     fn post_transaction(&self, client: &mut impl FuzzClient) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/pre-post-execution/#__codelineno-1-3)         // Your custom logic goes here    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/pre-post-execution/#__codelineno-1-4)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/pre-post-execution/#__codelineno-1-5) }`

Example[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/pre-post-execution/#example "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The following examples demonstrate:

*   Always forward in time before the transaction
*   Always forward in time after the transaction

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/pre-post-execution/#__codelineno-2-1) impl TransactionHooks for ExampleTransaction {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/pre-post-execution/#__codelineno-2-2)     fn pre_transaction(&self, client: &mut impl FuzzClient) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/pre-post-execution/#__codelineno-2-3)         client.forward_in_time(500);    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/pre-post-execution/#__codelineno-2-4)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/pre-post-execution/#__codelineno-2-5) }`

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/pre-post-execution/#__codelineno-3-1) impl TransactionHooks for ExampleTransaction {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/pre-post-execution/#__codelineno-3-2)     fn post_transaction(&self, client: &mut impl FuzzClient) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/pre-post-execution/#__codelineno-3-3)         client.forward_in_time(500);    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/pre-post-execution/#__codelineno-3-4)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/pre-post-execution/#__codelineno-3-5) }`

Back to top

# Trident API & Macro Reference - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/#trident-api-macro-reference)

Trident API & Macro Reference[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/#trident-api-macro-reference "Permanent link")

========================================================================================================================================

This section contains the API and macro reference for Trident.

Trident[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/#trident "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Trident struct is the main entry point for fuzzing. It provides methods to interact with the fuzzing environment.

*   [Trident](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident/trident/)
    

Trident's Fuzz Client[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/#tridents-fuzz-client "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

FuzzClient represents the API to interact with the client.

*   [FuzzClient](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/fuzz-client-trait/)
    

Trident Accounts attributes[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/#trident-accounts-attributes "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Trident Accounts attributes help to define accounts used in the fuzzing environment.

*   [TridentAccounts](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/)
    

Hooks[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/#hooks "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Transaction Hooks are used to customize what should be done before the transaction is executed, after it is executed and to check if the changes are valid with invariant checks.

*   [TransactionHooks](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/transaction-hooks/)
    

Instruction Hooks are used to customize instruction data and accounts if the Trident Accounts attributes are not enough.

*   [InstructionHooks](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/instruction-hooks/)
    

Trident Macros[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/#trident-macros "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Trident macros are used to define required methods for fuzzing.

*   [TridentTransaction](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-transaction/)
    
*   [TridentInstruction](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/)
    
*   [TridentAccounts](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/)
    
*   [TridentRemainingAccounts](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-remaining-accounts/)
    
*   [TridentFlowExecutor](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/)
    

Trident Types[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/#trident-types "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Trident types represent the types utilized during fuzzing.

*   [FuzzAccounts](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/)
    
*   [TridentAccount](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-account/)
    
*   [TridentPubkey](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-pubkey/)
    
*   [CustomTypes](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/custom-types/)

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# TridentAccount attributes - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#tridentaccount-attributes)

TridentAccount attributes[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#tridentaccount-attributes "Permanent link")

=============================================================================================================================================================================

These attributes are applied to individual account fields using the `#[account(...)]` syntax.

### `account(mut)`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#accountmut "Permanent link")

Marks the account as mutable. This will set the `is_writable` flag to `true` in the generated `AccountMeta`.

`This attribute is optional`

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-0-1) #[derive(TridentAccounts)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-0-2) pub struct ExampleAccounts {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-0-3)     #[account(mut)]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-0-4)     pub mutable_account: TridentAccount, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-0-5) }`

* * *

### `account(signer)`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#accountsigner "Permanent link")

Marks the account as a signer. This will set the `is_signer` flag to `true` in the generated `AccountMeta`.

`This attribute is optional`

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-1-1) #[derive(TridentAccounts)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-1-2) pub struct ExampleAccounts {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-1-3)     #[account(signer)]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-1-4)     pub authority: TridentAccount, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-1-5) }`

* * *

### `account(address)`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#accountaddress "Permanent link")

Sets a fixed address for the account. Useful for program IDs that have known addresses.

`This attribute is optional`

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-2-1) #[derive(TridentAccounts)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-2-2) pub struct ExampleAccounts {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-2-3)     #[account(address = "11111111111111111111111111111111")]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-2-4)     pub system_program: TridentAccount, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-2-5) }`

* * *

### `account(storage::name)`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#accountstoragename "Permanent link")

Specifies which storage to use for the account. This determines where the account address is stored and managed.

`This attribute is optional`

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-3-1) #[derive(TridentAccounts)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-3-2) pub struct ExampleAccounts {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-3-3)     #[account(storage::name = owner)]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-3-4)     pub owner: TridentAccount, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-3-5) }`

* * *

### `account(storage::account_id)`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#accountstorageaccount_id "Permanent link")

Specifies a range of random numbers generated and mapped to address (Pubkey).

A bigger range results in more random account addresses being fuzzed.

`This attribute is optional`

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-4-1) #[derive(TridentAccounts)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-4-2) pub struct ExampleAccounts {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-4-3)     #[account(storage::name = owner)]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-4-4)     pub owner: TridentAccount, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-4-5) }`

* * *

### `account(skip_snapshot)`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#accountskip_snapshot "Permanent link")

Excludes the account from state snapshots. Useful for accounts that don't need to be tracked for state changes.

`This attribute is optional`

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-5-1) #[derive(TridentAccounts)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-5-2) pub struct ExampleAccounts {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-5-3)     #[account(skip_snapshot)]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-5-4)     pub ignored_for_snapshots: TridentAccount, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-5-5) }`

* * *

### `account(seeds)`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#accountseeds "Permanent link")

Defines Program Derived Address (PDA) seeds for the account. The seeds can include references to other accounts in the struct, allowing for dependency-based PDA derivation.

`This attribute is optional but requires the storage attribute`

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-6-1) #[derive(TridentAccounts)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-6-2) pub struct ExampleAccounts {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-6-3)     #[account(storage = pdas, seeds = [b"seed", authority.key().as_ref()])]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-6-4)     pub pda_account: TridentAccount, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-6-5) }`

* * *

### `account(program_id)`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#accountprogram_id "Permanent link")

Specifies the program ID for PDA derivation. If not provided, the program ID of the instruction will be used.

`This attribute is applied at the field level and is used with seeds`

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-7-1) #[derive(TridentAccounts)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-7-2) pub struct ExampleAccounts {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-7-3)     #[account(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-7-4)         storage = custom_pda,        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-7-5)         seeds = [b"seed"],        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-7-6)         program_id = pubkey!("11111111111111111111111111111111")    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-7-7)     )]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-7-8)     pub custom_pda: TridentAccount, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-7-9) }`

* * *

### `account(lamports)`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#accountlamports "Permanent link")

Specifies the lamports for the account. If not provided, the default is 500 \* LAMPORTS\_PER\_SOL.

`This attribute is optional but requires the storage attribute`

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-8-1) #[derive(TridentAccounts)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-8-2) pub struct ExampleAccounts {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-8-3)     #[account(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-8-4)         storage = custom_pda,        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-8-5)         lamports = 5 * LAMPORTS_PER_SOL    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-8-6)     )]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-8-7)     pub wallet: TridentAccount, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-8-8) }`

* * *

### `account(space)`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#accountspace "Permanent link")

Specifies the space for the account. If not provided, the default is 0.

`This attribute is optional but requires the storage attribute and owner attribute`

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-9-1) #[derive(TridentAccounts)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-9-2) pub struct ExampleAccounts {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-9-3)     #[account(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-9-4)         storage = custom_pda,        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-9-5)         space = 8 + 100,        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-9-6)         owner = pubkey!("program id goes here")    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-9-7)     )]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-9-8)     pub custom_pda: TridentAccount, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-9-9) }`

* * *

### `account(owner)`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#accountowner "Permanent link")

Specifies the owner for the account. If not provided, the system program is the default.

`This attribute is optional but requires the storage attribute`

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-10-1) #[derive(TridentAccounts)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-10-2) pub struct ExampleAccounts {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-10-3)     #[account(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-10-4)         storage = custom_pda,        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-10-5)         owner = pubkey!("program id goes here")    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-10-6)     )]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-10-7)     pub custom_pda: TridentAccount, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/#__codelineno-10-8) }`

Back to top

# Instruction Hooks - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/instruction-hooks/#instruction-hooks)

Instruction Hooks[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/instruction-hooks/#instruction-hooks "Permanent link")

==========================================================================================================================================

These methods can be overridden to customize instruction behavior during fuzzing.

### `set_data`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/instruction-hooks/#set_data "Permanent link")

Override this method to customize how instruction data is set during fuzzing.

Override this method to customize how instruction accounts are set during fuzzing.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/instruction-hooks/#__codelineno-1-1) fn set_accounts(&mut self, trident: &mut Trident, fuzz_accounts: &mut Self::IxAccounts) {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/instruction-hooks/#__codelineno-1-2)     // Custom account setting logic [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/instruction-hooks/#__codelineno-1-3) }`

* * *

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/instruction-hooks/#__codelineno-2-1) fn set_remaining_accounts(     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/instruction-hooks/#__codelineno-2-2)     &mut self,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/instruction-hooks/#__codelineno-2-3)     trident: &mut Trident,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/instruction-hooks/#__codelineno-2-4)     fuzz_accounts: &mut Self::IxAccounts, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/instruction-hooks/#__codelineno-2-5) ) {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/instruction-hooks/#__codelineno-2-6)     // Custom remaining accounts setting logic [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/instruction-hooks/#__codelineno-2-7) }`

# Typed Accounts - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/typed-accounts/#typed-accounts)

Typed Accounts[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/typed-accounts/#typed-accounts "Permanent link")

=================================================================================================================================================================

If you need to work with `data accounts` in the `Transaction hooks`, you will first need to deserialize the accounts. For deserialization into known structs, Trident generates `types.rs`, where each struct derives `BorshDeserialize` and `BorshSerialize`.

Serialization/Deserialization

*   If you use custom Serialization/Deserialization, you will need to add it also to the `types.rs` file.

Example[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/typed-accounts/#example "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The following example demonstrates:

*   Obtaining example data account after the transaction, with `.get_snapshot_after()` (post transaction snapshot)
*   `.data_no_discriminator()` ensures that the first 8 bytes (account discriminator) are not included in the deserialization
*   Deserializing the data account into the `ExampleDataAccount` struct

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/typed-accounts/#__codelineno-0-1) // types.rs [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/typed-accounts/#__codelineno-0-2) #[derive(Arbitrary, Debug, BorshDeserialize, BorshSerialize, Clone)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/typed-accounts/#__codelineno-0-3) pub struct ExampleDataAccount {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/typed-accounts/#__codelineno-0-4)     pub data: u64, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/typed-accounts/#__codelineno-0-5) }`

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/typed-accounts/#__codelineno-1-1) // example_transaction.rs [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/typed-accounts/#__codelineno-1-2)[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/typed-accounts/#__codelineno-1-3) #[derive(Arbitrary, Debug, TridentTransaction)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/typed-accounts/#__codelineno-1-4) pub struct ExampleTransaction {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/typed-accounts/#__codelineno-1-5)     pub instruction: ExampleInstruction, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/typed-accounts/#__codelineno-1-6) } # Transaction Hooks - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/transaction-hooks/#transaction-hooks)

Transaction Hooks[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/transaction-hooks/#transaction-hooks "Permanent link")

==========================================================================================================================================

These methods can be overridden to customize transaction behavior during fuzzing.

### `pre_transaction`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/transaction-hooks/#pre_transaction "Permanent link")

Override this method to perform custom actions before the transaction is executed.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/transaction-hooks/#__codelineno-0-1) fn pre_transaction(&self, client: &mut impl FuzzClient) {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/transaction-hooks/#__codelineno-0-2)     // Custom pre-transaction logic    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/transaction-hooks/#__codelineno-0-3)     // e.g., set up accounts, perform checks, etc. [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/transaction-hooks/#__codelineno-0-4) }`

* * *

### `post_transaction`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/transaction-hooks/#post_transaction "Permanent link")

Override this method to perform custom actions after the transaction is executed.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/transaction-hooks/#__codelineno-1-1) fn post_transaction(&self, client: &mut impl FuzzClient) {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/transaction-hooks/#__codelineno-1-2)     // Custom post-transaction logic    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/transaction-hooks/#__codelineno-1-3)     // e.g., cleanup, additional checks, etc. [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/transaction-hooks/#__codelineno-1-4) }`

* * *

### `transaction_invariant_check`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/transaction-hooks/#transaction_invariant_check "Permanent link")

Override this method to perform custom invariant checks on the transaction results.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/transaction-hooks/#__codelineno-2-1) fn transaction_invariant_check(&self) -> Result<(), FuzzingError> {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/transaction-hooks/#__codelineno-2-2)     // Custom invariant checks    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/transaction-hooks/#__codelineno-2-3)     // Return Err(FuzzingError) if invariants are violated    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/transaction-hooks/#__codelineno-2-4)     Ok(()) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/transaction-hooks/#__codelineno-2-5) }`

**Returns:**

*   `Ok(())` if all invariants pass
*   `Err(FuzzingError)` if any invariant is violated

* * *

### `transaction_error_handler`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/transaction-hooks/#transaction_error_handler "Permanent link")

Override this method to handle transaction errors with custom logic.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/transaction-hooks/#__codelineno-3-1) fn transaction_error_handler(&self, error: TransactionError) {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/transaction-hooks/#__codelineno-3-2)     // Custom error handling logic    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/transaction-hooks/#__codelineno-3-3)     // e.g., logging, state cleanup, etc. [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/hooks/transaction-hooks/#__codelineno-3-4) }`

* * *

Back to top

# Trident - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident/trident/#trident)

Trident[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident/trident/#trident "Permanent link")

==============================================================================================================

The `Trident` struct is the main orchestrator for fuzzing operations. It manages the fuzzing client, random number generation, and provides methods for executing transactions and collecting metrics.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident/trident/#__codelineno-0-1) pub struct Trident {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident/trident/#__codelineno-0-2)     client: TridentSVM,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident/trident/#__codelineno-0-3)     fuzzing_data: TridentFuzzingData,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident/trident/#__codelineno-0-4)     rng: TridentRng, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident/trident/#__codelineno-0-5) }`

Core Methods[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident/trident/#core-methods "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### `execute_transaction`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident/trident/#execute_transaction "Permanent link")

Executes a transaction with all transaction hooks enabled, including pre/post transaction hooks and error handling.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident/trident/#__codelineno-1-1) pub fn execute_transaction<T>(     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident/trident/#__codelineno-1-2)     &mut self,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident/trident/#__codelineno-1-3)     transaction: &mut T,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident/trident/#__codelineno-1-4)     transaction_name_override: Option<&str>, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident/trident/#__codelineno-1-5) ) where     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident/trident/#__codelineno-1-6)     T: TransactionHooks + TransactionGetters + TransactionSetters + TransactionPrivateMethods + std::fmt::Debug`

**Parameters:** - `transaction` - The transaction to execute - `transaction_name_override` - Optional custom name for the transaction (used in metrics)

* * *

### `get_client`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident/trident/#get_client "Permanent link")

Returns a mutable reference to the underlying fuzzing client.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident/trident/#__codelineno-2-1) pub fn get_client(&mut self) -> &mut impl FuzzClient`

* * *

### `airdrop`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident/trident/#airdrop "Permanent link")

Adds lamports to the specified account address.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident/trident/#__codelineno-3-1) pub fn airdrop(&mut self, address: &Pubkey, amount: u64)`

**Parameters:** - `address` - The account to receive the lamports - `amount` - The number of lamports to add

* * *

Random Number Generation Methods[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident/trident/#random-number-generation-methods "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# Trident's Fuzz Client - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/fuzz-client-trait/#tridents-fuzz-client)

Trident's Fuzz Client[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/fuzz-client-trait/#tridents-fuzz-client "Permanent link")

===============================================================================================================================================================

Trident's Client (`FuzzClient`) is a wrapper around the [TridentSVM](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-svm/)
 that provides methods to manipulate the execution environment during fuzzing.

This section describes the methods that are available in the `FuzzClient`.

Trident Client Methods[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/fuzz-client-trait/#trident-client-methods "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### `deploy_entrypoint`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/fuzz-client-trait/#deploy_entrypoint "Permanent link")

Syscalls Feature Requirement

This method is only available if the `syscall-v1` or `syscall-v2` features are enabled.

Deploys a program through its entrypoint.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/fuzz-client-trait/#__codelineno-0-1) fn deploy_entrypoint(&mut self, program: TridentEntrypoint)`

* * *

### `deploy_program`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/fuzz-client-trait/#deploy_program "Permanent link")

Deploys a program as binary.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/fuzz-client-trait/#__codelineno-1-1) fn deploy_program(&mut self, program: TridentProgram)`

* * *

### `get_sysvar`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/fuzz-client-trait/#get_sysvar "Permanent link")

Retrieves `Sysvars` like `Rent`, `Clock`, etc.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/fuzz-client-trait/#__codelineno-2-1) fn get_sysvar<T: Sysvar>(&self) -> T`

* * *

### `warp_to_epoch`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/fuzz-client-trait/#warp_to_epoch "Permanent link")

Advances the fuzz test to a specific epoch.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/fuzz-client-trait/#__codelineno-3-1) fn warp_to_epoch(&mut self, warp_epoch: u64)`

* * *

### `warp_to_slot`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/fuzz-client-trait/#warp_to_slot "Permanent link")

Advances the fuzz test to a specific slot.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/fuzz-client-trait/#__codelineno-4-1) fn warp_to_slot(&mut self, warp_slot: u64)`

* * *

### `warp_to_timestamp`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/fuzz-client-trait/#warp_to_timestamp "Permanent link")

Sets the fuzz test to a specific timestamp.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/fuzz-client-trait/#__codelineno-5-1) fn warp_to_timestamp(&mut self, warp_timestamp: i64)`

* * *

### `forward_in_time`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/fuzz-client-trait/#forward_in_time "Permanent link")

Advances the fuzz test by the specified number of seconds.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/fuzz-client-trait/#__codelineno-6-1) fn forward_in_time(&mut self, seconds: i64)`

* * *

### `set_account_custom`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/fuzz-client-trait/#set_account_custom "Permanent link")

Creates or overwrites an account at the specified address, bypassing normal runtime checks.

* * *

### `get_account`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/fuzz-client-trait/#get_account "Permanent link")

# TridentAccounts - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#tridentaccounts)

TridentAccounts[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#tridentaccounts "Permanent link")

==============================================================================================================================================

The `TridentAccounts` macro is used to derive required methods for account structures.

Derived Traits[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#derived-traits "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The macro implements the following trait:

*   `AccountsMethods` - Methods to resolve accounts

Manual Implementation Note

There is no need to manually implement any methods of this trait. The macro handles all implementations automatically based on the account structure and attributes.

Accounts Methods[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#accounts-methods "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Internal Method

These methods are used internally by Trident and it is not expected to use them manually.

### `resolve_accounts`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#resolve_accounts "Permanent link")

Resolves all accounts based on their constraints and dependencies. The macro automatically analyzes seed dependencies and sorts fields in the correct resolution order.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#__codelineno-0-1) fn resolve_accounts(     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#__codelineno-0-2)     &mut self,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#__codelineno-0-3)     trident: &mut Trident,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#__codelineno-0-4)     ix_accounts: &mut Self::IxAccounts,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#__codelineno-0-5)     program_id: Pubkey,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#__codelineno-0-6)     instruction_data: &Self::IxData, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#__codelineno-0-7) )`

* * *

### `to_account_meta`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#to_account_meta "Permanent link")

Converts all accounts to AccountMeta format for Solana instructions.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#__codelineno-1-1) fn to_account_meta(&mut self) -> Vec<AccountMeta>`

* * *

### `capture_before`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#capture_before "Permanent link")

Captures the state of accounts before transaction execution.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#__codelineno-2-1) fn capture_before(&mut self, client: &mut impl FuzzClient)`

* * *

### `capture_after`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#capture_after "Permanent link")

Captures the state of accounts after transaction execution.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#__codelineno-3-1) fn capture_after(&mut self, client: &mut impl FuzzClient)`

* * *

Struct-Level Attributes[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#struct-level-attributes "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

These attributes are applied to the struct definition itself.

### `instruction_data`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#instruction_data "Permanent link")

Specifies the instruction data type that will be used with these accounts.

`This attribute is mandatory and applied at the struct level`

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#__codelineno-4-1) #[derive(TridentAccounts)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#__codelineno-4-2) #[instruction_data(ExampleInstructionData)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#__codelineno-4-3) pub struct ExampleAccounts {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#__codelineno-4-4)     // fields... [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#__codelineno-4-5) }`

* * *

### `storage`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#storage "Permanent link")

Specifies the storage type for accounts, which is used to manage account state during fuzzing.

`This attribute is mandatory and applied at the struct level`

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#__codelineno-5-1) #[derive(TridentAccounts)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#__codelineno-5-2) #[storage(ExampleStorage)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#__codelineno-5-3) pub struct ExampleAccounts {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/#__codelineno-5-4)     // fields... # TridentInstruction - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#tridentinstruction)

TridentInstruction[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#tridentinstruction "Permanent link")

=======================================================================================================================================================

The `TridentInstruction` macro is used to derive required methods for `Instructions`. This procedural macro automatically implements instruction-related functionality for structs that represent instructions.

Required Field Names

The macro parser strictly requires the struct to have an `accounts` field named exactly `accounts`. If a remaining accounts field is used, it must be named exactly `remaining_accounts`.

Derived Traits[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#derived-traits "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The macro implements the following traits:

*   `InstructionGetters` - Methods to retrieve instruction data
*   `InstructionSetters` - Methods to set up instruction state

Manual Implementation Note

There is no need to manually implement the getter, setter, or hook methods. The macro handles these implementations automatically based on the structure of your instruction.

Instruction Getters[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#instruction-getters "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Internal Method

These methods are used internally by Trident and it is not expected to use them manually.

### `get_discriminator`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#get_discriminator "Permanent link")

Returns the instruction discriminator (identifier bytes) that uniquely identifies this instruction of the program.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#__codelineno-0-1) fn get_discriminator(&self) -> Vec<u8>`

* * *

### `get_program_id`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#get_program_id "Permanent link")

Returns the program ID that will process this instruction.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#__codelineno-1-1) fn get_program_id(&self) -> solana_sdk::pubkey::Pubkey`

* * *

### `to_account_metas`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#to_account_metas "Permanent link")

Converts all accounts to AccountMeta format for Solana instructions.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#__codelineno-2-1) fn to_account_metas(&mut self) -> Vec<AccountMeta>`

* * *

Instruction Setters[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#instruction-setters "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Internal Method

These methods are used internally by Trident and it is not expected to use them manually.

### `set_snapshot_before`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#set_snapshot_before "Permanent link")

Captures the state of all accounts before instruction execution.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#__codelineno-3-1) fn set_snapshot_before(&mut self, client: &mut impl FuzzClient)`

* * *

### `set_snapshot_after`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#set_snapshot_after "Permanent link")

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#__codelineno-4-1) fn set_snapshot_after(&mut self, client: &mut impl FuzzClient)`

* * *

### `resolve_accounts`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#resolve_accounts "Permanent link")

Resolves all accounts needed for this instruction.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#__codelineno-5-1) fn resolve_accounts(     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#__codelineno-5-2)     &mut self,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#__codelineno-5-3)     client: &mut impl FuzzClient,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#__codelineno-5-4)     fuzz_accounts: &mut Self::IxAccounts, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#__codelineno-5-5) )`

* * *

Struct-Level Attributes[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#struct-level-attributes "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

These attributes are applied to the struct definition itself.

### `program_id`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#program_id "Permanent link")

Specifies the program ID that will process this instruction. This can be provided as a string literal containing a base58-encoded public key.

`This attribute is mandatory`

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#__codelineno-6-1) #[derive(Arbitrary, Debug, TridentInstruction)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#__codelineno-6-2) #[program_id("KLend2g3cP87fffoy8q1mQqGKjrxjC8boSyAYavgmjD")] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#__codelineno-6-3) pub struct ExampleInstruction {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#__codelineno-6-4)     pub accounts: ExampleInstructionAccounts,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#__codelineno-6-5)     pub data: ExampleInstructionData, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#__codelineno-6-6) }`

* * *

### `discriminator`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/#discriminator "Permanent link")

`This attribute is mandatory`

# TridentRemainingAccounts - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-remaining-accounts/#tridentremainingaccounts)

TridentRemainingAccounts[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-remaining-accounts/#tridentremainingaccounts "Permanent link")

==========================================================================================================================================================================

The `TridentRemainingAccounts` macro is used to derive required methods for `remaining account structures`.

The struct must have exactly one field that holds the remaining accounts and is of type `[TridentAccount; X]`, with `X` being the number of remaining accounts, required.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-1) #[derive(Arbitrary, Debug, TridentRemainingAccounts)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-2) pub struct ExampleRemainingAccounts {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-3)     pub remaining_accounts: [TridentAccount; 2], [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-0-4) }`

Derived Traits[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-remaining-accounts/#derived-traits "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The macro implements the following trait:

*   `RemainingAccountsMethods` - Methods to resolve remaining accounts

Manual Implementation Note

There is no need to manually implement any methods of this trait. The macro handles all implementations automatically based on the account structure and attributes.

Dynamic Sizing Behavior

The macro will only process accounts until it encounters the first unset remaining account. This allows for dynamic sizing of remaining accounts.

Remaining Accounts Methods[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-remaining-accounts/#remaining-accounts-methods "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Internal Method

These methods are used internally by Trident and it is not expected to use them manually.

The macro implements the `RemainingAccountsMethods` trait with the corresponding methods:

### `to_account_meta`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-remaining-accounts/#to_account_meta "Permanent link")

Convert accounts to account metas

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-1-1) fn to_account_meta(&mut self) -> Vec<AccountMeta>;`

* * *

### `capture_before`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-remaining-accounts/#capture_before "Permanent link")

Capture account state before transaction execution

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-2-1) fn capture_before(&mut self, client: &mut impl FuzzClient);`

* * *

### `capture_after`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-remaining-accounts/#capture_after "Permanent link")

Capture account state after transaction execution

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-remaining-accounts/#__codelineno-3-1) fn capture_after(&mut self, client: &mut impl FuzzClient);`

# TridentTransaction - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-transaction/#tridenttransaction)

TridentTransaction[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-transaction/#tridenttransaction "Permanent link")

=======================================================================================================================================================

The `TridentTransaction` macro is used to derive required methods for `Transactions`. This procedural macro automatically implements transaction-related functionality for structs that represent transactions.

Derived Traits[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-transaction/#derived-traits "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The macro implements the following traits:

*   `TransactionGetters` - Methods to retrieve transaction data
*   `TransactionSetters` - Methods to set up transaction state

Manual Implementation Note

There is no need to manually implement the TransactionGetters and TransactionSetters. The macro handles these implementations automatically based on the structure of your transaction.

Transaction Getters[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-transaction/#transaction-getters "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Internal Method

These methods are used internally by Trident and it is not expected to use them manually.

### `get_transaction_name`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-transaction/#get_transaction_name "Permanent link")

Returns the name of the transaction. If a custom name is provided via the `#[name("...")]` attribute, that name will be used; otherwise, the struct name is used.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-transaction/#__codelineno-0-1) fn get_transaction_name(&self) -> String`

* * *

* * *

### `get_instruction_program_ids`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-transaction/#get_instruction_program_ids "Permanent link")

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-transaction/#__codelineno-2-1) fn get_instruction_program_ids(&self) -> Vec<solana_sdk::pubkey::Pubkey>`

* * *

### `get_instruction_data`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-transaction/#get_instruction_data "Permanent link")

Returns the instruction-specific data/parameters for all instructions in the transaction.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-transaction/#__codelineno-3-1) fn get_instruction_data(&mut self, client: &mut impl FuzzClient) -> Vec<Vec<u8>>`

* * *

Transaction Setters[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-transaction/#transaction-setters "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Internal Method

`set_snapshot_before`, `set_snapshot_after` and `set_instructions` methods are used internally by Trident and is not expected to use them manually.

### `build`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-transaction/#build "Permanent link")

Creates a new transaction instance from fuzzer data.

* * *

### `set_snapshot_before`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-transaction/#set_snapshot_before "Permanent link")

Captures the state of all accounts before transaction execution.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-transaction/#__codelineno-6-1) fn set_snapshot_before(&mut self, client: &mut impl FuzzClient)`

* * *

### `set_snapshot_after`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-transaction/#set_snapshot_after "Permanent link")

Captures the state of all accounts after transaction execution.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-transaction/#__codelineno-7-1) fn set_snapshot_after(&mut self, client: &mut impl FuzzClient)`

* * *

### `set_instructions`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-transaction/#set_instructions "Permanent link")

Sets up all instructions for the transaction.

Instruction Setup Order

The order in which the instruction inputs are set is:

1.  `set_data` - Sets up instruction-specific data
2.  `resolve_accounts` - Resolves account addresses
3.  `set_accounts` - Sets up account metadata
4.  `set_remaining_accounts` - Sets up any additional accounts

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-transaction/#__codelineno-8-1) fn set_instructions(     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-transaction/#__codelineno-8-2)     &mut self,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-transaction/#__codelineno-8-3)     trident: &mut Trident,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-transaction/#__codelineno-8-4)     fuzz_accounts: &mut Self::IxAccounts, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-transaction/#__codelineno-8-5) )`

# Custom types - Trident
