Custom types[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/custom-types/#custom-types "Permanent link")

===================================================================================================================================

Trident generates custom types within `types.rs` file. These types are taken from the program's IDL.

You can add your own custom types to the `types.rs` file, or you can modify existing types.

# FuzzAccounts - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#fuzzaccounts)

FuzzAccounts[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#fuzzaccounts "Permanent link")

====================================================================================================================================

`FuzzAccounts` is a struct that contains `all the accounts that can be used in the fuzz test` i.e. `storage` for accounts.

By default, Trident generates the struct based on the program's IDL, i.e. for each account Trident generates a field in the struct.

On demand, you can add your own accounts to the struct, these accounts are meant to be used within the `set_accounts`, `set_remaining_accounts` and potentially within the `set_data` methods, with the corresponding account indexes.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-0-1) pub struct FuzzAccounts {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-0-2)     pub account1: AccountsStorage,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-0-3)     pub account2: AccountsStorage,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-0-4)     pub account3: AccountsStorage,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-0-5)     pub account4: AccountsStorage,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-0-6)     pub account5: AccountsStorage,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-0-7)     pub account6: AccountsStorage,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-0-8)     /// .... [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-0-9) }`

Implemented Methods[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#implemented-methods "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The following section contains the methods that are available for the `AccountsStorage` struct.

### `is_empty`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#is_empty "Permanent link")

Returns true if no accounts are stored.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-1-1) fn is_empty(&self) -> bool`

* * *

### `get_or_create`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#get_or_create "Permanent link")

Gets an existing account or creates a new one with specified metadata.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-2-1) fn get_or_create(     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-2-2)     &mut self,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-2-3)     account_id: AccountId,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-2-4)     trident: &mut Trident,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-2-5)     seeds: Option<PdaSeeds>,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-2-6)     account_metadata: Option<AccountMetadata> [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-2-7) ) -> Pubkey`

* * *

### `get_or_create_token_account`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#get_or_create_token_account "Permanent link")

Token Feature Requirement

This method is only available if the `token` feature is enabled.

Creates or retrieves a token account with specified parameters.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-3-1) fn get_or_create_token_account(     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-3-2)     &mut self,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-3-3)     account_id: AccountId,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-3-4)     trident: &mut Trident,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-3-5)     seeds: Option<PdaSeeds>,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-3-6)     mint: Pubkey,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-3-7)     owner: Pubkey,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-3-8)     amount: u64,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-3-9)     delegate: Option<Pubkey>,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-3-10)     delegated_amount: u64,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-3-11)     close_authority: Option<Pubkey> [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#__codelineno-3-12) ) -> Pubkey`

The `PdaSeeds` and `AccountMetadata` types are optional parameters that can be used to create a Program Derived Address (`Pda`) and pass additional metadata to the account creation process, respectively.

### `PdaSeeds`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/#pdaseeds "Permanent link")

# TridentAccount - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-account/#tridentaccount)

TridentAccount[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-account/#tridentaccount "Permanent link")

==========================================================================================================================================

Trident Account is a wrapper around `AccountMeta`, `SnapshotAccount` and `AccountId`.

`AccountMeta` is a type which is used within `Transaction`, it specifies account address, `isSigner` and `isWritable` flags.

`SnapshotAccount` is Trident's custom type which is used to capture account state before and after the transaction.

`AccountId` is a randomly generated number which is used to identify account within its corresponding `AccountStorage`.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-account/#__codelineno-0-1) #[derive(Debug, Clone)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-account/#__codelineno-0-2) pub struct TridentAccount {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-account/#__codelineno-0-3)     pub account_id: AccountId,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-account/#__codelineno-0-4)     account_meta: Option<AccountMeta>,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-account/#__codelineno-0-5)     snapshot_before: Option<SnapshotAccount>,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-account/#__codelineno-0-6)     snapshot_after: Option<SnapshotAccount>, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-account/#__codelineno-0-7) }`

Implemented Methods[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-account/#implemented-methods "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# Trident examples - Trident

 

Trident examples
================

*   **Hello World!**
    
    * * *
    
    Hello World example with Trident.
    
    [Hello World!](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/tree/develop/examples/hello_world)
    
*   **Cross-Program Invocation**
    
    * * *
    
    Trident supports Cross-Program Invocation, you can fuzz your programs and create NFTs at the same time.
    
    [Simple CPI](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/tree/develop/examples/cpi)
    
    [CPI with Metaplex Metadata Program](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/tree/develop/examples/metaplex)
    
*   **Benchmarking**
    
    * * *
    
    Trident contains benchmarks of [Daedaluzz: A Benchmark Generator for Smart-Contract Fuzzers](https://github.com/Consensys/daedaluzz)
     rewritten in Rust.
    
    [Trident Benchmark](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/tree/develop/examples/trident-benchmark)
    
*   **Fuzzing Pipeline**
    
    * * *
    
    Trident provides a fuzzing pipeline that can be used to fuzz your programs.
    
    [Fuzzing pipeline](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/blob/master/.github/workflows/fuzz.yml)
    

Back to top

---

# TridentPubkey - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-pubkey/#tridentpubkey)

TridentPubkey[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-pubkey/#tridentpubkey "Permanent link")

=======================================================================================================================================

`TridentPubkey` is a wrapper around `Pubkey` and `AccountId`.

`Pubkey` is a type from the `solana-sdk` crate that corresponds to a Solana account address.

`AccountId` is a randomly generated number which is used to identify account within its corresponding `AccountStorage`.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-pubkey/#__codelineno-0-1) #[derive(Debug, Clone)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-pubkey/#__codelineno-0-2) pub struct TridentPubkey {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-pubkey/#__codelineno-0-3)     pub account_id: AccountId,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-pubkey/#__codelineno-0-4)     pub pubkey: Pubkey, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-pubkey/#__codelineno-0-5) }`

Implemented Methods[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-pubkey/#implemented-methods "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The following section contains the methods that are available for the `TridentPubkey` struct.

### `set_pubkey`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-pubkey/#set_pubkey "Permanent link")

Sets the public key for this instance.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-pubkey/#__codelineno-1-1) fn set_pubkey(&mut self, pubkey: Pubkey)`

* * *

### `get_pubkey`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-pubkey/#get_pubkey "Permanent link")

Returns the stored public key.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-pubkey/#__codelineno-2-1) fn get_pubkey(&self) -> Pubkey`

* * *

Implemented Traits[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-pubkey/#implemented-traits "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   `From<AccountId>` - Creates a new instance with the given account\_id and default pubkey
*   `BorshSerialize` - Serializes only the pubkey field
*   `BorshDeserialize` - Deserializes only the pubkey field, sets default account\_id
*   `Serialize` (serde) - Serializes only the pubkey field
*   `Deserialize` (serde) - Deserializes only the pubkey field, sets default account\_id
*   `Arbitrary` - Generates random account\_id and default pubkey

Back to top

---

# TridentSVM - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-svm/#tridentsvm)

TridentSVM[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-svm/#tridentsvm "Permanent link")

==============================================================================================

TridentSVM is a fast execution and accounts storage environment which is utilized within the Trident.

Github repository: [Trident SVM](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident-svm)

TridentSVM uses [Anza's SVM API](https://www.anza.xyz/blog/anzas-new-svm-api)

# Flow Executor - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#flow-executor)

Flow Executor[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#flow-executor "Permanent link")

===============================================================================================================================================

The Flow Executor macros are a set of attribute macros used to define and control execution flows. These macros help organize and manage the execution of complex test scenarios.

Available Macros[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#available-macros "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Flow Executor functionality consists of four main attribute macros:

1.  `#[flow_executor]` - Implements the flow executor for a struct
2.  `#[flow]` - Marks a method as part of the execution flow
3.  `#[init]` - Marks a method to run once at the beginning of each iteration before all flow methods
4.  `#[end]` - Marks a method to run once at the end of each iteration after all flow methods

Usage[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#usage "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-1) #[derive(FuzzTestMethods)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-2) struct FuzzTest {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-3)     /// for fuzzing    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-4)     trident: Trident,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-5)     /// for storing fuzzing accounts    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-6)     fuzz_accounts: FuzzAccounts, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-7) } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-8)[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-9) #[flow_executor] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-10) impl FuzzTest {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-11)     fn new() -> Self {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-12)         Self {            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-13)             trident: Trident::default(),            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-14)             fuzz_accounts: FuzzAccounts::default(),        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-15)         }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-16)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-17)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-18)     #[init]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-19)     fn start(&mut self) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-20)         // perform any initialization here, this method will be executed        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-21)         // at start of each iteration    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-22)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-23)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-24)     #[flow]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-25)     fn flow1(&mut self) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-26)         // perform logic which is meant to be fuzzed        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-27)         // this flow is selected randomly from other flows    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-28)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-29)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-30)     #[flow]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-31)     fn flow2(&mut self) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-32)         // perform logic which is meant to be fuzzed        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-33)         // this flow is selected randomly from other flows    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-34)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-35)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-36)     #[end]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-37)     fn end(&mut self) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-38)         // perform any cleanup here, this method will be executed        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-39)         // at the end of each iteration    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-40)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-0-41) }`

Implementation-Level attributes[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#implementation-level-attributes "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### `#[flow_executor]`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#flow_executor "Permanent link")

The `flow_executor` attribute macro is applied to an `impl` block and implements the flow executor functionality for the struct.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-1-1) #[flow_executor] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-1-2) impl FuzzTest {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-1-3)     // Flow methods... [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-1-4) }`

* * *

Method-Level attributes[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#method-level-attributes "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### `#[init]`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#init "Permanent link")

The `init` attribute macro marks a method as the initialization method for the flows. This method is executed at the beginning of each iteration before all flow methods.

Initialization Method

It is possible to define only one initialization method.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-2-1) #[init] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-2-2) fn initialize(&mut self) {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-2-3)     // Initialization logic    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-2-4)     // Perform initialization Transaction here [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-2-5) }`

* * *

### `#[flow]`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#flow "Permanent link")

The `flow` attribute macro marks a method as part of the execution flow.

Flow Methods

It is possible to define multiple flow methods.

If multiple flows are defined, the fuzzer will pick randomly and generate a sequence of random flows to execute.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-3-1) #[flow] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-3-2) fn step_one(&mut self) {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-3-3)     // Flow step implementation [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-3-4) }`

* * *

### `#[end]`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#end "Permanent link")

The `end` attribute macro marks a method to run once at the end of each iteration after all flow methods.

Cleanup Method

It is possible to define only one end method.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-4-1) #[end] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-4-2) fn cleanup(&mut self) {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-4-3)     // Cleanup logic [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-4-4) }`

Generated Methods[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#generated-methods "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### `fuzz`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#fuzz "Permanent link")

Runs the fuzzing process with multiple concurrent fuzzing threads.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/#__codelineno-5-1) fn fuzz(iterations: u64, flow_calls_per_iteration: u64)`

*   `iterations` - Number of iterations to run
*   `flow_calls_per_iteration` - Number of flow methods called in each iteration (e.g. if the `flow_calls_per_iteration` is 100, the fuzzer will pick a random sequence of 100 flow methods to execute in each iteration)

Back to top

# Trident Manifest - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#trident-manifest)

Trident Manifest[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#trident-manifest "Permanent link")

===============================================================================================================

Trident supports its own Trident Manifest, called `Trident.toml`. This section describes all possible configuration fields.

Fuzzing Metrics[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-metrics "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-0-1) [fuzz.metrics] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-0-2) enabled = true [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-0-3) dashboard = false [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-0-4) json = false`

*   `enabled` - Trident will show and save statistics after the fuzzing session.
*   `dashboard` - Trident will save a HTML dashboard after the fuzzing session.
*   `json` - Trident will save a JSON file after the fuzzing session.

* * *

Regression testing[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#regression-testing "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-1-1) [fuzz.regression] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-1-2) enabled = true`

*   `enabled` - Trident will save a JSON file with all monitored states after the fuzzing session.

Regression testing

*   Keep in mind that the feature hashes contents of accounts, if the contents are dependant for example on time, the final hash might not be the same as the one from the first fuzzing session.

* * *

Fuzzing Coverage[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-coverage "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-1) [fuzz.coverage] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-2) enable = true               # default: false [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-3) server_port = 58432         # default: 58432 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-4) loopcount = 5               # default: 0 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-5) format = "json"             # default: "json" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-6) attach_extension = true     # default: false`

The coverage configuration enables code coverage analysis during fuzzing sessions, providing insights into which parts of your program are being tested.

*   `enable` - When set to `true`, Trident collects code coverage data throughout the fuzzing session and generates a comprehensive report upon completion.
*   `server_port` - Specifies the HTTP server port used for communication between Trident and the [Solana VS Code extension](https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=AckeeBlockchain.solana)
    .
*   `loopcount` - Defines the number of execution flows processed before generating an intermediate coverage data file. Lower values provide more frequent coverage updates at the cost of performance. When set to `0`, coverage files are only generated at the end of the fuzzing session.
*   `format` - Determines the output format for coverage reports. Trident supports both `json` and `html` formats.
*   `attach_extension` - Enables real-time coverage visualization in VS Code when the extension is active. This feature requires `loopcount` to be greater than `0` and `format` to be set to `json`.

Warning

Coverage is only gathered for the programs deployed through an entrypoint!

Entrypoint deployment guide

1.  Comment out the program in `Trident.toml`
    
     `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-3-1)  # [[fuzz.programs]] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-3-2)  # address = "example_address" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-3-3)  # program = "../target/deploy/example_program.so"`
    
2.  Add the program dependency to `Cargo.toml`
    
     `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-4-1)  [dependencies.example_program] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-4-2)  path = "../programs/example_program"`
    
3.  Add `syscall-v1` or `syscall-v2` feature depending on the version of `solana-program`. Programs written for `solana-program` v1.x should use `syscall-v1`, programs written for `solana-program` v2.x should use `syscall-v2` feature.
    
     `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-5-1)  [dependencies.trident-fuzz] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-5-2)  features = ["syscall-v2"]`
    
4.  Import the programs entrypoint in `test_fuzz.rs`
    
     `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-6-1)  use example_program::entry as example_entrypoint;`
    
5.  Deploy the entrypoint in `test_fuzz.rs`
    
     `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-1)  impl FuzzTest {   [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-2)    fn new() -> Self {       [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-3)        let mut trident = Trident::default(); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-4)       [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-5)        // Deploy through the entrypoint       [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-6)        let program = TridentEntrypoint::new(example_program::ID, None, processor!(example_entrypoint));       [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-7)        trident.get_client().deploy_entrypoint(program); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-8)       [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-9)        Self {           [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-10)            trident,           [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-11)            fuzz_accounts: FuzzAccounts::default(),       [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-12)        }   [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-13)    }   [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-14)    ...`

* * *

Programs[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#programs "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Use dumped program from desired cluster, during fuzzing.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-8-1) [[fuzz.programs]] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-8-2) address = "metaqbxxUerdq28cj1RbAWkYQm3ybzjb6a8bt518x1s" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-8-3) upgrade_authority = "account address goes here" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-8-4) program = "metaplex-program/metaplex-token-metadata.so"`

* * *

Accounts[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#accounts "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Use dumped accounts from desired cluster, during fuzzing.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-9-1) [[fuzz.accounts]] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-9-2) address = "6YG3J7PaxyMnnbU67ifyrgF3BzNzc7cD8hPkqK6ATweE" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-9-3) filename = "tests/accounts/core_bridge_mainnet/guardian_set_5_mock.json"`

* * *

Back to top

---

# Code Coverage - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/code-coverage/#code-coverage)

Code Coverage[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/code-coverage/#code-coverage "Permanent link")

=======================================================================================================================

Trident's code coverage feature analyzes which parts of your Solana program are tested during fuzzing sessions, helping you identify untested code paths and improve test effectiveness.

 Your browser does not support the video tag.

Key features:

*   **Real-time Analysis**: Monitor coverage as fuzzing progresses
*   **Multiple Formats**: Generate reports in JSON and HTML formats
*   **VS Code Integration**: Visualize coverage directly in your IDE using [Solana VS Code extension](https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=AckeeBlockchain.solana)
    
*   **Detailed Reporting**: Get insights into line coverage, branch coverage, and execution paths

Gathering Coverage Data[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/code-coverage/#gathering-coverage-data "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Enable coverage in the [Trident manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-coverage)
    
2.  Deploy your program through the [entrypoint](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#entrypoint-deployment)
    
3.  Run the fuzz test

Viewing Coverage Reports[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/code-coverage/#viewing-coverage-reports "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You have two options for displaying coverage data: generate an HTML report for browser viewing, or generate a JSON report for VS Code integration.

### Live Coverage Updates[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/code-coverage/#live-coverage-updates "Permanent link")

For real-time coverage monitoring during fuzzing:

1.  Set `format = "json"` in the [Trident manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-coverage)
    
2.  Set `loopcount` to a value other than `0` e.g., `5` for frequent updates, for more info check out [Trident manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#entrypoint-deployment)
    
3.  Install the [Solana VS Code extension](https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=AckeeBlockchain.solana)
    
4.  Choose one of these options:
    *   **Automatic**: Set `attach_extension = true` in the [Trident manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-coverage)
         to automatically show live updates while the fuzz test is running
    *   **Manual**: Use the command `Solana: Show Code Coverage` and select the "Attach to active fuzzing session" option

### Post-Session Coverage Analysis[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/code-coverage/#post-session-coverage-analysis "Permanent link")

1.  Set `format = "json"` in the [Trident manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-coverage)
     before running the fuzz test
2.  Run the fuzz test
3.  Install the [Solana VS Code extension](https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=AckeeBlockchain.solana)
    
4.  Run the VS Code command `Solana: Show Code Coverage` and select the "Load generated JSON report" option

### HTML Report[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/code-coverage/#html-report "Permanent link")

1.  Set `format = "html"` in the [Trident manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-coverage)
     before running the fuzz test
2.  Run the fuzz test
3.  After the fuzz test finishes, the HTML report will be stored in the `<fuzz-test-name>-coverage-report` folder
4.  Open the HTML report in your browser

Back to top

---

# Dashboard - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#dashboard)

Dashboard[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#dashboard "Permanent link")

===========================================================================================================

The Trident Dashboard provides a web-based interface for visualizing fuzzing session results through interactive charts and comprehensive statistics.

 Your browser does not support the video tag.

Features:

*   **Session Statistics**: View execution counts, success rates, and performance metrics
*   **Interactive Charts**: Explore results through dynamic visualizations
*   **Browser Access**: Open in any web browser without additional software
*   **Comprehensive Analysis**: Insights into instruction coverage and account interactions

Viewing the Dashboard[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#viewing-the-dashboard "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Open another terminal window and execute `trident server` from the fuzz-tests directory.
    
2.  Open your browser and navigate to the provided URL (typically `http://localhost:8080`).
    
3.  Enable the dashboard in the [Trident manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-metrics)
     by setting `dashboard = true`.
    
    `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-0-1) [fuzz.metrics] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-0-2) enabled = true [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-0-3) dashboard = true`
    
4.  Run the fuzz test to generate dashboard data.
    

Monitoring custom fuzzing metrics[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#monitoring-custom-fuzzing-metrics "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Trident allows you to monitor custom fuzzing metrics. If your program expects integer instruction inputs, it is possible to collect data on the randomly generated values and display them in the dashboard.

To do this, you need to add `trident.add_histogram_metric` to the `#[init]`, `#[flow]` or `#[end]` functions. The following code snippet shows how the `InitializeFnTransaction` instruction input is monitored; the statistics will be displayed in the dashboard.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-1) #[flow_executor] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-2) impl FuzzTest {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-3)     fn new() -> Self {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-4)         Self {            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-5)             trident: Trident::default(),            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-6)             fuzz_accounts: FuzzAccounts::default(),        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-7)         }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-8)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-9)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-10)     #[init]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-11)     fn start(&mut self) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-12)         let mut ix = InitializeFnTransaction::build(&mut self.trident, &mut self.fuzz_accounts); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-13)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-14)         self.trident.execute_transaction(&mut ix, Some("Init"));    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-15)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-16)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-17)     #[flow(weight = 5)]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-18)     fn flow1(&mut self) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-19)         let mut ix = InitializeFnTransaction::build(&mut self.trident, &mut self.fuzz_accounts);        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-20)         self.trident.execute_transaction(&mut ix, Some("Flow1")); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-21)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-22)         // Add the histogram metric to the dashboard        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-23)         self.trident            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-24)             .add_histogram_metric("flow1_metric", ix.instruction.data.input as f64);    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-25)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-26)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-27)     #[flow(weight = 5)]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-28)     fn flow2(&mut self) {      [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-29)       //....    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-30)     }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-31)     #[flow(weight = 90)]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-32)     fn flow3(&mut self) {      [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-33)       //....    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-34)     }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-35)     #[end]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-36)     fn cleanup(&mut self) -> Result<(), FuzzingError> {      [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-37)       //....    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-38)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/latest/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-39) }`

# Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/#trident)

Trident[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/#trident "Permanent link")

===========================================================================

![Trident](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/images/trident-logo-smaller.png)

Rust-based Fuzzing framework for Solana programs to help you ship secure code.

*   **Getting Started**
    
    * * *
    
    Install the Trident Fuzz Testing Framework
    
    [Getting started](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/getting-started/getting-started/)
    
*   **Start Fuzzing**
    
    * * *
    
    Focus on security and start fuzzing immediatelly
    
    [Start Fuzzing](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/fuzzing/first-steps/fuzz-test-initialization/)
    
*   **Check the GitHub for unreleased features**
    
    * * *
    
    Check our GitHub repository to see the unreleased features
    
    [Trident Repository](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/tree/develop)
    
*   **Trident by Examples**
    
    * * *
    
    Try the Fuzzing Examples
    
    [Trident Examples](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/fuzzing/extra/examples/)
    

What is Fuzzing ?[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/#what-is-fuzzing "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

_"Fuzz testing is an automated technique that provides generated random, invalid, or unexpected input data to your program. This helps discover unknown bugs and vulnerabilities, potentially preventing zero-day exploits."_

Trident equips developers with tools to efficiently develop fuzz tests for Anchor-based programs. It streamlines the fuzz testing process through automation and comprehensive support

*   **Trident Workflow**
    
    * * *
    
    *   **Automatically parses Anchor-based programs** to generate necessary implementations for deserializing instruction accounts.
    *   **Generates templates** for developers to customize according to the specific needs of their fuzz test scenarios.
    *   **Offers derive macros** to effortlessly implement required traits, reducing manual coding efforts.
    *   **Includes a bank client** and helper functions for simplified account management during testing.
    *   **Provides a Command-Line Interface** (CLI) for executing and debugging fuzz tests with ease.
*   **Trident Capabilities**
    
    * * *
    
    *   **Execution Order of Instructions**: Test different sequences and their effects on the program to uncover sequence-related vulnerabilities.
    *   **Instruction Parameters**: Identify how variations in inputs influence program behavior, testing for robustness against a wide range of data.
    *   **Instruction Accounts**: Explore the impact of different account states on the software's functionality, ensuring comprehensive account testing.
    *   **Comprehensive Testing**: Conduct thorough and effective fuzz testing by combining any of the above aspects.

Back to top

---

# Trident Documentation - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/#trident-documentation)

Trident Documentation[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/#trident-documentation "Permanent link")

========================================================================================================

Fuzzing is a technique to test the robustness of a program by providing it with random inputs.

Trident is a Manually Guided Fuzzing framework for Solana. It lets you to execute instructions of your Solana programs with random data and observe the changes in the state of the program.

Getting started[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/#getting-started "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   [Installation](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/installation/)
     - Install the Trident Fuzz Testing Framework
*   [Start Fuzzing](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/)
     - Focus on security and start fuzzing immediately

Advanced fuzzing customization[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/#advanced-fuzzing-customization "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Explore the various features Trident provides.

*   [Transaction Hooks](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/transaction-hooks/)
     - Create and manipulate transactions with different methods
*   [Multi-Instruction Transactions](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/trident-transactions/multi-instruction-transactions/)
     - Compose fuzzed transactions with multiple instructions
*   [Trident Manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/)
     - Customize your fuzz tests with different configurations
*   [Code Coverage](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/code-coverage/)
     - Track and display fuzz test code coverage
*   [Dashboard](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/)
     - A web-based interface for visualizing fuzzing session results
*   [Regression Testing](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/)
     - Track and compare fuzzing session results

# Trident - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/#trident)

Trident[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/#trident "Permanent link")

===========================================================================

Trident is a Rust-based framework to fuzz and integration test Solana programs to help you ship secure code.

Features[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/#features "Permanent link")

=============================================================================

*   **Automated Test Generation**: Simplifies the testing process by automatically creating templates for fuzz and integration tests for programs written using the Anchor Framework.
    
*   **Dynamic Data Generation**: Increases test coverage with random instruction data and pseudo-random accounts for unpredictable fuzz test scenarios.
    
*   **Custom Instruction Sequences**: Provides the flexibility to design specific sequences of instructions to meet particular testing needs or to focus on particular aspects of program behavior during fuzz testing. Invariant Checks: Allows for custom invariants checks to spot vulnerabilities and unwanted behaviors.
    

Back to top

---

# Trident API & Macro Reference - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-api-macro/#trident-api-macro-reference)

Trident API & Macro Reference[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-api-macro/#trident-api-macro-reference "Permanent link")

========================================================================================================================================

This section contains the API and macro reference for Trident.

Trident[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-api-macro/#trident "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Trident struct is the main entry point for fuzzing. It provides methods to interact with the fuzzing environment.

*   [Trident](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-api-macro/trident/trident/)
    

Trident's Fuzz Client[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-api-macro/#tridents-fuzz-client "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

FuzzClient represents the API to interact with the client.

*   [FuzzClient](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/fuzz-client-trait/)
    

Trident Accounts attributes[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-api-macro/#trident-accounts-attributes "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Trident Accounts attributes help to define accounts used in the fuzzing environment.

*   [TridentAccounts](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/)
    

Hooks[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-api-macro/#hooks "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Transaction Hooks are used to customize what should be done before the transaction is executed, after it is executed and to check if the changes are valid with invariant checks.

*   [TransactionHooks](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-api-macro/hooks/transaction-hooks/)
    

Instruction Hooks are used to customize instruction data and accounts if the Trident Accounts attributes are not enough.

*   [InstructionHooks](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-api-macro/hooks/instruction-hooks/)
    

Trident Macros[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-api-macro/#trident-macros "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Trident macros are used to define required methods for fuzzing.

*   [TridentTransaction](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-transaction/)
    
*   [TridentInstruction](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/)
    
*   [TridentAccounts](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/)
    
*   [TridentRemainingAccounts](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-remaining-accounts/)
    
*   [TridentFlowExecutor](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/)
    

Trident Types[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-api-macro/#trident-types "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Trident types represent the types utilized during fuzzing.

*   [FuzzAccounts](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-api-macro/trident-types/fuzz-accounts/)
    
*   [TridentAccount](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-account/)
    
*   [TridentPubkey](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-api-macro/trident-types/trident-pubkey/)
    
*   [CustomTypes](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-api-macro/trident-types/custom-types/)
    

Back to top

# TridentSVM - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-svm/#tridentsvm)

TridentSVM[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-svm/#tridentsvm "Permanent link")

==============================================================================================

TridentSVM is a fast execution and accounts storage environment which is utilized within the Trident.

Github repository: [Trident SVM](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident-svm)

TridentSVM uses [Anza's SVM API](https://www.anza.xyz/blog/anzas-new-svm-api)

# Trident examples - Trident

 

Trident examples
================

*   **Hello World!**
    
    * * *
    
    Hello World example with Trident.
    
    [Hello World!](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/tree/develop/examples/hello_world)
    
*   **Cross-Program Invocation**
    
    * * *
    
    Trident supports Cross-Program Invocation, you can fuzz your programs and create NFTs at the same time.
    
    [Simple CPI](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/tree/develop/examples/cpi)
    
    [CPI with Metaplex Metadata Program](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/tree/develop/examples/metaplex)
    
*   **Benchmarking**
    
    * * *
    
    Trident contains benchmarks of [Daedaluzz: A Benchmark Generator for Smart-Contract Fuzzers](https://github.com/Consensys/daedaluzz)
     rewritten in Rust.
    
    [Trident Benchmark](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/tree/develop/examples/trident-benchmark)
    
*   **Fuzzing Pipeline**
    
    * * *
    
    Trident provides a fuzzing pipeline that can be used to fuzz your programs.
    
    [Fuzzing pipeline](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/blob/master/.github/workflows/fuzz.yml)

# Start Fuzzing - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/#start-fuzzing)

Start Fuzzing[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/#start-fuzzing "Permanent link")

======================================================================================================

To start writing fuzz tests, you need to initialize Trident in your Anchor-based workspace.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-0-1) trident init`

If you have already initialized Trident, you can add a new fuzz test using:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-1-1) trident fuzz add`

Trident creates a new fuzz test template in the `trident-tests` directory, with the following structure:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-1) project-root [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-2) ├── trident-tests [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-3) │   ├── fuzz_0 # particular fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-4) │   │   ├── instructions # instructions folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-5) │   │   ├── transactions # transactions folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-6) │   │   ├── test_fuzz.rs # the binary target of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-7) │   │   ├── types.rs # the types of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-8) │   │   └── fuzz_instructions.rs # the definition of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-9) │   ├── fuzz_1 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-10) │   ├── fuzz_X # possible multiple fuzz tests [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-11) │   ├── fuzzing # compilations and crashes folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-12) │   ├── Cargo.toml [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-13) │   └── Trident.toml [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-14) └── ...`

`Instructions` folder contains the `instructions` that can be used in the fuzz test.

`Transactions` folder contains the `transactions` that will be used during the fuzzing, each transaction can contain `one` or `multiple instructions`, based on the developer's choice. By default there is only one instruction in each transaction.

Back to top

---

     - Visualize fuzzing metrics in a dashboard

# Trident Manifest - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#trident-manifest)

Trident Manifest[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#trident-manifest "Permanent link")

===============================================================================================================

Trident supports its own Trident Manifest, called `Trident.toml`. This section describes all possible configuration fields.

Fuzzing Metrics[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-metrics "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-0-1) [fuzz.metrics] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-0-2) enabled = true [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-0-3) dashboard = false [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-0-4) json = false`

*   `enabled` - Trident will show and save statistics after the fuzzing session.
*   `dashboard` - Trident will save a HTML dashboard after the fuzzing session.
*   `json` - Trident will save a JSON file after the fuzzing session.

* * *

Regression testing[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#regression-testing "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-1-1) [fuzz.regression] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-1-2) enabled = true`

*   `enabled` - Trident will save a JSON file with all monitored states after the fuzzing session.

Regression testing

*   Keep in mind that the feature hashes contents of accounts, if the contents are dependant for example on time, the final hash might not be the same as the one from the first fuzzing session.

* * *

Fuzzing Coverage[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-coverage "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-1) [fuzz.coverage] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-2) enable = true               # default: false [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-3) server_port = 58432         # default: 58432 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-4) loopcount = 5               # default: 0 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-5) format = "json"             # default: "json" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-6) attach_extension = true     # default: false`

The coverage configuration enables code coverage analysis during fuzzing sessions, providing insights into which parts of your program are being tested.

*   `enable` - When set to `true`, Trident collects code coverage data throughout the fuzzing session and generates a comprehensive report upon completion.
*   `server_port` - Specifies the HTTP server port used for communication between Trident and the [Solana VS Code extension](https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=AckeeBlockchain.solana)
    .
*   `loopcount` - Defines the number of execution flows processed before generating an intermediate coverage data file. Lower values provide more frequent coverage updates at the cost of performance. When set to `0`, coverage files are only generated at the end of the fuzzing session.
*   `format` - Determines the output format for coverage reports. Trident supports both `json` and `html` formats.
*   `attach_extension` - Enables real-time coverage visualization in VS Code when the extension is active. This feature requires `loopcount` to be greater than `0` and `format` to be set to `json`.

Warning

Coverage is only gathered for the programs deployed through an entrypoint!

Entrypoint deployment guide

1.  Comment out the program in `Trident.toml`
    
     `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-3-1)  # [[fuzz.programs]] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-3-2)  # address = "example_address" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-3-3)  # program = "../target/deploy/example_program.so"`
    
2.  Add the program dependency to `Cargo.toml`
    
     `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-4-1)  [dependencies.example_program] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-4-2)  path = "../programs/example_program"`
    
3.  Add `syscall-v1` or `syscall-v2` feature depending on the version of `solana-program`. Programs written for `solana-program` v1.x should use `syscall-v1`, programs written for `solana-program` v2.x should use `syscall-v2` feature.
    
     `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-5-1)  [dependencies.trident-fuzz] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-5-2)  features = ["syscall-v2"]`
    
4.  Import the programs entrypoint in `test_fuzz.rs`
    
     `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-6-1)  use example_program::entry as example_entrypoint;`
    
5.  Deploy the entrypoint in `test_fuzz.rs`
    
     `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-1)  impl FuzzTest {   [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-2)    fn new() -> Self {       [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-3)        let mut trident = Trident::default(); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-4)       [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-5)        // Deploy through the entrypoint       [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-6)        let program = TridentEntrypoint::new(example_program::ID, None, processor!(example_entrypoint));       [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-7)        trident.get_client().deploy_entrypoint(program); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-8)       [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-9)        Self {           [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-10)            trident,           [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-11)            fuzz_accounts: FuzzAccounts::default(),       [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-12)        }   [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-13)    }   [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-14)    ...`

* * *

Programs[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#programs "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Use dumped program from desired cluster, during fuzzing.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-8-1) [[fuzz.programs]] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-8-2) address = "metaqbxxUerdq28cj1RbAWkYQm3ybzjb6a8bt518x1s" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-8-3) upgrade_authority = "account address goes here" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-8-4) program = "metaplex-program/metaplex-token-metadata.so"`

* * *

Accounts[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#accounts "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Use dumped accounts from desired cluster, during fuzzing.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-9-1) [[fuzz.accounts]] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-9-2) address = "6YG3J7PaxyMnnbU67ifyrgF3BzNzc7cD8hPkqK6ATweE" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-9-3) filename = "tests/accounts/core_bridge_mainnet/guardian_set_5_mock.json"`

* * *

Back to top

# Installation - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/installation/#installation)

Installation[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/installation/#installation "Permanent link")

==========================================================================================================

Trident requires the following prerequisites:

Prerequisites

Before proceeding, ensure you have installed:

*   [Rust](https://www.rust-lang.org/tools/install)
     (stable version)
*   [Solana CLI](https://solana.com/docs/intro/installation)
    
*   [Anchor](https://www.anchor-lang.com/docs/installation)
    

Check out [supported versions](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/installation/#supported-versions)
 for version compatibility.

Install Trident[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/installation/#install-trident "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/installation/#__codelineno-0-1) cargo install trident-cli`

You can also use the `version` flag to install a specific version:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/installation/#__codelineno-1-1) cargo install trident-cli --version x.y.z`

Install cargo-llvm-cov[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/installation/#install-cargo-llvm-cov "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To enable code coverage tracking during fuzzing, install [cargo-llvm-cov](https://github.com/taiki-e/cargo-llvm-cov)
:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/installation/#__codelineno-2-1) cargo +stable install cargo-llvm-cov --locked`

Supported versions[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/installation/#supported-versions "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Version Table Legend

*   \= Develop branch
*   \= Released version
*   `-` = Not required/supported

| **Version Type** | **Anchor** | **Solana** | **Rust** | **Honggfuzz** | **AFL** |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Development | `>=0.29.0` | `>=1.17.3` | `1.86` | `-` | `-` |
| **Current (0.11.x)** | `>=0.29.0` | `>=1.17.3` | `1.86` | `-` | `-` |
| **0.10.x** | `>=0.29.0 < 0.31.0` | `>=1.17.3 < 2.1` | `nightly` | `0.5.56` | `0.15.11` |
| **0.9.x** | `>=0.29.0 < 0.31.0` | `>=1.17.3 < 2.1` | `nightly` | `0.5.56` | `0.15.11` |
| **0.8.x** | `0.30.1` | `^1.17.4` | `nightly` | `0.5.56` | `-` |
| **0.7.x** | `>=0.29.*` | `^1.17.4` | `nightly` | `0.5.56` | `-` |
| **0.6.x** | `>=0.29.*` | `^1.17` | `nightly` | `0.5.55` | `-` |
| **0.5.x** | `~0.28.*` | `=1.16.6` | `-` | `-` | `-` |
| **0.4.x** | `~0.27.*` | `>=1.15` | `-` | `-` | `-` |
| **0.3.x** | `~0.25.*` | `>=1.10` | `-` | `-` | `-` |
| **0.2.x** | `~0.24.*` | `>=1.9` | `-` | `-` | `-` |

# Installation - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/getting-started/getting-started/#installation)

Installation[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/getting-started/getting-started/#installation "Permanent link")

=====================================================================================================================

This guide will walk you through the Installation process of Trident.

Important

**Prerequisite**

It is expected that you have installed:

*   Rust ([Install Rust](https://www.rust-lang.org/tools/install)
    )
*   Solana CLI ([Install Solana CLI](https://docs.solanalabs.com/cli/install)
    )
*   Anchor Framework ([Install Anchor](https://www.anchor-lang.com/docs/installation)
    )

For supported versions check the [Supported Versions](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/getting-started/getting-started/#supported-versions)

Install System Dependencies[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/getting-started/getting-started/#install-system-dependencies "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Update your package list and install the required packages:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/getting-started/getting-started/#__codelineno-0-1) sudo apt-get update [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/getting-started/getting-started/#__codelineno-0-2) sudo apt-get install -y \     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/getting-started/getting-started/#__codelineno-0-3)     curl \    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/getting-started/getting-started/#__codelineno-0-4)     git \    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/getting-started/getting-started/#__codelineno-0-5)     build-essential \    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/getting-started/getting-started/#__codelineno-0-6)     pkg-config \    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/getting-started/getting-started/#__codelineno-0-7)     libssl-dev \    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/getting-started/getting-started/#__codelineno-0-8)     npm \    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/getting-started/getting-started/#__codelineno-0-9)     vim \    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/getting-started/getting-started/#__codelineno-0-10)     nano \    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/getting-started/getting-started/#__codelineno-0-11)     wget \    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/getting-started/getting-started/#__codelineno-0-12)     binutils-dev \    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/getting-started/getting-started/#__codelineno-0-13)     libunwind-dev \    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/getting-started/getting-started/#__codelineno-0-14)     lldb`

Install Trident and Honggfuzz[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/getting-started/getting-started/#install-trident-and-honggfuzz "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Install them using the following commands:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/getting-started/getting-started/#__codelineno-1-1) cargo install trident-cli [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/getting-started/getting-started/#__codelineno-1-2) cargo install honggfuzz`

Supported versions[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/getting-started/getting-started/#supported-versions "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Trident CLI | Anchor | Solana | Rust | Honggfuzz |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `v0.7.0` | `>=0.29.*`1 | `^1.17.4` | `nightly` | `0.5.56` |
| `v0.6.0` | `>=0.29.*`1 | `^1.17` | `nightly` | `0.5.55` |
| `v0.5.0` | `~0.28.*` | `=1.16.6` | \-  | \-  |
| `v0.4.0` | `~0.27.*` | `>=1.15` | \-  | \-  |
| `v0.3.0` | `~0.25.*` | `>=1.10` | \-  | \-  |
| `v0.2.0` | `~0.24.*` | `>=1.9` | \-  | \-  |

1.  To use Trident with Anchor 0.29.0, run the following commands from your project's root directory after Trident initialization:
    
    `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/getting-started/getting-started/#__codelineno-2-1) cargo update [[email protected]](https://ackee.xyz/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)  --precise 0.29.0 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/getting-started/getting-started/#__codelineno-2-2) cargo update [[email protected]](https://ackee.xyz/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)  --precise 0.29.0`
    

Back to top
