# Introduction - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/integration-tests/poc-introduction/#introduction)

Introduction[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/integration-tests/poc-introduction/#introduction "Permanent link")

========================================================================================================================

Trident supports writing Integration Tests in Rust.

marcinv@XPS15:~/Work/tooling/trident/examples/turnstile$ marcinv@XPS15:~/Work/tooling/trident/examples/turnstile$ t marcinv@XPS15:~/Work/tooling/trident/examples/turnstile$ tr marcinv@XPS15:~/Work/tooling/trident/examples/turnstile$ tri marcinv@XPS15:~/Work/tooling/trident/examples/turnstile$ trid marcinv@XPS15:~/Work/tooling/trident/examples/turnstile$ tride marcinv@XPS15:~/Work/tooling/trident/examples/turnstile$ triden marcinv@XPS15:~/Work/tooling/trident/examples/turnstile$ trident marcinv@XPS15:~/Work/tooling/trident/examples/turnstile$ trident marcinv@XPS15:~/Work/tooling/trident/examples/turnstile$ trident marcinv@XPS15:~/Work/tooling/trident/examples/turnstile$ trident t marcinv@XPS15:~/Work/tooling/trident/examples/turnstile$ trident te marcinv@XPS15:~/Work/tooling/trident/examples/turnstile$ trident tes marcinv@XPS15:~/Work/tooling/trident/examples/turnstile$ trident test marcinv@XPS15:~/Work/tooling/trident/examples/turnstile$ trident test Finished test \[unoptimized + debuginfo\] target(s) in 0.17s Running unittests src/lib.rs (target/debug/deps/program\_client-35df7129a7acbd48)running 0 teststest result: ok. 0 passed; 0 failed; 0 ignored; 0 measured; 0 filtered out; finished in 0.00s Running tests/test.rs (target/debug/deps/test-e1d41610f5897c1f)running 2 tests\-------------- TEST START --------------program\_keypair(1).pubkey = Po1RaS8BEDbNcn5oXsFryAeQ6Wn8fvmE111DJaKCgPCWaiting for fees to stabilize 1...test test\_unhappy\_path ... okWaiting for fees to stabilize 2...test test\_happy\_path ... oktest result: ok. 2 passed; 0 failed; 0 ignored; 0 measured; 0 filtered out; finished in 14.89s Running unittests src/lib.rs (target/debug/deps/turnstile-451803623b25a701)running 1 testtest test\_id ... oktest result: ok. 1 passed; 0 failed; 0 ignored; 0 measured; 0 filtered out; finished in 0.00s Doc-tests program\_clientmarcinv@XPS15:~/Work/tooling/trident/examples/turnstile$ exit

# Commands - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#commands)

Commands[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#commands "Permanent link")

==============================================================================================

Trident CLI supports the following commands:

`trident init`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#trident-init "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Initializes Trident Workspace and generates new Fuzz Test Template. Creates the following structure:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-1) project-root [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-2) ├── trident-tests [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-3) │   ├── fuzz_0 # particular fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-4) │   │   ├── instructions # instructions folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-5) │   │   ├── transactions # transactions folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-6) │   │   ├── test_fuzz.rs # the binary target of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-7) │   │   ├── types.rs # the types of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-8) │   │   └── fuzz_instructions.rs # the definition of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-9) │   ├── fuzz_1 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-10) │   ├── fuzz_X # possible multiple fuzz tests [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-11) │   ├── fuzzing # compilations and crashes folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-12) │   ├── Cargo.toml [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-13) │   └── Trident.toml # Configuration file located in trident-tests directory [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-14) └── ...`

#### Options[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#options "Permanent link")

*   `-f, --force` - Force Trident initialization. Trident dependencies will be updated based on the version of Trident CLI.
*   `-s, --skip-build` - Skip building the program before initializing Trident.
*   `-p, --program-name <FILE>` - Specify the name of the program for which fuzz test will be generated.
*   `-t, --test-name <NAME>` - Name of the fuzz test to initialize.

* * *

`trident how`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#trident-how "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Show the HowTo message about writing fuzz tests.

* * *

`trident fuzz`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#trident-fuzz "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Run fuzz subcommands. With fuzz subcommands you can add new fuzz test template or you can run fuzz test on already initialized one.

**Examples:**

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#__codelineno-1-1) trident fuzz add [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#__codelineno-1-2) trident fuzz run fuzz_0 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#__codelineno-1-3) trident fuzz debug <FUZZ_TARGET> <SEED>`

### `trident fuzz add`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#trident-fuzz-add "Permanent link")

Generate new Fuzz Test template.

#### Options[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#options_1 "Permanent link")

*   `-p, --program-name <FILE>` - Specify the name of the program for which the fuzz test will be generated.
*   `-t, --test-name <NAME>` - Name of the fuzz test to add.
*   `-s, --skip-build` - Skip building the program before adding new fuzz test.

* * *

### `trident fuzz run <fuzz_target>`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#trident-fuzz-run-fuzz_target "Permanent link")

Directory Note

Execute fuzz tests from the `trident-tests` directory.

Solana Logs

In case you want to see the logs of the fuzzed transactions, prefix the command with `TRIDENT_LOG=1`.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#__codelineno-2-1) TRIDENT_LOG=1 trident fuzz run <fuzz_target>`

Runs the specified Fuzz Target using Trident's Manually Guided Fuzzing (e.g., fuzz\_0).

#### Arguments[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#arguments "Permanent link")

*   `<fuzz_target>` - Name of the desired fuzz template to execute (for example fuzz\_0).
*   `[seed]` - Master seed used for fuzzing, if not provided it will be generated randomly.

#### Options[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#options_2 "Permanent link")

*   `-w, --with-exit-code` - Run the fuzzing with exit code, i.e. if it discovers crash the Trident will exit with exit code 1.

* * *

### `trident fuzz debug <fuzz_target> <seed>`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#trident-fuzz-debug-fuzz_target-seed "Permanent link")

Debug crashes by analyzing specific crash files using the provided seed.

#### Arguments[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#arguments_1 "Permanent link")

*   `<fuzz_target>` - Name of the desired fuzz template to execute (for example fuzz\_0).
*   `<seed>` - Master seed of the desired fuzz template to execute.

Debug Output

The debug output includes:

1.  Transaction logs
2.  Instruction data structures
3.  Panic/Crash information

* * *

`trident clean`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#trident-clean "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Clean build target, additionally perform `anchor clean`.

* * *

`trident server`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#trident-server "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Starts the Trident Server, in order to make it easier to visualize the fuzzing dashboard, more info in the [dashboard](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/)
 section.

* * *

`trident compare`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/#trident-compare "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Allows you to compare two fuzzing regression results. More info in the [regression](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/)
 section.

* * *

Back to top

---

# Changelog - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/CHANGELOG/#changelog)

Changelog[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/CHANGELOG/#changelog "Permanent link")

=========================================================================================

All notable changes to this project will be documented in this file.

The format is based on [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.0.0/)
, and this project adheres to [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html)
 (SemVer).

**Note**: Version 0 of Semantic Versioning is handled differently from version 1 and above. The minor version will be incremented upon a breaking change and the patch version will be incremented for features.

    )

    )

    )

    )
*   feat/allow direct accounts manipulation and storage ([#142](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/142)
    )
*   feat/support of non-corresponding instruction and context names ([#130](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/130)
    )
*   feat/refactored and improved program flow during init and build, added activity indicator ([#129](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/129)
    )
*   feat/allow solana versions up to v1.17.\* and pin Rust 1.77 nightly compiler ([#128](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/128)
    )
*   feat/new init command option to initialize fuzz or poc tests only ([#124](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/124)
    )

    )

    )

    )

    )

    )
*   feat/fuzzer framework core, macros, helpers, templates, and examples. ([#111](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/111)
    )
*   feat/improved trident-tests folder structure for PoC and Fuzz Tests ([#109](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/109)
    )
*   feat/support for additional fuzzer parameters in Trident.toml config file ([#107](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/107)
    )

    )
*   feat/client now reads by default keypair from default location ([#105](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/105)
    )
*   feat/added new --exit-code option to return corresponding exit code based on fuzz test result ([#104](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/104)

    )

    )

    )
*   fix/fixed fuzz test generation with init-if-needed Anchor feature ([#131](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/131)
    )

    )

    )

\[0.5.0\] - 2023-08-28[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/CHANGELOG/#050-2023-08-28 "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Added[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/CHANGELOG/#added_1 "Permanent link")

*   cli: Added trident subcommand `fuzz` to run and debug fuzz tests using honggfuzz-rs.
*   cli: Added trident `--skip-fuzzer` option for `init` subcommand to skip generation of fuzz test templates.
*   client: Added new Cargo feature `fuzzing` that enables optional dependencies related to fuzz testing.

\[0.4.1\] - 2023-08-21[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/CHANGELOG/#041-2023-08-21 "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Changed[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/CHANGELOG/#changed "Permanent link")

*   Upgrade Solana (`=1.16.6`) and Anchor framework (`=0.28.0`) versions.

### Fixed[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/CHANGELOG/#fixed_1 "Permanent link")

*   Implemented Anchor Client logic was not able to work with newer version of Anchor. Fixed with `async_rpc` and `async` feature.
*   Trident init IDL Parse Error on newer version of Rust, fixed with updated `accounts` token.

\[0.3.0\] - 2022-09-23[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/CHANGELOG/#030-2022-09-23 "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Changed[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/CHANGELOG/#changed_1 "Permanent link")

*   Upgrade Solana (`~1.10`) and Anchor framework (`~0.25`) versions

### Added[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/CHANGELOG/#added_2 "Permanent link")

*   Custom Solana RPC error reporter. If the Solana RPC error is thrown, the error code, message and data (logs) are reported to the output.
*   Custom imports in the `.program_client`. User is able to import custom types and structures into program client. The import part of the code would not be re-generated.

\[0.2.0\] - 2022-07-27[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/CHANGELOG/#020-2022-07-27 "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Added[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/CHANGELOG/#added_3 "Permanent link")

*   Trident is now configurable. This requires `Trident.toml` file to exist in the project's root directory - without this file the execution will fail. To solve this re-run `trident init` or just create an empty `Trident.toml` file in the project's root directory.

Back to top

---

*   feat/removed/updated deprecated functions, removed allow deprecated macros ([#103](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/103)
    )
*   feat/added new function to read keypair file generated by Anchor ([#102](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/102)
    )
*   feat/clean command ([#101](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/101)
    )
*   feat/improved program\_client generated code ([#100](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/100)
    )
*   feat/automatically add hfuzz\_target to .gitignore file ([#99](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/99)
    )
*   feat/support for dynamic templates. ([#98](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/98)
    )

**Fixed**

*   fix/refactored fuzz test executor error handling ([#127](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/127)
    )
*   fix/warn user on composite accounts and continue fuzz test generation ([#133](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/133)
    )
*   fix/progress bar loop lock release ([#132](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/132)
    )
*   fix/fixed fuzz test generation with init-if-needed Anchor feature ([#131](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/131)
    )
*   fix/program client custom types ([#117](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/117)
    )
*   fix/check fuzz test name collision by checking the name against HashSet ([#114](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/114)
    )

\[0.5.0\] - 2023-08-28[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/CHANGELOG/#050-2023-08-28 "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   cli: Added trident subcommand `fuzz` to run and debug fuzz tests using honggfuzz-rs.
*   cli: Added trident `--skip-fuzzer` option for `init` subcommand to skip generation of fuzz test templates.
*   client: Added new Cargo feature `fuzzing` that enables optional dependencies related to fuzz testing.

\[0.4.1\] - 2023-08-21[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/CHANGELOG/#041-2023-08-21 "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Changed**

*   Upgrade Solana (`=1.16.6`) and Anchor framework (`=0.28.0`) versions.

**Fixed**

*   Implemented Anchor Client logic was not able to work with newer version of Anchor. Fixed with `async_rpc` and `async` feature.
*   Trident init IDL Parse Error on newer version of Rust, fixed with updated `accounts` token.

\[0.3.0\] - 2022-09-23[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/CHANGELOG/#030-2022-09-23 "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Changed**

*   Upgrade Solana (`~1.10`) and Anchor framework (`~0.25`) versions

**Added**

*   Custom Solana RPC error reporter. If the Solana RPC error is thrown, the error code, message and data (logs) are reported to the output.
*   Custom imports in the `.program_client`. User is able to import custom types and structures into program client. The import part of the code would not be re-generated.

\[0.2.0\] - 2022-07-27[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/CHANGELOG/#020-2022-07-27 "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   Trident is now configurable. This requires `Trident.toml` file to exist in the project's root directory - without this file the execution will fail. To solve this re-run `trident init` or just create an empty `Trident.toml` file in the project's root directory.

Back to top

---

# Changelog - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/CHANGELOG/#changelog)

Changelog[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/CHANGELOG/#changelog "Permanent link")

=================================================================================================

All notable changes to this project will be documented in this file.

The format is based on [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.0.0/)
, and this project adheres to [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html)
 (SemVer).

**Note**: Version 0 of Semantic Versioning is handled differently from version 1 and above. The minor version will be incremented upon a breaking change and the patch version will be incremented for features.

    )

    )

**Removed**

    )
*   Add support for reproducible fuzzing with thread-specific seeds ([332](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/332)
    )
*   Move Trident.toml into trident-tests folder ([328](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/328)
    )

\[0.10.0\] - 2025-03-13[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/CHANGELOG/#0100-2025-03-13 "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   TransactionSelector allows to select and execute random transaction with hooks and without hooks ([297](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/297)
    )
*   Added "random\_tail" attribute to TridentFlowExecutor macro to allow random tail generation ([296](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/296)
    )
*   Added support for seeds constraint for accounts structs ([284](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/284)
    )
*   Additional methods accessing the AccountsStorage and creating corresponding accounts are now optional ("token","vote", "stake") ([279](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/279)
    )
*   Derive macros now use own syn parser for better extensibility and UX ([275](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/275)
    )
*   Program ID inside test\_fuzz.rs file is now automatically filled in is present in the program IDL ([272](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/272)
    )
*   Added additional attributes to TridentAccounts, mut and signer ([268](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/268)
    )
*   Users can now specify a program for which they want to add or initialize a fuzz test using `--program-name` flag ([273](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/273)
    )
*   Allow custom test name specification in fuzz test creation with `--test-name` flag ([274](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/274)
    )

**Removed**

*   The DisplayIx macro is now removed, Debug trait was implemented for instruction inputs ([281](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/281)
    )

**Changed**

*   FuzzTestExecutor and FlowExecutor are grouped together and FuzzTest has client as generic instead of TridentSVM ([294](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/294)
    )
*   Changed Transaction sequence logic ([289](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/289)
    )
*   AccountsStorages are simplified, no types are required to define ([276](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/276)
    )
*   Trident Architecture changes containing multiple features and improvements (details in the PR)([267](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/267)
    )
*   get or create token account methods fixed for native token accounts ([262](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/262)
    )

# FAQ - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/faq/#faq)

FAQ[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/faq/#faq "Permanent link")

===============================================================================

_Is Trident supported only with Anchor?_

*   Currently yes, Trident under the hood obtains data from the IDL generated by Anchor.

_I created the Fuzz Test, what should I do next?_

*   Start here [Start Fuzzing](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/)
    .

_Is Trident open-source?_

*   Yes, here [Trident](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident)
    .

_I would like to report an Issue with Trident, what should I do?_

*   Create [issue](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/issues)
    .

_Is Trident deployed on Mainnet / Devnet / Testnet?_

*   No, Trident is Fuzz Testing Framework, not Solana Program.

_What type of Fuzzer is Trident?_

*   Currently, we refer to it as _"coverage guided gray box fuzzer"_.

Back to top

---

# Installation - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/home/home-installation/#installation)

Installation[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/home/home-installation/#installation "Permanent link")

============================================================================================================

Dependencies[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/home/home-installation/#dependencies "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Check [supported versions](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/home/home-installation/#supported-versions)
 section for further details.

*   Install [Rust](https://www.rust-lang.org/tools/install)
    
*   Install [Solana tool suite](https://docs.solana.com/cli/install-solana-cli-tools)
    
*   Install [Anchor](https://www.anchor-lang.com/docs/installation)
    
*   Install [Honggfuzz-rs](https://github.com/rust-fuzz/honggfuzz-rs#how-to-use-this-crate)
     for fuzz testing

Installation[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/home/home-installation/#installation_1 "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/home/home-installation/#__codelineno-0-1) cargo install trident-cli [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/home/home-installation/#__codelineno-0-2)[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/home/home-installation/#__codelineno-0-3) # or the specific version [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/home/home-installation/#__codelineno-0-4)[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/home/home-installation/#__codelineno-0-5) cargo install --version <version> trident-cli`

### Supported versions[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/home/home-installation/#supported-versions "Permanent link")

*   We support `Anchor` and `Solana` versions specified in the table below.

| Trident CLI | Anchor | Solana | Rust |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `v0.6.0` | `>=0.29.*`1 | `^1.17` | `nightly` |
| `v0.5.0` | `~0.28.*` | `=1.16.6` |     |
| `v0.4.0` | `~0.27.*` | `>=1.15` |     |
| `v0.3.0` | `~0.25.*` | `>=1.10` |     |
| `v0.2.0` | `~0.24.*` | `>=1.9` |     |

1.  To use Trident with Anchor 0.29.0, run the following commands from your project's root directory after Trident initialization:
    
    `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/home/home-installation/#__codelineno-1-1) cargo update [[email protected]](https://ackee.xyz/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)  --precise 0.29.0 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/home/home-installation/#__codelineno-1-2) cargo update [[email protected]](https://ackee.xyz/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)  --precise 0.29.0`
    

Back to top

# Run - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/integration-tests/poc-run/#run)

Run[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/integration-tests/poc-run/#run "Permanent link")

=============================================================================================

Once you have finished the implementation of the Integration Test, you can run the Test as follows:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/integration-tests/poc-run/#__codelineno-0-1) trident test`

Skipping tests[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/integration-tests/poc-run/#skipping-tests "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   You can add the `#[ignore]` macro to skip the test.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/integration-tests/poc-run/#__codelineno-1-1) #[trident_test] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/integration-tests/poc-run/#__codelineno-1-2) #[ignore] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.7.0/integration-tests/poc-run/#__codelineno-1-3) async fn test() {}`

# Introduction - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-introduction/#introduction)

Introduction[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-introduction/#introduction "Permanent link")

==================================================================================================================

Fuzzing is a software testing technique that involves providing invalid, unexpected, or random data as inputs to a computer program. The aim is to uncover bugs and vulnerabilities that might not be detected with conventional testing strategies.

Trident[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-introduction/#trident "Permanent link")

========================================================================================================

The `Trident` testing framework equips developers with tools to efficiently develop fuzz tests for Anchor-based programs. It streamlines the fuzz testing process through automation and comprehensive support:

*   Automatically parses Anchor-based programs to generate necessary implementations for deserializing instruction accounts.
*   Generates templates for developers to customize according to the specific needs of their fuzz test scenarios.
*   Offers derive macros to effortlessly implement required traits, reducing manual coding efforts.
*   Includes a bank client and helper functions for simplified account management during testing.
*   Provides a Command-Line Interface (CLI) for executing and debugging fuzz tests with ease.

`Trident` is built for customization, enabling developers to tailor their fuzz tests by adjusting:

*   **Execution Order of Instructions**: Test different sequences and their effects on the program to uncover sequence-related vulnerabilities.
*   **Instruction Parameters**: Identify how variations in inputs influence program behavior, testing for robustness against a wide range of data.
*   **Instruction Accounts**: Explore the impact of different account states on the software's functionality, ensuring comprehensive account testing.
*   **Comprehensive Testing**: Conduct thorough and effective fuzz testing by combining any of the above aspects.

This framework supports a detailed and methodical approach to fuzz testing, facilitating the identification and remediation of potential vulnerabilities in software applications.

Back to top

---

# Start Fuzzing - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/#start-fuzzing)

Start Fuzzing[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/#start-fuzzing "Permanent link")

======================================================================================================

To start writting fuzz tests, you need to initialize Trident in your Anchor-based workspace.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-0-1) trident init`

If you have already initialized Trident, you can add a new fuzz test using:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-1-1) trident fuzz add`

Trident creates a new fuzz test template in the `trident-tests` directory, with the following structure:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-1) project-root [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-2) ├── trident-tests [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-3) │   ├── fuzz_0 # particular fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-4) │   │   ├── instructions # instructions folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-5) │   │   ├── transactions # transactions folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-6) │   │   ├── test_fuzz.rs # the binary target of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-7) │   │   ├── types.rs # the types of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-8) │   │   └── fuzz_instructions.rs # the definition of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-9) │   ├── fuzz_1 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-10) │   ├── fuzz_X # possible multiple fuzz tests [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-11) │   ├── fuzzing # compilations and crashes folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-12) │   └── Cargo.toml [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-13) ├── Trident.toml [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-14) └── ...`

`Instructions` folder contains the `instructions` that can be used in the fuzz test.

`Transactions` folder contains the `transactions` that will be used during the fuzzing, each transaction can contain `one` or `multiple instructions`, based on the developers choice. By default there is only one instruction in each transaction.

Back to top

---

# Start Fuzzing - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/#start-fuzzing)

Start Fuzzing[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/#start-fuzzing "Permanent link")

===================================================================================================

To start writing fuzz tests, you need to initialize Trident in your Anchor-based workspace.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-0-1) trident init`

If you have already initialized Trident, you can add a new fuzz test using:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-1-1) trident fuzz add`

Trident creates a new fuzz test template in the `trident-tests` directory, with the following structure:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-1) project-root [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-2) ├── trident-tests [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-3) │   ├── fuzz_0 # particular fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-4) │   │   ├── instructions # instructions folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-5) │   │   ├── transactions # transactions folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-6) │   │   ├── test_fuzz.rs # the binary target of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-7) │   │   ├── types.rs # the types of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-8) │   │   └── fuzz_instructions.rs # the definition of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-9) │   ├── fuzz_1 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-10) │   ├── fuzz_X # possible multiple fuzz tests [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-11) │   ├── fuzzing # compilations and crashes folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-12) │   ├── Cargo.toml [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-13) │   └── Trident.toml [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/#__codelineno-2-14) └── ...`

`Instructions` folder contains the `instructions` that can be used in the fuzz test.

`Transactions` folder contains the `transactions` that will be used during the fuzzing, each transaction can contain `one` or `multiple instructions`, based on the developer's choice. By default there is only one instruction in each transaction.

# Run and Debug - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#run-and-debug)

Run and Debug[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#run-and-debug "Permanent link")

=================================================================================================================

Run[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#run "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once you have finished the implementation of the Fuzz Test, you can run the Test as follows:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-0-1) # Replace <TARGET_NAME> with the name of particular [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-0-2) # fuzz test (for example: "fuzz_0") [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-0-3) trident fuzz run <TARGET_NAME>`

Under the hood Trident uses [honggfuzz-rs](https://github.com/rust-fuzz/honggfuzz-rs)
.

You can pass [supported parameters](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/blob/develop/examples/fuzz_example0/Trident.toml)
 via the **Trident.toml** configuration file. For example:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-1) # Content of Trident.toml [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-2) [fuzz] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-3) # Timeout in seconds (default: 10) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-4) timeout = 10 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-5) # Number of fuzzing iterations (default: 0 [no limit]) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-6) iterations = 10000 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-7) # Number of concurrent fuzzing threads (default: 0 [number of CPUs / 2]) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-8) threads = 0 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-9) # Don't close children's stdin, stdout, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-10) # stderr; can be noisy (default: false) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-11) keep_output = false [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-12) # Disable ANSI console; use simple log output (default: false) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-13) verbose = false [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-14) # Exit upon seeing the first crash (default: false) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-15) exit_upon_crash = true [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-16) # Maximal number of mutations per one run (default: 6) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-17) mutations_per_run = 6 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-18) # Target compilation directory, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-19) # (default: "" ["trident-tests/fuzz_tests/fuzzing/hfuzz_target"]). [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-20) # To not clash with cargo build's default target directory. [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-21) cargo_target_dir = "" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-22) # Honggfuzz working directory, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-23) # (default: "" ["trident-tests/fuzz_tests/fuzzing/hfuzz_workspace"]). [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-24) hfuzz_workspace = "" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-25) # Directory where crashes are saved to (default: "" [workspace directory]) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-26) crashdir = "" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-27) # Input file extension (e.g. 'swf'), (default: "" ['fuzz']) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-28) extension = "" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-29) # Number of seconds this fuzzing session will last (default: 0 [no limit]) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-30) run_time = 0 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-31) # Maximal size of files processed by the fuzzer [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-32) # in bytes (default: 1048576 = 1MB) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-33) max_file_size = 1048576 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-34) # Save all test-cases (not only the unique ones) by [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-35) # appending the current time-stamp to the filenames (default: false) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-1-36) save_all = false`

Or you can pass any parameter via [environment variables](https://github.com/rust-fuzz/honggfuzz-rs#environment-variables)
.

A list of hongfuzz parameters can be found in honggfuzz [usage documentation](https://github.com/google/honggfuzz/blob/master/docs/USAGE.md#cmdline---help)
. The parameters passed via **environment variables** have **higher priority**. For example:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-2-1) # Time-out: 10 secs [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-2-2) # Number of concurrent fuzzing threads: 1 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-2-3) # Number of fuzzing iterations: 10000 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-2-4) # Display Solana logs in the terminal [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-2-5) HFUZZ_RUN_ARGS="-t 10 -n 1 -N 10000 -Q" trident fuzz run <TARGET_NAME>`

Debug[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#debug "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To debug your program with values from a crash file:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-3-1) # fuzzer will run the <TARGET_NAME> with the specified <CRASH_FILE_PATH> [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-3-2) trident fuzz run-debug <TARGET_NAME> <CRASH_FILE_PATH> [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-3-3) # for example: [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-run-debug/#__codelineno-3-4) trident fuzz run-debug fuzz_0 trident-tests/fuzz_tests/fuzzing/fuzz_0/cr1.fuzz`

Back to top

# Fuzz Test Lifecycle - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-lifecycle/#fuzz-test-lifecycle)

Fuzz Test Lifecycle[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-lifecycle/#fuzz-test-lifecycle "Permanent link")

=============================================================================================================================

In the sequence diagram below you can see a simplified fuzz test lifecycle.

Some diagram states are labeled with emojis:

*   ⚡ Mandatory methods that must be implemented by the user.
*   👤 Optional methods that can be implemented by the user.

Lifecycle[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-lifecycle/#lifecycle "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  The fuzzer is running until:
    1.  The maximal number of iterations is reached (if specified).
    2.  A crash was detected and the `exit_upon_crash` parameter was set.
    3.  User interrupted the test manually (for example by hitting `CTRL+C`).
2.  In each iteration, the fuzzer generates a sequence of random instructions to execute.
    1.  User can optionally customize how the instructions are generated and can specify the instructions that should be executed at the beginning (`pre_ixs`), in the middle (`ixs`) and at the end (`post_ixs`) of each iteration. This can be useful for example if your program needs an initialization or you want to fuzz some specific program state.
3.  For each instruction:
    1.  User defined mandatory method `get_accounts()` is called to collect necessary instruction accounts.
    2.  User defined mandatory method `get_data()` is called to collect instruction data.
    3.  A snapshot of all instruction accounts before the instruction execution is saved.
    4.  The instruction is executed.
    5.  A snapshot of all instruction accounts after the instruction execution is saved.
    6.  User defined optional method `check()` is called to check accounts data and evaluate invariants.

fuzzer\_iterations = 0

fuzzer\_iterations = 0

fuzzer\_iterations < 

max\_iterations

fuzzer\_iterations <...

done

done

create pre-instruction 

accounts snapshots

create pre-instruction...

execute instruction

execute instruction

create post-instruction 

accounts snapshots

create post-instruction...

check invariants 👤

check invariants 👤

fuzzer\_iterations++

fuzzer\_iterations++Generate instructions

pre\_ixs 👤

pre\_ixs 👤

ixs 👤

ixs 👤

post\_ixs 👤

post\_ixs 👤

end

end

for ix in instructions

for ix in instructions

get instruction accounts ⚡

get instruction accounts ⚡

get instruction data ⚡

get instruction data ⚡

next ix

next ixText is not SVG - cannot display

Back to top

# Writing fuzz test - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/#writing-fuzz-test)

Writing fuzz test[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/#writing-fuzz-test "Permanent link")

=================================================================================================================================

Trident is Manually Guided fuzzing framework for Solana programs.

In order to start fuzzing, you need to guide the fuzzer by specifying what are the expected inputs to instruction or the expected sequences of instructions to execute.

**Why is this important?**

Letting the fuzzer to generate completely random instruction inputs and completely random sequences of instruction would lead in most case

*   to transaction failures, which would mean the fuzzer is not properly fuzzing the logic within the program; and
*   executing irrelevant random instruction sequences, which would again lead to transaction failures.

Guide the fuzzer[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/#guide-the-fuzzer "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Start with properly configuring different types of instruction inputs:

*   [Instruction Data](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-data/)
    
*   [Instruction Accounts](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/)
    
*   [Fuzzing Flows](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/)
    
*   (Optional) [Remaining Accounts](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/)
    

Back to top

---

# Current limitations - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-current-limitations/#current-limitations)

Current limitations[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/fuzzing/fuzzing-current-limitations/#current-limitations "Permanent link")

=======================================================================================================================================

This section summarizes some known limitations in the current development stage. Further development will be focused on resolving these limitations.

*   Only fuzzing of one program without CPIs to other custom programs is supported.
*   Remaining accounts in check methods are not supported.
*   Composite accounts are not supported (however it is possible to generate a fuzz test and finish the composite accounts deserialization manually).

Back to top

---

# Trident API & Macro Reference - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-api-macro/#trident-api-macro-reference)

Trident API & Macro Reference[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-api-macro/#trident-api-macro-reference "Permanent link")

=====================================================================================================================================

This section contains the API and macro reference for Trident.

Trident[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-api-macro/#trident "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Trident struct is the main entry point for fuzzing. It provides methods to interact with the fuzzing environment.

*   [Trident](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-api-macro/trident/trident/)
    

Trident's Fuzz Client[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-api-macro/#tridents-fuzz-client "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

FuzzClient represents the API to interact with the client.

*   [FuzzClient](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/fuzz-client-trait/)
    

Trident Accounts attributes[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-api-macro/#trident-accounts-attributes "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Trident Accounts attributes help to define accounts used in the fuzzing environment.

*   [TridentAccounts](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-api-macro/attributes-for-accounts/account-attributes/)
    

Hooks[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-api-macro/#hooks "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Transaction Hooks are used to customize what should be done before the transaction is executed, after it is executed and to check if the changes are valid with invariant checks.

*   [TransactionHooks](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-api-macro/hooks/transaction-hooks/)
    

Instruction Hooks are used to customize instruction data and accounts if the Trident Accounts attributes are not enough.

*   [InstructionHooks](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-api-macro/hooks/instruction-hooks/)
    

Trident Macros[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-api-macro/#trident-macros "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Trident macros are used to define required methods for fuzzing.

*   [TridentTransaction](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-transaction/)
    
*   [TridentInstruction](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-instruction/)
    
*   [TridentAccounts](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-accounts/)
    
*   [TridentRemainingAccounts](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-remaining-accounts/)
    
*   [TridentFlowExecutor](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-api-macro/trident-macros/trident-flow-executor/)

# Executing the Fuzz Test - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#executing-the-fuzz-test)

Executing the Fuzz Test[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#executing-the-fuzz-test "Permanent link")

==============================================================================================================================================

To execute the fuzz test, navigate to the `trident-tests` directory and run the following command to execute the fuzz test:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-0-1) trident fuzz run <FUZZ_TARGET> <SEED> [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-0-2) # for example: [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-0-3) # trident fuzz run fuzz_0 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-0-4) # seed is optional, if not provided, a random seed will be used`

Directory Note

Execute fuzz tests from the `trident-tests` directory.

Solana Logs

In case you want to see the logs of the fuzzed transactions, prefix the command with `TRIDENT_LOG=1`.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-1-1) TRIDENT_LOG=1 trident fuzz run <fuzz_target> <seed>`

For the output reference and additional options such as debugging the found issues, check out [Commands](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/basics/commands/)
.

For the additional customization through the `trident.toml` file, check out the [Trident Manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/)
 page.

Back to top

---

# Run - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/integration-tests/poc-run/#run)

Run[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/integration-tests/poc-run/#run "Permanent link")

=============================================================================================

Once you have finished the implementation of the Integration Test, you can run the Test as follows:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/integration-tests/poc-run/#__codelineno-0-1) trident test`

Skipping tests[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/integration-tests/poc-run/#skipping-tests "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   You can add the `#[ignore]` macro to skip the test.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/integration-tests/poc-run/#__codelineno-1-1) #[trident_test] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/integration-tests/poc-run/#__codelineno-1-2) #[ignore] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.6.0/integration-tests/poc-run/#__codelineno-1-3) async fn test() {}`

Back to top

# Introduction - Trident

# Code Coverage - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/code-coverage/#code-coverage)

Code Coverage[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/code-coverage/#code-coverage "Permanent link")

=======================================================================================================================

Trident's code coverage feature analyzes which parts of your Solana program are tested during fuzzing sessions, helping you identify untested code paths and improve test effectiveness.

 Your browser does not support the video tag.

Key features:

*   **Real-time Analysis**: Monitor coverage as fuzzing progresses
*   **Multiple Formats**: Generate reports in JSON and HTML formats
*   **VS Code Integration**: Visualize coverage directly in your IDE using [Solana VS Code extension](https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=AckeeBlockchain.solana)
    
*   **Detailed Reporting**: Get insights into line coverage, branch coverage, and execution paths

Gathering Coverage Data[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/code-coverage/#gathering-coverage-data "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Enable coverage in the [Trident manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-coverage)
    
2.  Deploy your program through the [entrypoint](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#entrypoint-deployment)
    
3.  Run the fuzz test

Viewing Coverage Reports[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/code-coverage/#viewing-coverage-reports "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You have two options for displaying coverage data: generate an HTML report for browser viewing, or generate a JSON report for VS Code integration.

### Live Coverage Updates[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/code-coverage/#live-coverage-updates "Permanent link")

For real-time coverage monitoring during fuzzing:

1.  Set `format = "json"` in the [Trident manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-coverage)
    
2.  Set `loopcount` to a value other than `0` e.g., `5` for frequent updates, for more info check out [Trident manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#entrypoint-deployment)
    
3.  Install the [Solana VS Code extension](https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=AckeeBlockchain.solana)
    
4.  Choose one of these options:
    *   **Automatic**: Set `attach_extension = true` in the [Trident manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-coverage)
         to automatically show live updates while the fuzz test is running
    *   **Manual**: Use the command `Solana: Show Code Coverage` and select the "Attach to active fuzzing session" option

### Post-Session Coverage Analysis[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/code-coverage/#post-session-coverage-analysis "Permanent link")

1.  Set `format = "json"` in the [Trident manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-coverage)
     before running the fuzz test
2.  Run the fuzz test
3.  Install the [Solana VS Code extension](https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=AckeeBlockchain.solana)
    
4.  Run the VS Code command `Solana: Show Code Coverage` and select the "Load generated JSON report" option

### HTML Report[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/code-coverage/#html-report "Permanent link")

1.  Set `format = "html"` in the [Trident manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-coverage)
     before running the fuzz test
2.  Run the fuzz test
3.  After the fuzz test finishes, the HTML report will be stored in the `<fuzz-test-name>-coverage-report` folder
4.  Open the HTML report in your browser

Back to top

# Trident Manifest - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#trident-manifest)

Trident Manifest[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#trident-manifest "Permanent link")

============================================================================================================

Trident supports its own Trident Manifest, called `Trident.toml`. This section describes all possible configuration fields.

Fuzzing Metrics[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-metrics "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-0-1) [fuzz.metrics] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-0-2) enabled = true [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-0-3) dashboard = false [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-0-4) json = false`

*   `enabled` - Trident will show and save statistics after the fuzzing session.
*   `dashboard` - Trident will save a HTML dashboard after the fuzzing session.
*   `json` - Trident will save a JSON file after the fuzzing session.

* * *

Regression testing[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#regression-testing "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-1-1) [fuzz.regression] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-1-2) enabled = true`

*   `enabled` - Trident will save a JSON file with all monitored states after the fuzzing session.

Regression testing

*   Keep in mind that the feature hashes contents of accounts, if the contents are dependant for example on time, the final hash might not be the same as the one from the first fuzzing session.

* * *

Fuzzing Coverage[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-coverage "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-1) [fuzz.coverage] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-2) enable = true               # default: false [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-3) server_port = 58432         # default: 58432 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-4) loopcount = 5               # default: 0 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-5) format = "json"             # default: "json" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-6) attach_extension = true     # default: false`

The coverage configuration enables code coverage analysis during fuzzing sessions, providing insights into which parts of your program are being tested.

*   `enable` - When set to `true`, Trident collects code coverage data throughout the fuzzing session and generates a comprehensive report upon completion.
*   `server_port` - Specifies the HTTP server port used for communication between Trident and the [Solana VS Code extension](https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=AckeeBlockchain.solana)
    .
*   `loopcount` - Defines the number of execution flows processed before generating an intermediate coverage data file. Lower values provide more frequent coverage updates at the cost of performance. When set to `0`, coverage files are only generated at the end of the fuzzing session.
*   `format` - Determines the output format for coverage reports. Trident supports both `json` and `html` formats.
*   `attach_extension` - Enables real-time coverage visualization in VS Code when the extension is active. This feature requires `loopcount` to be greater than `0` and `format` to be set to `json`.

Warning

Coverage is only gathered for the programs deployed through an entrypoint!

Entrypoint deployment guide

1.  Comment out the program in `Trident.toml`
    
     `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-3-1)  # [[fuzz.programs]] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-3-2)  # address = "example_address" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-3-3)  # program = "../target/deploy/example_program.so"`
    
2.  Add the program dependency to `Cargo.toml`
    
     `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-4-1)  [dependencies.example_program] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-4-2)  path = "../programs/example_program"`
    
3.  Add `syscall-v1` or `syscall-v2` feature depending on the version of `solana-program`. Programs written for `solana-program` v1.x should use `syscall-v1`, programs written for `solana-program` v2.x should use `syscall-v2` feature.
    
     `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-5-1)  [dependencies.trident-fuzz] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-5-2)  features = ["syscall-v2"]`
    
4.  Import the programs entrypoint in `test_fuzz.rs`
    
     `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-6-1)  use example_program::entry as example_entrypoint;`
    
5.  Deploy the entrypoint in `test_fuzz.rs`
    
     `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-1)  impl FuzzTest {   [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-2)    fn new() -> Self {       [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-3)        let mut trident = Trident::default(); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-4)       [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-5)        // Deploy through the entrypoint       [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-6)        let program = TridentEntrypoint::new(example_program::ID, None, processor!(example_entrypoint));       [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-7)        trident.get_client().deploy_entrypoint(program); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-8)       [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-9)        Self {           [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-10)            trident,           [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-11)            fuzz_accounts: FuzzAccounts::default(),       [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-12)        }   [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-13)    }   [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-14)    ...`

* * *

Programs[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#programs "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Use dumped program from desired cluster, during fuzzing.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-8-1) [[fuzz.programs]] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-8-2) address = "metaqbxxUerdq28cj1RbAWkYQm3ybzjb6a8bt518x1s" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-8-3) upgrade_authority = "account address goes here" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-8-4) program = "metaplex-program/metaplex-token-metadata.so"`

* * *

Accounts[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#accounts "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Use dumped accounts from desired cluster, during fuzzing.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-9-1) [[fuzz.accounts]] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-9-2) address = "6YG3J7PaxyMnnbU67ifyrgF3BzNzc7cD8hPkqK6ATweE" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-9-3) filename = "tests/accounts/core_bridge_mainnet/guardian_set_5_mock.json"`

* * *

# TridentSVM - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-svm/#tridentsvm)

TridentSVM[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-svm/#tridentsvm "Permanent link")

===========================================================================================

TridentSVM is a fast execution and accounts storage environment which is utilized within the Trident.

TridentSVM uses [Anza's SVM API](https://www.anza.xyz/blog/anzas-new-svm-api)

# Installation - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/installation/installation/#installation)

Installation[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/installation/installation/#installation "Permanent link")

===============================================================================================================

Important

**Prerequisite**

It is expected that you have installed:

*   Rust ([Install Rust](https://www.rust-lang.org/tools/install)
    )
*   Solana CLI ([Install Solana CLI](https://docs.solanalabs.com/cli/install)
    )
*   Anchor Framework ([Install Anchor](https://www.anchor-lang.com/docs/installation)
    )

For supported versions check the [Supported Versions](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/installation/installation/#supported-versions)

Install System Dependencies[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/installation/installation/#install-system-dependencies "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Update your package list and install the required packages:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-0-1) sudo apt-get update [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-0-2) sudo apt-get install -y \     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-0-3)     curl \    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-0-4)     git \    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-0-5)     build-essential \    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-0-6)     pkg-config \    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-0-7)     libssl-dev \    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-0-8)     npm \    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-0-9)     vim \    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-0-10)     nano \    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-0-11)     wget \    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-0-12)     binutils-dev \    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-0-13)     libunwind-dev \    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-0-14)     lldb`

Install Hongfuzz[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/installation/installation/#install-hongfuzz "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Install honggfuzz

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-1-1) cargo install honggfuzz`

Install Trident[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/installation/installation/#install-trident "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-2-1) cargo install trident-cli`

Supported versions[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/installation/installation/#supported-versions "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| **_Trident CLI_** | **_Anchor_** | **_Solana_** | **_Rust_** | **_Honggfuzz_** |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **_`develop`_** | `0.30.1` | `^1.17.4` | `nightly` | `0.5.56` |
| **_`0.8.*`_** | `0.30.1` | `^1.17.4` | `nightly` | `0.5.56` |
| **_`0.7.0`_** | `>=0.29.*`1 | `^1.17.4` | `nightly` | `0.5.56` |
| **_`0.6.0`_** | `>=0.29.*`1 | `^1.17` | `nightly` | `0.5.55` |
| **_`0.5.0`_** | `~0.28.*` | `=1.16.6` | \-  | \-  |
| **_`0.4.0`_** | `~0.27.*` | `>=1.15` | \-  | \-  |
| **_`0.3.0`_** | `~0.25.*` | `>=1.10` | \-  | \-  |
| **_`0.2.0`_** | `~0.24.*` | `>=1.9` | \-  | \-  |

1.  To use Trident with Anchor 0.29.0, run the following commands from your project's root directory after Trident initialization:
    
    `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-3-1) cargo update [[email protected]](https://ackee.xyz/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)  --precise 0.29.0 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-3-2) cargo update [[email protected]](https://ackee.xyz/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)  --precise 0.29.0`

# Dashboard - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#dashboard)

Dashboard[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#dashboard "Permanent link")

===========================================================================================================

The Trident Dashboard provides a web-based interface for visualizing fuzzing session results through interactive charts and comprehensive statistics.

 Your browser does not support the video tag.

Features:

*   **Session Statistics**: View execution counts, success rates, and performance metrics
*   **Interactive Charts**: Explore results through dynamic visualizations
*   **Browser Access**: Open in any web browser without additional software
*   **Comprehensive Analysis**: Insights into instruction coverage and account interactions

Viewing the Dashboard[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#viewing-the-dashboard "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Open another terminal window and execute `trident server` from the fuzz-tests directory.
    
2.  Open your browser and navigate to the provided URL (typically `http://localhost:8080`).
    
3.  Enable the dashboard in the [Trident manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-metrics)
     by setting `dashboard = true`.
    
    `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-0-1) [fuzz.metrics] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-0-2) enabled = true [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-0-3) dashboard = true`
    
4.  Run the fuzz test to generate dashboard data.
    

Monitoring custom fuzzing metrics[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#monitoring-custom-fuzzing-metrics "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Trident allows you to monitor custom fuzzing metrics. If your program expects integer instruction inputs, it is possible to collect data on the randomly generated values and display them in the dashboard.

To do this, you need to add `trident.add_histogram_metric` to the `#[init]`, `#[flow]` or `#[end]` functions. The following code snippet shows how the `InitializeFnTransaction` instruction input is monitored; the statistics will be displayed in the dashboard.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-1) #[flow_executor] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-2) impl FuzzTest {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-3)     fn new() -> Self {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-4)         Self {            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-5)             trident: Trident::default(),            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-6)             fuzz_accounts: FuzzAccounts::default(),        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-7)         }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-8)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-9)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-10)     #[init]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-11)     fn start(&mut self) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-12)         let mut ix = InitializeFnTransaction::build(&mut self.trident, &mut self.fuzz_accounts); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-13)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-14)         self.trident.execute_transaction(&mut ix, Some("Init"));    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-15)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-16)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-17)     #[flow(weight = 5)]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-18)     fn flow1(&mut self) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-19)         let mut ix = InitializeFnTransaction::build(&mut self.trident, &mut self.fuzz_accounts);        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-20)         self.trident.execute_transaction(&mut ix, Some("Flow1")); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-21)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-22)         // Add the histogram metric to the dashboard        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-23)         self.trident            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-24)             .add_histogram_metric("flow1_metric", ix.instruction.data.input as f64);    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-25)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-26)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-27)     #[flow(weight = 5)]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-28)     fn flow2(&mut self) {      [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-29)       //....    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-30)     }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-31)     #[flow(weight = 90)]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-32)     fn flow3(&mut self) {      [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-33)       //....    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-34)     }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-35)     #[end]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-36)     fn cleanup(&mut self) -> Result<(), FuzzingError> {      [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-37)       //....    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-38)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-39) }`

# Trident examples - Trident

 

Trident examples
================

*   **Hello World!**
    
    * * *
    
    Hello World example with Trident.

    Trident provides a fuzzing pipeline that can be used to fuzz your programs.
