# Writing fuzz test - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#initialize-trident)

Writing fuzz test
=================

Initialize Trident[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#initialize-trident "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Initialize Trident in the Anchor-based workspace.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-0-1) trident init`

Info

Trident under the hood

*   Builds the Anchor-based project.
*   Reads the generated IDL.
*   Based on the IDL creates the fuzzing template.

Tip

If you have Trident already initialized, you can add new fuzz test using `trident fuzz add`.

Fill the Fuzz test Template[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#fill-the-fuzz-test-template "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Define Fuzz Accounts[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#define-fuzz-accounts "Permanent link")

Define `AccountsStorage` type for each Account you would like to use.

Important

Keep in mind:

*   You do not need to specify every `AccountStorage`, some accounts do not necessarily need to be stored in their corresponding storage.
    *   For example `System Program` does not need to be stored, rather can be used from the `solana_sdk`.
*   If you are about to Initialize `Mint` or `Token Account` in your Solana Program.
    *   use `Keypair` or `PdaStore` (not `MintStore` or `TokenStore`).
*   If you are going to initialize `Associated Token Account` in your Solana Program.
    *   use `PdaStore`.
*   You can rename `FuzzAccounts` fields to whatever you want. The default names were generated based on the Program's `IDL`.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-1-1) #[doc = r" Use AccountsStorage<T> where T can be one of:"] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-1-2) #[doc = r" Keypair, PdaStore, TokenStore, MintStore, ProgramStore"] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-1-3) #[derive(Default)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-1-4) pub struct FuzzAccounts {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-1-5)     author: AccountsStorage<Keypair>,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-1-6)     hello_world_account: AccountsStorage<PdaStore>,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-1-7)     // No need to fuzz system_program    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-1-8)     // system_program: AccountsStorage<todo!()>, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-1-9) }`

Tip

For more details about the `AccountsStorage` check [AccountsStorage](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/account-storages/)
.

### Implement Fuzz Instructions[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#implement-fuzz-instructions "Permanent link")

Each Instruction in the Fuzz Test has to have defined the following functions:

*   `get_program_id()`
    *   Specifies to which program the Instruction belongs. This function is **automatically defined** and should not need any updates. The importance is such that if you have multiple programs in your workspace, Trident can generate Instruction Sequences of Instruction corresponding to different programs.
*   `get_data()`
    *   Specifies what Instruction inputs are send to the Program Instructions.
*   `get_accounts()`
    *   Specifies what Accounts are send to the Program Instructions.

Tip

*   For more info about how to write these functions, check the [Fuzz Instructions](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/)
    .
*   For the examples how to write these functions, check the [Examples](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/examples/examples/)
    .

Execute[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#execute "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Run Fuzz Test[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#run-fuzz-test "Permanent link")

To execute the desired fuzz test using the Honggfuzz, run:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-2-1) # Replace <TARGET_NAME> with the name of particular [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-2-2) # fuzz test (for example: "fuzz_0") [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-2-3) trident fuzz run-hfuzz <TARGET_NAME>`

### Debug Fuzz Test[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#debug-fuzz-test "Permanent link")

To debug your program using Honggfuzz with values from a crash file:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-3-1) # fuzzer will run the <TARGET_NAME> with the specified <CRASH_FILE_PATH> [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-3-2) trident fuzz debug-hfuzz <TARGET_NAME> <CRASH_FILE_PATH>`

Tip

By default, the crashfiles are stored in the

*   `trident-tests/fuzz_tests/fuzzing/honggfuzz/hfuzz_workspace/<FUZZ_TARGET>` for Hongfuzz and

Tip

For more info about the fuzzing outputs chech the [Commands](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/)

Back to top

---

# Regression testing - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#regression-testing)

Regression testing[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#regression-testing "Permanent link")

==============================================================================================================================

Regression testing is the process of re-running tests to ensure that previously working functionality still works after code changes.

Trident allows for regression testing by specifying which accounts should be included in the regression test, generating a JSON file format with all monitored state and providing a subcommand to compare two regression test results.

Regression test setup[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#regression-test-setup "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  First, decide which account(s) should be included in the regression test.
    
2.  Add the accounts for tracking, this can be done as shown in the following code snippet. Check the `add_to_regression` method.
    
    `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-1) #[flow_executor] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-2) impl FuzzTest {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-3)     fn new() -> Self {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-4)         Self {            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-5)             trident: Trident::default(),            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-6)             fuzz_accounts: FuzzAccounts::default(),        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-7)         }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-8)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-9)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-10)     #[init]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-11)     fn start(&mut self) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-12)         let mut ix = InitializeFnTransaction::build(&mut self.trident, &mut self.fuzz_accounts); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-13)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-14)         self.trident.execute_transaction(&mut ix, Some("Init")); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-15)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-16)         // Add the account to the regression test        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-17)         self.trident.add_to_regression(            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-18)             &ix.instruction.accounts.hello_world_account.pubkey(),            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-19)             "hello_world_account",        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-20)         );    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-21)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-22)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-23)     #[flow(weight = 5)]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-24)     fn flow1(&mut self) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-25)         // This flow will be executed 60% of the time        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-26)         let mut ix = InitializeFnTransaction::build(&mut self.trident, &mut self.fuzz_accounts);        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-27)         self.trident.execute_transaction(&mut ix, Some("Flow1"));    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-28)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-29)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-30)     #[flow(weight = 5)]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-31)     fn flow2(&mut self) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-32)         // This flow will be executed 40% of the time        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-33)         let mut ix = InitializeFnTransaction::build(&mut self.trident, &mut self.fuzz_accounts);        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-34)         self.trident.execute_transaction(&mut ix, Some("Flow2"));    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-35)     }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-36)     #[flow(weight = 90)]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-37)     fn flow3(&mut self) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-38)         // This flow will be executed 40% of the time        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-39)         let mut ix = InitializeFnTransaction::build(&mut self.trident, &mut self.fuzz_accounts);        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-40)         self.trident.execute_transaction(&mut ix, Some("Flow3"));    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-41)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-42)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-43)     #[end]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-44)     fn cleanup(&mut self) -> Result<(), FuzzingError> {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-45)         // This method will be called after all flows have been executed        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-46)         Ok(())    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-47)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-48) } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-49)[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-50) fn main() {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-51)     FuzzTest::fuzz(1000, 100); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-52) }`
    
3.  Enable the regression test in the [Trident manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-metrics)
     by setting:
    
    `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-1-1) [fuzz.regression] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-1-2) enabled = true`
    
4.  Run the fuzz test to generate the regression test data.
    
5.  Run the same fuzz test with the same MASTER SEED on a different version of the program.
    
6.  Run the following command to compare the generated JSON files.
    

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.11.1/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-2-1) trident compare <path_to_json_file_1> <path_to_json_file_2>`

Back to top

---

# Installation - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/installation/#installation)

Installation[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/installation/#installation "Permanent link")

=======================================================================================================

Trident requires the following prerequisites:

Prerequisites

Before proceeding, ensure you have installed:

*   [Rust](https://www.rust-lang.org/tools/install)
     (stable version)
*   [Solana CLI](https://solana.com/docs/intro/installation)
    
*   [Anchor](https://www.anchor-lang.com/docs/installation)
    

Check out [supported versions](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/installation/#supported-versions)
 for version compatibility.

Install Trident[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/installation/#install-trident "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/installation/#__codelineno-0-1) cargo install trident-cli`

You can also use the `version` flag to install a specific version:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/installation/#__codelineno-1-1) cargo install trident-cli --version x.y.z`

Install cargo-llvm-cov[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/installation/#install-cargo-llvm-cov "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To enable code coverage tracking during fuzzing, install [cargo-llvm-cov](https://github.com/taiki-e/cargo-llvm-cov)
:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/installation/#__codelineno-2-1) cargo +stable install cargo-llvm-cov --locked`

Supported versions[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/installation/#supported-versions "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Version Table Legend

*   \= Develop branch
*   \= Released version
*   `-` = Not required/supported

| **Version Type** | **Anchor** | **Solana** | **Rust** | **Honggfuzz** | **AFL** |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Development | `>=0.29.0` | `>=1.17.3` | `1.86` | `-` | `-` |
| **Current (0.11.x)** | `>=0.29.0` | `>=1.17.3` | `1.86` | `-` | `-` |
| **0.10.x** | `>=0.29.0 < 0.31.0` | `>=1.17.3 < 2.1` | `nightly` | `0.5.56` | `0.15.11` |
| **0.9.x** | `>=0.29.0 < 0.31.0` | `>=1.17.3 < 2.1` | `nightly` | `0.5.56` | `0.15.11` |
| **0.8.x** | `0.30.1` | `^1.17.4` | `nightly` | `0.5.56` | `-` |
| **0.7.x** | `>=0.29.*` | `^1.17.4` | `nightly` | `0.5.56` | `-` |
| **0.6.x** | `>=0.29.*` | `^1.17` | `nightly` | `0.5.55` | `-` |
| **0.5.x** | `~0.28.*` | `=1.16.6` | `-` | `-` | `-` |
| **0.4.x** | `~0.27.*` | `>=1.15` | `-` | `-` | `-` |
| **0.3.x** | `~0.25.*` | `>=1.10` | `-` | `-` | `-` |
| **0.2.x** | `~0.24.*` | `>=1.9` | `-` | `-` | `-` |

# Installation - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/installation/#installation)

Installation[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/installation/#installation "Permanent link")

==========================================================================================================

Trident requires the following prerequisites:

Prerequisites

Before proceeding, ensure you have installed:

*   [Rust](https://www.rust-lang.org/tools/install)
     (stable version)
*   [Solana CLI](https://solana.com/docs/intro/installation)
    
*   [Anchor](https://www.anchor-lang.com/docs/installation)
    

Check out [supported versions](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/installation/#supported-versions)
 for version compatibility.

Install system dependencies[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/installation/#install-system-dependencies "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Update your package list:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/installation/#__codelineno-0-1) sudo apt update [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/installation/#__codelineno-0-2) sudo apt upgrade`

Install the required packages:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/installation/#__codelineno-1-1) sudo apt install build-essential [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/installation/#__codelineno-1-2) sudo apt-get install binutils-dev [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/installation/#__codelineno-1-3) sudo apt-get install libunwind-dev`

Install Trident[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/installation/#install-trident "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/installation/#__codelineno-2-1) cargo install trident-cli`

You can also use the `version` flag to install a specific version:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/installation/#__codelineno-3-1) cargo install trident-cli --version x.y.z`

Install Hongfuzz and AFL[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/installation/#install-hongfuzz-and-afl "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/installation/#__codelineno-4-1) cargo install honggfuzz [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/installation/#__codelineno-4-2) cargo install cargo-afl`

To install a specific version use the following commands:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/installation/#__codelineno-5-1) cargo install honggfuzz --version x.y.z [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/installation/#__codelineno-5-2) cargo install cargo-afl --version x.y.z`

Supported versions[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/installation/#supported-versions "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# Commands - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#commands)

Commands[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#commands "Permanent link")

===========================================================================================

Trident CLI supports the following commands:

`trident init`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#trident-init "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Initializes Trident Workspace and generates new Fuzz Test Template. Creates the following structure:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-1) project-root [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-2) ├── trident-tests [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-3) │   ├── fuzz_0 # particular fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-4) │   │   ├── instructions # instructions folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-5) │   │   ├── transactions # transactions folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-6) │   │   ├── test_fuzz.rs # the binary target of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-7) │   │   ├── types.rs # the types of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-8) │   │   └── fuzz_instructions.rs # the definition of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-9) │   ├── fuzz_1 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-10) │   ├── fuzz_X # possible multiple fuzz tests [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-11) │   ├── fuzzing # compilations and crashes folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-12) │   ├── Cargo.toml [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-13) │   └── Trident.toml # Configuration file located in trident-tests directory [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-14) └── ...`

#### Options[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#options "Permanent link")

*   `-f, --force` - Force Trident initialization. Trident dependencies will be updated based on the version of Trident CLI.
*   `-s, --skip-build` - Skip building the program before initializing Trident.
*   `-p, --program-name <FILE>` - Specify the name of the program for which fuzz test will be generated.
*   `-t, --test-name <NAME>` - Name of the fuzz test to initialize.

* * *

`trident how`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#trident-how "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Show the HowTo message about writing fuzz tests.

* * *

`trident fuzz`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#trident-fuzz "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Run fuzz subcommands. With fuzz subcommands you can add new fuzz test template or you can run fuzz test on already initialized one.

**Examples:**

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#__codelineno-1-1) trident fuzz add [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#__codelineno-1-2) trident fuzz run fuzz_0 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#__codelineno-1-3) trident fuzz debug <FUZZ_TARGET> <SEED>`

### `trident fuzz add`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#trident-fuzz-add "Permanent link")

Generate new Fuzz Test template.

#### Options[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#options_1 "Permanent link")

*   `-p, --program-name <FILE>` - Specify the name of the program for which the fuzz test will be generated.
*   `-t, --test-name <NAME>` - Name of the fuzz test to add.
*   `-s, --skip-build` - Skip building the program before adding new fuzz test.

* * *

### `trident fuzz run <fuzz_target>`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#trident-fuzz-run-fuzz_target "Permanent link")

Directory Note

Execute fuzz tests from the `trident-tests` directory.

Solana Logs

In case you want to see the logs of the fuzzed transactions, prefix the command with `TRIDENT_LOG=1`.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#__codelineno-2-1) TRIDENT_LOG=1 trident fuzz run <fuzz_target>`

Runs the specified Fuzz Target using Trident's Manually Guided Fuzzing (e.g., fuzz\_0).

#### Arguments[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#arguments "Permanent link")

*   `<fuzz_target>` - Name of the desired fuzz template to execute (for example fuzz\_0).
*   `[seed]` - Master seed used for fuzzing, if not provided it will be generated randomly.

#### Options[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#options_2 "Permanent link")

*   `-w, --with-exit-code` - Run the fuzzing with exit code, i.e. if it discovers crash the Trident will exit with exit code 1.

* * *

### `trident fuzz debug <fuzz_target> <seed>`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#trident-fuzz-debug-fuzz_target-seed "Permanent link")

Debug crashes by analyzing specific crash files using the provided seed.

#### Arguments[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#arguments_1 "Permanent link")

*   `<fuzz_target>` - Name of the desired fuzz template to execute (for example fuzz\_0).
*   `<seed>` - Master seed of the desired fuzz template to execute.

Debug Output

The debug output includes:

1.  Transaction logs
2.  Instruction data structures
3.  Panic/Crash information

* * *

`trident clean`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#trident-clean "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Clean build target, additionally perform `anchor clean`.

* * *

`trident server`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#trident-server "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Starts the Trident Server, in order to make it easier to visualize the fuzzing dashboard, more info in the [dashboard](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/)
 section.

* * *

`trident compare`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/#trident-compare "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Allows you to compare two fuzzing regression results. More info in the [regression](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/)
 section.

* * *

Back to top

---

# Commands - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#commands)

Commands[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#commands "Permanent link")

==============================================================================================

Trident CLI supports the following commands:

`trident init`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#trident-init "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Initializes Trident Workspace and generates new Fuzz Test Template. Creates the following structure:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-1) project-root [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-2) ├── trident-tests [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-3) │   ├── fuzz_0 # particular fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-4) │   │   ├── instructions # instructions folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-5) │   │   ├── transactions # transactions folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-6) │   │   ├── test_fuzz.rs # the binary target of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-7) │   │   ├── types.rs # the types of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-8) │   │   └── fuzz_instructions.rs # the definition of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-9) │   ├── fuzz_1 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-10) │   ├── fuzz_X # possible multiple fuzz tests [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-11) │   ├── fuzzing # compilations and crashes folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-12) │   └── Cargo.toml [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-13) ├── Trident.toml [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#__codelineno-0-14) └── ...`

#### Options[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#options "Permanent link")

*   `-f, --force` - Force Trident initialization. Updates Trident dependencies based on the CLI version.
*   `-p, --program-name <NAME>` - Specify the program name for which the fuzz test will be generated.
*   `-t, --test-name <NAME>` - Specify a custom name for the fuzz test to initialize.

* * *

`trident how`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#trident-how "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Print How To message about writing fuzz tests.

* * *

`trident fuzz`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#trident-fuzz "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Fuzzing-related commands with various subcommands:

### `trident fuzz run-afl <fuzz_target>`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#trident-fuzz-run-afl-fuzz_target "Permanent link")

Directory Note

Execute fuzz tests from the `trident-tests` directory.

Solana Logs

In case you want to see the logs of the fuzzed transactions, prefix the command with `TRIDENT_LOG=1`.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#__codelineno-1-1) TRIDENT_LOG=1 trident fuzz run-afl <fuzz_target>`

Runs AFL on the specified Fuzz Target (e.g., fuzz\_0).

* * *

### `trident fuzz run-hfuzz <fuzz_target>`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#trident-fuzz-run-hfuzz-fuzz_target "Permanent link")

Directory Note

Execute fuzz tests from the `trident-tests` directory.

Solana Logs

In case you want to see the logs of the fuzzed transactions, prefix the command with `TRIDENT_LOG=1`.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#__codelineno-2-1) TRIDENT_LOG=1 trident fuzz run-hfuzz <fuzz_target>`

Runs Honggfuzz on the specified Fuzz Target (e.g., fuzz\_0).

The output includes:

1.  **Iterations**: Number of fuzzing iterations completed
2.  **Mode**: Feedback Driven Mode - generates data based on coverage progress
3.  **Speed**: Average iterations per second
4.  **Crashes**: Number of detected crashes (panics or failed invariant checks)

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#__codelineno-3-1) ------------------------[  0 days 00 hrs 00 mins 01 secs ]----------------------   [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#__codelineno-3-2)   Iterations : 688 (out of: 1000 [68%])  [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#__codelineno-3-3)   Mode [3/3] : Feedback Driven Mode      [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#__codelineno-3-4)       Target : .../release/fuzz_0     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#__codelineno-3-5)      Threads : 16, CPUs: 32, CPU%: 1262% [39%/CPU]       [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#__codelineno-3-6)        Speed : 680/sec [avg: 688]     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#__codelineno-3-7)      Crashes : 1 [unique: 1, blocklist: 0, verified: 0]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#__codelineno-3-8)     Timeouts : 0 [10 sec] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#__codelineno-3-9)  Corpus Size : 98, max: 1048576 bytes, init: 0 files    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#__codelineno-3-10)     Coverage : edge: 10345/882951 [1%] pc: 163 cmp: 622547`

* * *

### `trident fuzz debug-afl <fuzz_target> <crash_file_path>`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#trident-fuzz-debug-afl-fuzz_target-crash_file_path "Permanent link")

Debug AFL crashes by analyzing specific crash files.

* * *

### `trident fuzz debug-hfuzz <fuzz_target> <crash_file_path>`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#trident-fuzz-debug-hfuzz-fuzz_target-crash_file_path "Permanent link")

Debug Honggfuzz crashes by analyzing specific crash files.

Debug Output

The debug output currently includes verbose lldb information. It shows:

1.  Transaction logs
2.  Instruction data structures
3.  Panic/Crash information

* * *

### `trident fuzz add`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#trident-fuzz-add "Permanent link")

Directory Note

This commands needs to be executed from the project root directory.

Adds a new Fuzz Test Template.

#### Options[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#options_1 "Permanent link")

*   `-p, --program-name <NAME>` - Specify the program name for which the fuzz test will be generated.
*   `-t, --test-name <NAME>` - Specify a custom name for the fuzz test to add.

* * *

`trident clean`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/#trident-clean "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Executes `anchor clean` and cleans Honggfuzz targets while preserving crashfiles and fuzzing inputs.

Back to top

# FAQ - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/faq/#faq)

FAQ[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/faq/#faq "Permanent link")

============================================================================

_Is Trident supported only with Anchor?_

*   Currently yes, Trident under the hood obtains data from the IDL generated by Anchor.

_I created the Fuzz Test, what should I do next?_

*   Start here [Start Fuzzing](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/)
    .

_Is Trident open-source?_

*   Yes, here [Trident](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident)
    .

_I would like to report an Issue with Trident, what should I do?_

*   Create [issue](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/issues)
    .

_Is Trident deployed on Mainnet / Devnet / Testnet?_

*   No, Trident is Fuzz Testing Framework, not Solana Program.

_What type of Fuzzer is Trident?_

*   Currently, we refer to it as _"coverage guided gray box fuzzer"_.

Back to top

---

# Changelog - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/CHANGELOG/#changelog)

Changelog[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/CHANGELOG/#changelog "Permanent link")

==============================================================================================

All notable changes to this project will be documented in this file.

The format is based on [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.0.0/)
, and this project adheres to [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html)
 (SemVer).

**Note**: Version 0 of Semantic Versioning is handled differently from version 1 and above. The minor version will be incremented upon a breaking change and the patch version will be incremented for features.

\[dev\] - Unreleased[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/CHANGELOG/#dev-unreleased "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

**Removed**

**Changed**

\[0.11.1\] - 2025-10-21[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/CHANGELOG/#0111-2025-10-21 "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

**Removed**

*   Removed lld linker ([394](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/394)
    )

**Changed**

\[0.11.0\] - 2025-08-14[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/CHANGELOG/#0110-2025-08-14 "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   Add server for displaying content of fuzzing artifacts ([347](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/347)
    )
*   Add fuzz artifacts directory to the fuzz test folder ([343](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/343)
    )
*   Added state monitoring support for fuzzing metrics ([341](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/341)
    )
*   Added dashboard support for fuzzing metrics ([340](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/340)
    )
*   Code coverage tracking support enabled and configured via Trident.toml. Coverage data can be visualized using the VS Code extension [330](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/330)
    
*   Added features to enable syscalls in fuzzing ([329](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/329)
    )
*   Add `--skip-build` flag to only initialize fuzz test without building the project ([325](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/325)
    )
*   Add support for space, lamports and owner to TridentAccounts macro ([320](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/320)
    )

**Removed**

**Changed**

*   FuzzTest fields are now aggregated into Trident struct ([339](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/339)
    )
*   Add support for reproducible fuzzing with thread-specific seeds ([332](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/332)
    )
*   Move Trident.toml into trident-tests folder ([328](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/328)
    )
*   Conversion from AFL and Honggfuzz into Manually Guided Fuzzing ([324](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/324)
    )
*   Update template generation to use tera ([326](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/326)
    )

\[0.10.0\] - 2025-03-13[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/CHANGELOG/#0100-2025-03-13 "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   TransactionSelector allows to select and execute random transaction with hooks and without hooks ([297](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/297)
    )
*   Added "random\_tail" attribute to TridentFlowExecutor macro to allow random tail generation ([296](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/296)
    )
*   Added support for seeds constraint for accounts structs ([284](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/284)
    )
*   Additional methods accessing the AccountsStorage and creating corresponding accounts are now optional ("token","vote", "stake") ([279](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/279)
    )
*   Derive macros now use own syn parser for better extensibility and UX ([275](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/275)
    )
*   Program ID inside test\_fuzz.rs file is now automatically filled in is present in the program IDL ([272](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/272)
    )
*   Added additional attributes to TridentAccounts, mut and signer ([268](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/268)
    )
*   Users can now specify a program for which they want to add or initialize a fuzz test using `--program-name` flag ([273](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/273)
    )
*   Allow custom test name specification in fuzz test creation with `--test-name` flag ([274](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/274)
    )

**Removed**

*   The DisplayIx macro is now removed, Debug trait was implemented for instruction inputs ([281](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/281)
    )

**Changed**

*   FuzzTestExecutor and FlowExecutor are grouped together and FuzzTest has client as generic instead of TridentSVM ([294](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/294)
    )
*   Changed Transaction sequence logic ([289](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/289)
    )
*   AccountsStorages are simplified, no types are required to define ([276](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/276)
    )
*   Trident Architecture changes containing multiple features and improvements (details in the PR)([267](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/267)
    )
*   get or create token account methods fixed for native token accounts ([262](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/262)
    )

*   feat/allow direct accounts manipulation and storage ([#142](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/142)
    )
*   feat/support of non-corresponding instruction and context names ([#130](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/130)
    )
*   feat/refactored and improved program flow during init and build, added activity indicator ([#129](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/129)
    )
*   feat/allow solana versions up to v1.17.\* and pin Rust 1.77 nightly compiler ([#128](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/128)
    )
*   feat/new init command option to initialize fuzz or poc tests only ([#124](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/124)
    )
*   feat/debug-mode detailed output ([#125](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/125)
    )

**Fixed**

*   fix/refactored fuzz test executor error handling ([#127](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/127)
    )
*   fix/warn user on composite accounts and continue fuzz test generation ([#133](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/133)
    )

    )

    )
*   fix/program client custom types ([#117](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/117)
    )
*   fix/check fuzz test name collision by checking the name against HashSet ([#114](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/114)
    )

\[0.5.0\] - 2023-08-28[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/CHANGELOG/#050-2023-08-28 "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   cli: Added trident subcommand `fuzz` to run and debug fuzz tests using honggfuzz-rs.
*   cli: Added trident `--skip-fuzzer` option for `init` subcommand to skip generation of fuzz test templates.
*   client: Added new Cargo feature `fuzzing` that enables optional dependencies related to fuzz testing.

\[0.4.1\] - 2023-08-21[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/CHANGELOG/#041-2023-08-21 "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Changed**

*   Upgrade Solana (`=1.16.6`) and Anchor framework (`=0.28.0`) versions.

**Fixed**

*   Implemented Anchor Client logic was not able to work with newer version of Anchor. Fixed with `async_rpc` and `async` feature.
*   Trident init IDL Parse Error on newer version of Rust, fixed with updated `accounts` token.

\[0.3.0\] - 2022-09-23[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/CHANGELOG/#030-2022-09-23 "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Changed**

*   Upgrade Solana (`~1.10`) and Anchor framework (`~0.25`) versions

**Added**

*   Custom Solana RPC error reporter. If the Solana RPC error is thrown, the error code, message and data (logs) are reported to the output.
*   Custom imports in the `.program_client`. User is able to import custom types and structures into program client. The import part of the code would not be re-generated.

\[0.2.0\] - 2022-07-27[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/CHANGELOG/#020-2022-07-27 "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   Trident is now configurable. This requires `Trident.toml` file to exist in the project's root directory - without this file the execution will fail. To solve this re-run `trident init` or just create an empty `Trident.toml` file in the project's root directory.

Back to top

---

# Commands - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#trident-init)

Commands
========

* * *

trident init[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#trident-init "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   This command Initializes Trident Workspace and generates new Fuzz Test Template.
    
*   The command will generate the following folder structure:
    
    `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-0-1) project-root [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-0-2) ├── trident-tests [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-0-3) │   ├── fuzz_tests # fuzz tests folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-0-4) │   │   ├── fuzz_0 # particular fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-0-5) │   │   │   ├── test_fuzz.rs # the binary target of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-0-6) │   │   │   └── fuzz_instructions.rs # the definition of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-0-7) │   │   ├── fuzz_1 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-0-8) │   │   ├── fuzz_X # possible multiple fuzz tests [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-0-9) │   │   ├── fuzzing # compilations and crashes folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-0-10) │   │   └── Cargo.toml [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-0-11) ├── Trident.toml [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-0-12) └── ...`
    

* * *

trident how[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#trident-how "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Print How To message about how to start writting fuzz tests.

* * *

trident fuzz[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#trident-fuzz "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Behavior depends on the subcommands.

### trident fuzz run-hfuzz[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#trident-fuzz-run-hfuzz "Permanent link")

*   Run Honggfuzz on the specified Fuzz Target (i.e. the Fuzz Template, for example fuzz\_0).

#### Output[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#output "Permanent link")

Important

The output provided by Honggfuzz is as follows:

1.  Number of Fuzzing Iterations.
2.  Feedback Driven Mode = Honggfuzz generates data based on the feedback (i.e. feedback based on Coverage progress).
3.  Average Iterations per second.
4.  Number of crashes it found (**panics** or failed **invariant checks**).

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-1-1) ------------------------[  0 days 00 hrs 00 mins 01 secs ]----------------------   [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-1-2)   Iterations : 688 (out of: 1000 [68%]) # -- 1. --  [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-1-3)   Mode [3/3] : Feedback Driven Mode # -- 2. --      [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-1-4)       Target : trident-tests/fuzz_tests/fuzzing.....wn-linux-gnu/release/fuzz_0     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-1-5)      Threads : 16, CPUs: 32, CPU%: 1262% [39%/CPU]       [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-1-6)        Speed : 680/sec [avg: 688] # -- 3. --     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-1-7)      Crashes : 1 [unique: 1, blocklist: 0, verified: 0] # -- 4. --    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-1-8)     Timeouts : 0 [10 sec] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-1-9)  Corpus Size : 98, max: 1048576 bytes, init: 0 files  [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-1-10)   Cov Update : 0 days 00 hrs 00 mins 00 secs ago    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-1-11)     Coverage : edge: 10345/882951 [1%] pc: 163 cmp: 622547 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-1-12) ---------------------------------- [ LOGS ] ------------------/ honggfuzz 2.6 /-`

### trident fuzz debug-hfuzz[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#trident-fuzz-debug-hfuzz "Permanent link")

*   Run Honggfuzz debug on the specified Fuzz Target (i.e. the Fuzz Template, for example fuzz\_0), with specified crash file, to see where the crash file found an issue.

#### Output[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#output_1 "Permanent link")

Important

The debug output is at current development stage really verbose and contains lldb parts. We are working on improving this experience. In the picture below you can see an example of provided debug output.

1.  Series of Transaction Logs
2.  Structures of data send within the Instructions
3.  **Panic** or **Crash**, based on if the Fuzzing panicked within the Solana Program or Invariant Check failed.

![alt text](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/images/run-debug.png)

### trident fuzz add[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#trident-fuzz-add "Permanent link")

*   Adds new Fuzz Test Template.

* * *

trident clean[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/commands/commands/#trident-clean "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Calls `anchor clean` and cleans targets created by the underlying Honggfuzz. Crashfiles and Fuzzing Inputs are preserved.

Back to top

---

# FAQ - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/faq/#faq)

FAQ[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/faq/#faq "Permanent link")

===============================================================================

_Is Trident supported only with Anchor?_

*   Currently yes, Trident under the hood obtains data from the IDL generated by Anchor.

_I created the Fuzz Test, what should I do next?_

*   Start here [Start Fuzzing](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/)
    .

_Is Trident open-source?_

*   Yes, here [Trident](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident)
    .

_I would like to report an Issue with Trident, what should I do?_

*   Create [issue](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/issues)
    .

_Is Trident deployed on Mainnet / Devnet / Testenet?_

*   No, Trident is Fuzz Testing Framework, not Solana Program.

_What type of Fuzzer is Trident?_

*   Currently, we refer to it as _"coverage guided gray box fuzzer"_.

Back to top

---

# Trident Features - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/features/#trident-features)

Trident Features[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/features/#trident-features "Permanent link")

===============================================================================================================

Trident contains multiple features to enhance the fuzzing experience and increase ability to discover bugs.

*   **AccountStorages**
    
    * * *
    
    Initialize, store and re-use random Accounts.
    
    [**AccountStorages**](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/account-storages/)
    
*   **FuzzInstructions**
    
    * * *
    
    All available Program Instructions as FuzzInstructions Variants.
    
    [**FuzzInstructions**](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/)
    
*   **Custom Instruction Sequences**
    
    * * *
    
    Specify Instruction Sequqnces you would like to executed instead of completely random execution order.
    
    [**Custom Instruction Sequences**](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/)
    
*   **Invariant Checks**
    
    * * *
    
    Allows to compare Account contents before and after the Instruction was successfully executed.
    
    [**Invariant Checks**](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/invariant-checks/)
    
*   **Genesis Accounts**
    
    * * *
    
    Specify genesis Accounts that will be included in the Fuzzing Environment. Use Mainnet Programs or dumped Accounts.
    
    [**Genesis**](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/)
    
*   **Fuzzing Statistics**
    
    * * *
    
    Show Fuzzing Statistics after the Fuzzing Session ended.
    
    [**Fuzzing Statistics**](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzzing-statistics/)
    
*   **Arbitrary Data**
    
    * * *
    
    Customize structure of Instruction Input arguments.
    
    [**Arbitrary Data**](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/)
    
*   **Trident Manifest**
    
    * * *
    
    Customize Fuzzing experience with the Trident Manifest.
    
    [**Trident Manifest**](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/)
    
*   **Custom Error Handlers**
    
    * * *
    
    Continue Instruction Sequence in case of Instruction Error was returned or specify custom behavior based on the returned error.
    
    [**Custom Error Handlers**](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/error-handlers/)
    

Back to top

---

# Changelog - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/CHANGELOG/#changelog)

Changelog[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/CHANGELOG/#changelog "Permanent link")

=================================================================================================

All notable changes to this project will be documented in this file.

The format is based on [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.0.0/)
, and this project adheres to [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html)
 (SemVer).

**Note**: Version 0 of Semantic Versioning is handled differently from version 1 and above. The minor version will be incremented upon a breaking change and the patch version will be incremented for features.

\[dev\] - Unreleased[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/CHANGELOG/#dev-unreleased "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

**Removed**

**Changed**

\[0.10.0\] - 2025-03-13[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/CHANGELOG/#0100-2025-03-13 "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   TransactionSelector allows to select and execute random transaction with hooks and without hooks ([297](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/297)
    )
*   Added "random\_tail" attribute to TridentFlowExecutor macro to allow random tail generation ([296](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/296)
    )
*   Added support for seeds constraint for accounts structs ([284](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/284)
    )
*   Additional methods accessing the AccountsStorage and creating corresponding accounts are now optional ("token","vote", "stake") ([279](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/279)
    )
*   Derive macros now use own syn parser for better extensibility and UX ([275](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/275)
    )
*   Program ID inside test\_fuzz.rs file is now automatically filled in is present in the program IDL ([272](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/272)
    )
*   Added additional attributes to TridentAccounts, mut and signer ([268](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/268)
    )
*   Users can now specify a program for which they want to add or initialize a fuzz test using `--program-name` flag ([273](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/273)
    )
*   Allow custom test name specification in fuzz test creation with `--test-name` flag ([274](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/274)
    )

**Removed**

*   The DisplayIx macro is now removed, Debug trait was implemented for instruction inputs ([281](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/281)
    )

**Changed**

*   FuzzTestExecutor and FlowExecutor are grouped together and FuzzTest has client as generic instead of TridentSVM ([294](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/294)
    )
*   Changed Transaction sequence logic ([289](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/289)
    )
*   AccountsStorages are simplified, no types are required to define ([276](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/276)
    )
*   Trident Architecture changes containing multiple features and improvements (details in the PR)([267](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/267)
    )
*   get or create token account methods fixed for native token accounts ([262](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/262)
    )

\[0.9.1\] - 2025-02-03[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/CHANGELOG/#091-2025-02-03 "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   added warp to time manipulation ([259](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/259)
    )
*   added methods to check if account storage is empty ([258](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/258)
    )
*   added support for post-instruction behavior ([257](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/257)
    )

**Removed**

**Changed**

\[0.9.0\] - 2025-01-15[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/CHANGELOG/#090-2025-01-15 "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   added support for composite accounts ([245](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/245)
    )
*   Trident SVM + AFL (see the PR for more details) ([234](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/234)
    )

**Removed**

*   removed fuzz\_iteration from test\_fuzz.rs ([243](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/243)
    )

**Changed**

*   renamed Config to TridentConfig ([246](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/246)
    )
*   errors are simplified and transaction error contains only transaction error ([244](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/244)
    )

\[0.8.1\] - 2024-11-14[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/CHANGELOG/#081-2024-11-14 "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Removed**

*   removed unnecesarry deserialization with AccountsSnapshots, to deserialize data implementation AccountDeserialize can be used ([221](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/221)
    )

**Changed**

*   improve AccountsStorage module structure and remove unnecessary methods in FuzzClient ([223](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/223)
    )
*   improve manipulations with AccountsStorages in get\_accounts() function ([219](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/219)
    )

**Added**

*   add pre\_sequence!, middle\_sequence! and post\_sequence! for easier sequence definition ([220](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/220)
    )
*   add/ add support for Clock sysvar manipulations with the client(i.e. warp to slot/epoch and forward in time) ([217](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/217)
    )

\[0.8.0\] - 2024-10-21[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/CHANGELOG/#080-2024-10-21 "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   impr/ allow to specify programs and accounts in the Trident Manifest ([207](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/207)
    )
*   impr/ added get\_program\_id function to the IxOps and FuzzTestExecutor ([199](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/199)
    )

**Changed**

*   impr/ improve init command, modify program manifest automatically, add init force, add howto subcommand ([208](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/208)
    )
*   impr/ allow to derive AccountsSnapshots for empty Account Context ([209](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/209)
    )
*   impr/ fuzz flags are read at start of fuzzing session from Config instead of env variable and transaction dispatch was added to increase FuzzTestExecutor readability ([204](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/204)
    )
*   impr/ allow various instructions to be generated in case of multiple programs in the Anchor workspace ([200](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/200)
    )
*   feat/ option to add account into Fuzz Test environment with base64 data ([197](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/197)
    )
*   impr/ instead of parsing source code and creating our IDL, read anchor IDL ([198](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/196)
    )

**Removed**

*   del/remove integration tests supported by Trident, this feature adds more unnecessary overhead compared to its value ([196](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/198)
    )

\[0.7.0\] - 2024-08-14[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/CHANGELOG/#070-2024-08-14 "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   impr/ add feature flag to the AccountsSnapshots macro ([183](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/183)
    )
*   feat/ add Support for CPI ([182](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/182)
    )
*   feat/ add option to initialize Trident with Macro/File (for Snapshots) option based on preference ([179](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/179)
    )
*   feat/create AccountsSnapshots derive macro for Snapshots creation ([#177](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/177)
    )
*   feat/fuzzing moved to separate crate trident-fuzz ([#175](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/175)
    )

\[0.5.0\] - 2023-08-28[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/CHANGELOG/#050-2023-08-28 "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   cli: Added trident subcommand `fuzz` to run and debug fuzz tests using honggfuzz-rs.
*   cli: Added trident `--skip-fuzzer` option for `init` subcommand to skip generation of fuzz test templates.
*   client: Added new Cargo feature `fuzzing` that enables optional dependencies related to fuzz testing.

\[0.4.1\] - 2023-08-21[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/CHANGELOG/#041-2023-08-21 "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Changed**

*   Upgrade Solana (`=1.16.6`) and Anchor framework (`=0.28.0`) versions.

**Fixed**

*   Implemented Anchor Client logic was not able to work with newer version of Anchor. Fixed with `async_rpc` and `async` feature.
*   Trident init IDL Parse Error on newer version of Rust, fixed with updated `accounts` token.

\[0.3.0\] - 2022-09-23[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/CHANGELOG/#030-2022-09-23 "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Changed**

*   Upgrade Solana (`~1.10`) and Anchor framework (`~0.25`) versions

**Added**

*   Custom Solana RPC error reporter. If the Solana RPC error is thrown, the error code, message and data (logs) are reported to the output.
*   Custom imports in the `.program_client`. User is able to import custom types and structures into program client. The import part of the code would not be re-generated.

\[0.2.0\] - 2022-07-27[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/CHANGELOG/#020-2022-07-27 "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   Trident is now configurable. This requires `Trident.toml` file to exist in the project's root directory - without this file the execution will fail. To solve this re-run `trident init` or just create an empty `Trident.toml` file in the project's root directory.
