# Writing fuzz test - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/#writing-fuzz-test)

Writing fuzz test[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/#writing-fuzz-test "Permanent link")

==============================================================================================================================

Trident is Manually Guided fuzzing framework for Solana programs.

In order to start fuzzing, you need to guide the fuzzer by specifying what are the expected inputs to instruction or the expected sequences of instructions to execute.

**Why is this important?**

Letting the fuzzer to generate completely random instruction inputs and completely random sequences of instruction would lead in most case

*   to transaction failures, which would mean the fuzzer is not properly fuzzing the logic within the program; and
*   executing irrelevant random instruction sequences, which would again lead to transaction failures.

Guide the fuzzer[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/#guide-the-fuzzer "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Start with properly configuring different types of instruction inputs:

*   [Instruction Data](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-data/)
    
*   [Instruction Accounts](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/)
    
*   [Fuzzing Flows](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/fuzzing-flows/)
    
*   (Optional) [Remaining Accounts](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/)
    

Back to top

---

# Executing the Fuzz Test - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#executing-the-fuzz-test)

Executing the Fuzz Test[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#executing-the-fuzz-test "Permanent link")

===========================================================================================================================================

To execute the fuzz test, navigate to the `trident-tests` directory and run the following command to execute the fuzz test:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-0-1) trident fuzz run <FUZZ_TARGET> <SEED> [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-0-2) # for example: [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-0-3) # trident fuzz run fuzz_0 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-0-4) # seed is optional, if not provided, a random seed will be used`

Directory Note

Execute fuzz tests from the `trident-tests` directory.

Solana Logs

In case you want to see the logs of the fuzzed transactions, prefix the command with `TRIDENT_LOG=1`.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-1-1) TRIDENT_LOG=1 trident fuzz run <fuzz_target> <seed>`

For the output reference and additional options such as debugging the found issues, check out [Commands](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/basics/commands/)
.

For the additional customization through the `trident.toml` file, check out the [Trident Manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/)
 page.

Back to top

---

# Writing fuzz test - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/#writing-fuzz-test)

Writing fuzz test[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/#writing-fuzz-test "Permanent link")

=================================================================================================================================

In order to start fuzzing, you need to guide the fuzzer to use correct and meaningful instruction inputs.

Trident generates random data for instruction executions. However, allowing the fuzzer to generate completely random account addresses would lead to numerous failed transactions, making the fuzzing process ineffective.

Each program instruction has a corresponding file in the instructions directory. Instructions consist of two main components:

*   Instruction Accounts
*   Instruction Data
*   (Optional) Remaining Accounts

Guide the Instruction Inputs[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/#guide-the-instruction-inputs "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Start with properly configuring different types of instruction inputs:

*   [Instruction Accounts](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-accounts/)
    
*   [Instruction Data](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/instruction-data/)
    
*   (Optional) [Remaining Accounts](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/writting-fuzz-test/remaining-accounts/)
    

Back to top

---

# FAQ - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/faq/faq/#faq)

FAQ[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/faq/faq/#faq "Permanent link")

===========================================================================

### Is Trident supported only with Anchor ?[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/faq/faq/#is-trident-supported-only-with-anchor "Permanent link")

*   Currently yes, Trident under the hood obtains data from the IDL generated by Anchor.

### I created the Fuzz Test what should I do next ?[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/faq/faq/#i-created-the-fuzz-test-what-should-i-do-next "Permanent link")

*   Start here [Writing Fuzz Tests](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/)
    . For additional features check [Features](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/features/)
    . If you are not sure about anything check [Get Help](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/get-help/get-help/)
    

### My program Instruction contains custom type such as Struct or Enum on its input, but it does not derive Arbitrary.[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/faq/faq/#my-program-instruction-contains-custom-type-such-as-struct-or-enum-on-its-input-but-it-does-not-derive-arbitrary "Permanent link")

*   In this case you need to specify same type in the Fuzz Test (with the same fields). And implement From Trait to convert to your type. Check [Custom Data Types](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#custom-data-types)
     or [Examples of Arbitrary](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/examples/examples/)
    .

### Is Trident open-source ?[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/faq/faq/#is-trident-open-source "Permanent link")

*   Yes, here [Trident](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident)
    

### I would like to report Issue with Trident, what should I do ?[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/faq/faq/#i-would-like-to-report-issue-with-trident-what-should-i-do "Permanent link")

*   Write Issue [Issues](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/issues)
    

### Is Trident deployed on Mainnet / Devnet / Testenet ?[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/faq/faq/#is-trident-deployed-on-mainnet-devnet-testenet "Permanent link")

*   No, Trident is Fuzz Testing Framework, not Solana Program.

### What type of Fuzzer Trident is ?[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/faq/faq/#what-type-of-fuzzer-trident-is "Permanent link")

*   Currently, we refer to it as _"coverage guided gray box fuzzer"_.

Back to top

---

# Executing the Fuzz Test - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#executing-the-fuzz-test)

Executing the Fuzz Test[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#executing-the-fuzz-test "Permanent link")

==============================================================================================================================================

To execute the fuzz test, navigate to the `trident-tests` directory and run the following command to execute the fuzz test using Honggfuzz:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-0-1) trident fuzz run-hfuzz <FUZZ_TARGET> [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-0-2) # for example: [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-0-3) # trident fuzz run-hfuzz fuzz_0`

To execute the fuzz test using AFL, run the following command:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-1-1) trident fuzz run-afl <FUZZ_TARGET> [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-1-2) # for example: [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-1-3) # trident fuzz run-afl fuzz_0`

Directory Note

Execute fuzz tests from the `trident-tests` directory.

Solana Logs

In case you want to see the logs of the fuzzed transactions, prefix the command with `TRIDENT_LOG=1`.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-2-1) TRIDENT_LOG=1 trident fuzz run-afl <fuzz_target> [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/start-fuzzing/executing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-2-2) TRIDENT_LOG=1 trident fuzz run-hfuzz <fuzz_target>`

For the output reference and additional options such as debugging the found issues, check out [Commands](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/basics/commands/)
.

Back to top

---

# Code Coverage - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/code-coverage/#code-coverage)

Code Coverage[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/code-coverage/#code-coverage "Permanent link")

====================================================================================================================

Trident's code coverage feature analyzes which parts of your Solana program are tested during fuzzing sessions, helping you identify untested code paths and improve test effectiveness.

 Your browser does not support the video tag.

Key features:

*   **Real-time Analysis**: Monitor coverage as fuzzing progresses
*   **Multiple Formats**: Generate reports in JSON and HTML formats
*   **VS Code Integration**: Visualize coverage directly in your IDE using [Solana VS Code extension](https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=AckeeBlockchain.solana)
    
*   **Detailed Reporting**: Get insights into line coverage, branch coverage, and execution paths

Gathering Coverage Data[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/code-coverage/#gathering-coverage-data "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Enable coverage in the [Trident manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-coverage)
    
2.  Deploy your program through the [entrypoint](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#entrypoint-deployment)
    
3.  Run the fuzz test

Viewing Coverage Reports[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/code-coverage/#viewing-coverage-reports "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You have two options for displaying coverage data: generate an HTML report for browser viewing, or generate a JSON report for VS Code integration.

### Live Coverage Updates[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/code-coverage/#live-coverage-updates "Permanent link")

For real-time coverage monitoring during fuzzing:

1.  Set `format = "json"` in the [Trident manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-coverage)
    
2.  Set `loopcount` to a value other than `0` e.g., `5` for frequent updates, for more info check out [Trident manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#entrypoint-deployment)
    
3.  Install the [Solana VS Code extension](https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=AckeeBlockchain.solana)
    
4.  Choose one of these options:
    *   **Automatic**: Set `attach_extension = true` in the [Trident manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-coverage)
         to automatically show live updates while the fuzz test is running
    *   **Manual**: Use the command `Solana: Show Code Coverage` and select the "Attach to active fuzzing session" option

### Post-Session Coverage Analysis[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/code-coverage/#post-session-coverage-analysis "Permanent link")

1.  Set `format = "json"` in the [Trident manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-coverage)
     before running the fuzz test
2.  Run the fuzz test
3.  Install the [Solana VS Code extension](https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=AckeeBlockchain.solana)
    
4.  Run the VS Code command `Solana: Show Code Coverage` and select the "Load generated JSON report" option

### HTML Report[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/code-coverage/#html-report "Permanent link")

1.  Set `format = "html"` in the [Trident manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-coverage)
     before running the fuzz test
2.  Run the fuzz test
3.  After the fuzz test finishes, the HTML report will be stored in the `<fuzz-test-name>-coverage-report` folder
4.  Open the HTML report in your browser

Back to top

---

# Trident's Fuzz Client - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/#tridents-fuzz-client)

Trident's Fuzz Client[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/#tridents-fuzz-client "Permanent link")

=============================================================================================================================================

Trident's Client (`FuzzClient`) is a wrapper around the [TridentSVM](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-svm/)
 that provides methods to manipulate with the execution environment during fuzzing.

This section describes the methods that are available in the `FuzzClient`.

Trident Client Methods[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/#trident-client-methods "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### `new_client`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/#new_client "Permanent link")

Creates a new instance of the fuzzing client with the specified programs and configuration.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/#__codelineno-0-1) fn new_client(programs: &[ProgramEntrypoint], config: &TridentConfig) -> Self`

* * *

### `deploy_native_program`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/#deploy_native_program "Permanent link")

Deploys a native program to the fuzzing client.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/#__codelineno-1-1) fn deploy_native_program(program: ProgramEntrypoint)`

* * *

### `get_sysvar`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/#get_sysvar "Permanent link")

Retrieves `Sysvars` like `Rent`, `Clock`, etc.

* * *

### `warp_to_epoch`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/#warp_to_epoch "Permanent link")

Advances the fuzz test to a specific epoch.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/#__codelineno-3-1) fn warp_to_epoch(warp_epoch: u64)`

* * *

### `warp_to_slot`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/#warp_to_slot "Permanent link")

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/#__codelineno-4-1) fn warp_to_slot(warp_slot: u64)`

* * *

### `warp_to_timestamp`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/#warp_to_timestamp "Permanent link")

Sets the fuzz test to a specific timestamp.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/#__codelineno-5-1) fn warp_to_timestamp(warp_timestamp: i64)`

* * *

### `forward_in_time`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/#forward_in_time "Permanent link")

Advances the fuzz test by the specified number of seconds.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/#__codelineno-6-1) fn forward_in_time(seconds: i64)`

* * *

### `set_account_custom`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/#set_account_custom "Permanent link")

Creates or overwrites an account at the specified address, bypassing normal runtime checks.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/#__codelineno-7-1) fn set_account_custom(address: &Pubkey, account: &AccountSharedData)`

* * *

### `get_account`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/#get_account "Permanent link")

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/#__codelineno-9-1) fn payer() -> Keypair`

* * *

### `clear_accounts`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/#clear_accounts "Permanent link")

Removes temporary accounts created during the fuzzing iteration.

Warning

This method is called internally by Trident (after each fuzzing iteration, to reset state to default).

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/#__codelineno-10-1) fn clear_accounts()`

* * *

Retrieves the most recent blockhash.

Warning

Currently, this method is not implemented and call to this method will result in a panic.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/#__codelineno-11-1) fn get_last_blockhash() -> Hash`

* * *

### `process_instructions`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/#process_instructions "Permanent link")

Executes a set of instructions and waits for them to be either finalized or rejected.

Warning

This method is called internally by Trident, no need for manual invocation.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-api-macro/trident-fuzz-client/#__codelineno-12-1) fn process_instructions(instructions: &[Instruction]) -> Result<(), TransactionError>`

# Dashboard - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#dashboard)

Dashboard[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#dashboard "Permanent link")

========================================================================================================

The Trident Dashboard provides a web-based interface for visualizing fuzzing session results through interactive charts and comprehensive statistics.

 Your browser does not support the video tag.

Features:

*   **Session Statistics**: View execution counts, success rates, and performance metrics
*   **Interactive Charts**: Explore results through dynamic visualizations
*   **Browser Access**: Open in any web browser without additional software
*   **Comprehensive Analysis**: Insights into instruction coverage and account interactions

Viewing the Dashboard[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#viewing-the-dashboard "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Open another terminal window and execute `trident server` from the fuzz-tests directory.
    
2.  Open your browser and navigate to the provided URL (typically `http://localhost:8080`).
    
3.  Enable the dashboard in the [Trident manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-metrics)
     by setting `dashboard = true`.
    
    `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-0-1) [fuzz.metrics] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-0-2) enabled = true [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-0-3) dashboard = true`
    
4.  Run the fuzz test to generate dashboard data.
    

Monitoring custom fuzzing metrics[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#monitoring-custom-fuzzing-metrics "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Trident allows you to monitor custom fuzzing metrics. If your program expects integer instruction inputs, it is possible to collect data on the randomly generated values and display them in the dashboard.

To do this, you need to add `trident.add_histogram_metric` to the `#[init]`, `#[flow]` or `#[end]` functions. The following code snippet shows how the `InitializeFnTransaction` instruction input is monitored; the statistics will be displayed in the dashboard.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-1) #[flow_executor] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-2) impl FuzzTest {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-3)     fn new() -> Self {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-4)         Self {            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-5)             trident: Trident::default(),            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-6)             fuzz_accounts: FuzzAccounts::default(),        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-7)         }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-8)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-9)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-10)     #[init]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-11)     fn start(&mut self) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-12)         let mut ix = InitializeFnTransaction::build(&mut self.trident, &mut self.fuzz_accounts); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-13)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-14)         self.trident.execute_transaction(&mut ix, Some("Init"));    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-15)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-16)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-17)     #[flow(weight = 5)]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-18)     fn flow1(&mut self) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-19)         let mut ix = InitializeFnTransaction::build(&mut self.trident, &mut self.fuzz_accounts);        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-20)         self.trident.execute_transaction(&mut ix, Some("Flow1")); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-21)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-22)         // Add the histogram metric to the dashboard        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-23)         self.trident            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-24)             .add_histogram_metric("flow1_metric", ix.instruction.data.input as f64);    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-25)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-26)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-27)     #[flow(weight = 5)]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-28)     fn flow2(&mut self) {      [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-29)       //....    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-30)     }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-31)     #[flow(weight = 90)]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-32)     fn flow3(&mut self) {      [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-33)       //....    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-34)     }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-35)     #[end]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-36)     fn cleanup(&mut self) -> Result<(), FuzzingError> {      [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-37)       //....    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-38)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/dashboard/#__codelineno-1-39) }`

# Regression testing - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#regression-testing)

Regression testing[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#regression-testing "Permanent link")

===========================================================================================================================

Regression testing is the process of re-running tests to ensure that previously working functionality still works after code changes.

Trident allows for regression testing by specifying which accounts should be included in the regression test, generating a JSON file format with all monitored state and providing a subcommand to compare two regression test results.

Regression test setup[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#regression-test-setup "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  First, decide which account(s) should be included in the regression test.
    
2.  Add the accounts for tracking, this can be done as shown in the following code snippet. Check the `add_to_regression` method.
    
    `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-1) #[flow_executor] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-2) impl FuzzTest {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-3)     fn new() -> Self {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-4)         Self {            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-5)             trident: Trident::default(),            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-6)             fuzz_accounts: FuzzAccounts::default(),        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-7)         }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-8)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-9)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-10)     #[init]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-11)     fn start(&mut self) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-12)         let mut ix = InitializeFnTransaction::build(&mut self.trident, &mut self.fuzz_accounts); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-13)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-14)         self.trident.execute_transaction(&mut ix, Some("Init")); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-15)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-16)         // Add the account to the regression test        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-17)         self.trident.add_to_regression(            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-18)             &ix.instruction.accounts.hello_world_account.pubkey(),            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-19)             "hello_world_account",        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-20)         );    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-21)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-22)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-23)     #[flow(weight = 5)]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-24)     fn flow1(&mut self) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-25)         // This flow will be executed 60% of the time        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-26)         let mut ix = InitializeFnTransaction::build(&mut self.trident, &mut self.fuzz_accounts);        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-27)         self.trident.execute_transaction(&mut ix, Some("Flow1"));    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-28)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-29)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-30)     #[flow(weight = 5)]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-31)     fn flow2(&mut self) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-32)         // This flow will be executed 40% of the time        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-33)         let mut ix = InitializeFnTransaction::build(&mut self.trident, &mut self.fuzz_accounts);        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-34)         self.trident.execute_transaction(&mut ix, Some("Flow2"));    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-35)     }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-36)     #[flow(weight = 90)]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-37)     fn flow3(&mut self) {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-38)         // This flow will be executed 40% of the time        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-39)         let mut ix = InitializeFnTransaction::build(&mut self.trident, &mut self.fuzz_accounts);        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-40)         self.trident.execute_transaction(&mut ix, Some("Flow3"));    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-41)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-42)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-43)     #[end]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-44)     fn cleanup(&mut self) -> Result<(), FuzzingError> {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-45)         // This method will be called after all flows have been executed        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-46)         Ok(())    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-47)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-48) } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-49)[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-50) fn main() {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-51)     FuzzTest::fuzz(1000, 100); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-0-52) }`
    
3.  Enable the regression test in the [Trident manifest](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-manifest/#fuzzing-metrics)
     by setting:
    
    `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-1-1) [fuzz.regression] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-1-2) enabled = true`
    
4.  Run the fuzz test to generate the regression test data.
    
5.  Run the same fuzz test with the same MASTER SEED on a different version of the program.
    
6.  Run the following command to compare the generated JSON files.
    

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/trident-advanced/regression/#__codelineno-2-1) trident compare <path_to_json_file_1> <path_to_json_file_2>`

Back to top

# Changelog - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/CHANGELOG/#changelog)

Changelog[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/CHANGELOG/#changelog "Permanent link")

=========================================================================================

All notable changes to this project will be documented in this file.

The format is based on [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.0.0/)
, and this project adheres to [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html)
 (SemVer).

**Note**: Version 0 of Semantic Versioning is handled differently from version 1 and above. The minor version will be incremented upon a breaking change and the patch version will be incremented for features.

\[dev\] - Unreleased[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/CHANGELOG/#dev-unreleased "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

\[0.8.1\] - 2024-11-14[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/CHANGELOG/#081-2024-11-14 "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Removed**

*   removed unnecesarry deserialization with AccountsSnapshots, to deserialize data implementation AccountDeserialize can be used ([221](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/221)
    )

**Changed**

*   improve AccountsStorage module structure and remove unnecessary methods in FuzzClient ([223](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/223)
    )
*   improve manipulations with AccountsStorages in get\_accounts() function ([219](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/219)
    )

**Added**

*   add pre\_sequence!, middle\_sequence! and post\_sequence! for easier sequence definition ([220](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/220)
    )
*   add/ add support for Clock sysvar manipulations with the client(i.e. warp to slot/epoch and forward in time) ([217](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/217)
    )

\[0.8.0\] - 2024-10-21[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/CHANGELOG/#080-2024-10-21 "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   impr/ allow to specify programs and accounts in the Trident Manifest ([207](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/207)
    )
*   impr/ added get\_program\_id function to the IxOps and FuzzTestExecutor ([199](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/199)
    )

**Changed**

*   impr/ improve init command, modify program manifest automatically, add init force, add howto subcommand ([208](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/208)
    )
*   impr/ allow to derive AccountsSnapshots for empty Account Context ([209](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/209)
    )
*   impr/ fuzz flags are read at start of fuzzing session from Config instead of env variable and transaction dispatch was added to increase FuzzTestExecutor readability ([204](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/204)
    )
*   impr/ allow various instructions to be generated in case of multiple programs in the Anchor workspace ([200](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/200)
    )
*   feat/ option to add account into Fuzz Test environment with base64 data ([197](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/197)
    )
*   impr/ instead of parsing source code and creating our IDL, read anchor IDL ([198](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/196)
    )

**Removed**

*   del/remove integration tests supported by Trident, this feature adds more unnecessary overhead compared to its value ([196](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/198)
    )

\[0.7.0\] - 2024-08-14[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/CHANGELOG/#070-2024-08-14 "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   impr/ add feature flag to the AccountsSnapshots macro ([183](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/183)
    )
*   feat/ add Support for CPI ([182](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/182)
    )
*   feat/ add option to initialize Trident with Macro/File (for Snapshots) option based on preference ([179](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/179)
    )

\[0.5.0\] - 2023-08-28[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/CHANGELOG/#050-2023-08-28 "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   cli: Added trident subcommand `fuzz` to run and debug fuzz tests using honggfuzz-rs.
*   cli: Added trident `--skip-fuzzer` option for `init` subcommand to skip generation of fuzz test templates.
*   client: Added new Cargo feature `fuzzing` that enables optional dependencies related to fuzz testing.

\[0.4.1\] - 2023-08-21[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/CHANGELOG/#041-2023-08-21 "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Changed**

*   Upgrade Solana (`=1.16.6`) and Anchor framework (`=0.28.0`) versions.

**Fixed**

*   Implemented Anchor Client logic was not able to work with newer version of Anchor. Fixed with `async_rpc` and `async` feature.
*   Trident init IDL Parse Error on newer version of Rust, fixed with updated `accounts` token.

\[0.3.0\] - 2022-09-23[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/CHANGELOG/#030-2022-09-23 "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Changed**

*   Upgrade Solana (`~1.10`) and Anchor framework (`~0.25`) versions

**Added**

*   Custom Solana RPC error reporter. If the Solana RPC error is thrown, the error code, message and data (logs) are reported to the output.
*   Custom imports in the `.program_client`. User is able to import custom types and structures into program client. The import part of the code would not be re-generated.

\[0.2.0\] - 2022-07-27[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/CHANGELOG/#020-2022-07-27 "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   Trident is now configurable. This requires `Trident.toml` file to exist in the project's root directory - without this file the execution will fail. To solve this re-run `trident init` or just create an empty `Trident.toml` file in the project's root directory.

Back to top

# General Configuration - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/general/#general-configuration)

General Configuration[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/general/#general-configuration "Permanent link")

=================================================================================================================================

`programs`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/general/#programs "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Use dumped program from desired cluster, during fuzzing.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/general/#__codelineno-0-1) [[fuzz.programs]] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/general/#__codelineno-0-2) address = "metaqbxxUerdq28cj1RbAWkYQm3ybzjb6a8bt518x1s" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/general/#__codelineno-0-3) program = "metaplex-program/metaplex-token-metadata.so"`

* * *

`accounts`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/general/#accounts "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Use dumped accounts from desired cluster, during fuzzing.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/general/#__codelineno-1-1) [[fuzz.accounts]] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/general/#__codelineno-1-2) address = "6YG3J7PaxyMnnbU67ifyrgF3BzNzc7cD8hPkqK6ATweE" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/general/#__codelineno-1-3) filename = "tests/accounts/core_bridge_mainnet/guardian_set_5_mock.json"`

* * *

`fuzzing_with_stats`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/general/#fuzzing_with_stats "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Trident will show statistics after the fuzzing session. This option forces use of honggfuzz parameter `keep_output` as true in order to be able to catch fuzzer stdout.

`(default: false)`

Statistics Support Limitation

Fuzzing with stats is currently not supported with `AFL`.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/general/#__codelineno-2-1) [fuzz] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/general/#__codelineno-2-2) fuzzing_with_stats = true`

* * *

`allow_duplicate_txs`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/general/#allow_duplicate_txs "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Allow processing of duplicate transactions. Setting to true might speed up fuzzing but can cause false positive crashes.

`(default: false)`

Transaction Validity Check

With swtich from `ProgramTest` to `TridentSVM`, there is no check for the transactions validity, so this check currently does nothing.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/general/#__codelineno-3-1) [fuzz] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/general/#__codelineno-3-2) allow_duplicate_txs = false`

Back to top

# AFL Configuration - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/afl/#afl-configuration)

AFL Configuration[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/afl/#afl-configuration "Permanent link")

=====================================================================================================================

`run_time`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/afl/#run_time "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Number of seconds this fuzzing session will last.

`(default: 0 [no limit])`

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/afl/#__codelineno-0-1) [afl] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/afl/#__codelineno-0-2) run_time = 0`

* * *

`iterations`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/afl/#iterations "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Number of fuzzing iterations.

`(default: 0 [no limit])`

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/afl/#__codelineno-1-1) [afl] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/afl/#__codelineno-1-2) iterations = 0`

* * *

`cargo_target_dir`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/afl/#cargo_target_dir "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Target compilation directory, to not clash with cargo build's default target directory.

`(default: "" ["trident-tests/fuzz_tests/fuzzing/afl/afl_target"])`

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/afl/#__codelineno-2-1) [afl] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/afl/#__codelineno-2-2) cargo_target_dir = ""`

* * *

`afl_workspace_in`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/afl/#afl_workspace_in "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   AFL working input directory.

`(default: "" ["trident-tests/fuzz_tests/fuzzing/afl/afl_workspace/in"])`

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/afl/#__codelineno-3-1) [afl] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/afl/#__codelineno-3-2) afl_workspace_in = ""`

* * *

`afl_workspace_out`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/afl/#afl_workspace_out "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   AFL working output directory.

`(default: "" ["trident-tests/fuzz_tests/fuzzing/afl/afl_workspace/out"])`

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/afl/#__codelineno-4-1) [afl] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/afl/#__codelineno-4-2) afl_workspace_out = ""`

* * *

`seeds`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/afl/#seeds "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Predefined inputs to the AFL. You can specify multiple input seeds.

Seed Generation Priority

`bytes_count` has precedence before `seed`, in that case if both are specified. Seed is generated as random array of `bytes_count` bytes.

*   `file_name`
    
    *   Filename under which the test input is generated, the location of file is `afl_workspace_in` directory.
    
    `(default: "" ["trident-seed"])`
    
*   `seed`
    
    *   String used as seed.
    
    `(default: "" ["trident"])`
    
*   `override_file`
    
    *   If the file already exists at specific location, select if override.
    
    `(default: false)`
    
*   `bytes_count`
    
    *   Number of randomly generated bytes.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/afl/#__codelineno-5-1) [[afl.seeds]] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/afl/#__codelineno-5-2) file_name = "" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/afl/#__codelineno-5-3) seed = "" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/afl/#__codelineno-5-4) override_file = true [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.10.0/trident-manifest/afl/#__codelineno-5-5) bytes_count = 20`

Back to top

# Fuzzing Statistics - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzzing-statistics/#fuzzing-statistics)

Fuzzing Statistics[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzzing-statistics/#fuzzing-statistics "Permanent link")

=============================================================================================================================

Trident allows you to see statistics after the fuzzing session ended.

Important

In order to show statistics set `fuzzing_with_stats` within the `Trident.toml` to `true`.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzzing-statistics/#__codelineno-0-1) [fuzz] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzzing-statistics/#__codelineno-0-2) # ... [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzzing-statistics/#__codelineno-0-3) fuzzing_with_stats = true [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzzing-statistics/#__codelineno-0-4) # ...`

Available Statistics[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzzing-statistics/#available-statistics "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Simple[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzzing-statistics/#simple "Permanent link")

*   Number of invocations of each instruction during the fuzzing session.
*   Number of successful invocations of each instruction during the fuzzing session.
*   Number of failed invariants checks for each instruction during the fuzzing session.

Note

Keep in mind that the number of fuzz iterations does not directly correspond to the total number of invocations. In one fuzz iteration, the fuzzer might be unable to deserialize fuzz data into instructions, causing the entire iteration to be skipped.

On the other hand this is expected behavior as the underlying data are randomly (with coverage feedback) generated, so the Honggfuzz will not necessarily find appropriate data each iteration.

Tip

Consider checking the [Examples](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/examples/examples/)
 section for more tips.

Back to top

---

# Invariant Checks - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/invariant-checks/#invariant-checks)

Invariant Checks[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/invariant-checks/#invariant-checks "Permanent link")

=======================================================================================================================

Trident allows you to (optionally) specify Invariant Checks for each Instruction.

The Invariant Check will be called after the Instruction was successfully invoked. Within the Invariant Check you can compare the contents of Accounts before and after the Instruction was called.

Important

Returning error in the Invariant Check is considered as detected undesired behavior (i.e. issue/crash detected).

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-1) fn check(     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-2)     &self,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-3)     _pre_ix: &[SnapshotAccount],    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-4)     post_ix: &[SnapshotAccount],    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-5)     _ix_data: Self::IxData, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-6) ) -> Result<(), FuzzingError> {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-7)     if let Ok(hello_world_account) =        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-8)         hello_world::StoreHelloWorld::try_deserialize(&mut post_ix[1].data())    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-9)     {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-10)         if hello_world_account.input == 253 {            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-11)             return Err(FuzzingError::Custom(1));        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-12)         }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-13)     }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-14)     Ok(()) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-15) }`

Important

Order of accounts within the array is the same as the order of accounts on the instruction input of your program.

Account Deserialization[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/invariant-checks/#account-deserialization "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `SnapshotAccount` provides methods to obtain parts of the account (e.g. address, its data, owner etc.). If you want to deserialize data into struct defined within your program (or within for example `anchor-spl`), you can use approach from source code above, meaning utilze `try_deserialize` generated by anchor within your program.

Tip

Consider checking the [Examples](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/examples/examples/)
 section for more tips.

Back to top

---

# Instructions Sequences - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#instructions-sequences)

Instructions Sequences[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#instructions-sequences "Permanent link")

=========================================================================================================================================

Trident allows you to specify **custom Instruction squences** you would like to execute.

Possible Instruction sequences are split into 3 parts

*   **pre-Instructions**
*   **Instructions**
*   **post-Instructions**

For example if you program always needs to start with some kind of Initialization instruction, you can specify this Initialize Instruction using the `pre_sequence()` macro as shown in the source code below.

``[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-1) // test_fuzz.rs [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-2)[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-3) /// ... [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-4)[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-5) struct InstructionsSequence; [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-6) /// Define instruction sequences for invocation. [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-7) /// `pre` runs at the start, `middle` in the middle, and `post` at the end. [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-8) /// For example, to call `InitializeFn`, `UpdateFn` and then `WithdrawFn` during [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-9) /// each fuzzing iteration: [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-10) /// ``` [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-11) /// impl FuzzDataBuilder<FuzzInstruction> for InstructionsSequence { [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-12) ///     pre_sequence!(InitializeFn,UpdateFn); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-13) ///     middle_sequence!(WithdrawFn); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-14) ///} [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-15) /// ``` [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-16) /// For more details, see: https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/features/instructions-sequences/#instructions-sequences [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-17) impl FuzzDataBuilder<FuzzInstruction> for InstructionsSequence {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-18)     pre_sequence!(InitializeFn);    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-19)     middle_sequence!();    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-20)     post_sequence!(); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-21) } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-22)[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-23) /// ...``

Tip

*   The arguments to the macro are variants of `FuzzInstruction` specified in `fuzz_instructions.rs`.
*   Empty macro parameters (such as `middle_sequence!()`), will skip that section, meaning no instructions will be executed during the section.
*   If no macro is defined for a section, a random instruction sequence will be generated for the section.

Manual trait override[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#manual-trait-override "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

It is not necessary to use the macro as explained above. The trait implementation (i.e., the methods) can be implemented manually, as shown in the code below. This approach allows for greater customization if needed. The rules are the same as described above.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-1) // test_fuzz.rs [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-2)[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-3) // do not forget to include the required structures [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-4) use fuzz_instructions::InitVesting; [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-5) use fuzz_instructions::WithdrawUnlocked; [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-6)[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-7) impl FuzzDataBuilder<FuzzInstruction> for MyFuzzData {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-8)     fn pre_ixs(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-9)         u: &mut arbitrary::Unstructured    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-10)     ) -> arbitrary::Result<Vec<FuzzInstruction>> {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-11)         let init_ix =            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-12)             FuzzInstruction::InitVesting(InitVesting::arbitrary(u)?); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-13)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-14)         Ok(vec![init_ix])    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-15)     }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-16)     fn ixs(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-17)         u: &mut arbitrary::Unstructured    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-18)     ) -> arbitrary::Result<Vec<FuzzInstruction>> {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-19)         let withdraw_ix =            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-20)             FuzzInstruction::WithdrawUnlocked(WithdrawUnlocked::arbitrary(u)?); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-21)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-22)         Ok(vec![withdraw_ix])    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-23)     }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-24)     fn post_ixs(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-25)         _u: &mut arbitrary::Unstructured    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-26)     ) -> arbitrary::Result<Vec<FuzzInstruction>> {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-27)         Ok(vec![])    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-28)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-29) }`

Tip

Consider checking the [Examples](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/examples/examples/)
 section for more tips.

# Genesis - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#genesis)

Genesis[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#genesis "Permanent link")

=====================================================================================================

Genesis Programs[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#genesis-programs "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Trident allows you to use Cross Program Invocation of both Native and SBF programs.

### Native[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#native "Permanent link")

In case of multiple programs within the Anchor Workspace. Make sure that all of the programs you would like to call Cross Program Invocation to are included in the initial state of the Fuzz Test Environment.

Important

Source code below:

*   `fuzzing_program_callee` is included in the `ProgramTestClientBlocking`
*   `fuzzing_program_caller` is included in the `ProgramTestClientBlocking`

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-0-1) // test_fuzz.rs [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-0-2)[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-0-3) fn fuzz_iteration<T: FuzzTestExecutor<U> + std::fmt::Display, U>(     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-0-4)     fuzz_data: FuzzData<T, U> [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-0-5) ) {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-0-6)     let fuzzing_program_callee = FuzzingProgram::new(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-0-7)         PROGRAM_NAME_CALLEE,        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-0-8)         &PROGRAM_ID_CALLEE,        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-0-9)         processor!(convert_entry!(entry_callee)),    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-0-10)     ); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-0-11)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-0-12)     let fuzzing_program_caller = FuzzingProgram::new(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-0-13)         PROGRAM_NAME_CALLER,        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-0-14)         &PROGRAM_ID_CALLER,        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-0-15)         processor!(convert_entry!(entry_caller)),    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-0-16)     ); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-0-17)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-0-18)     let mut client =        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-0-19)         ProgramTestClientBlocking::new(            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-0-20)             &[fuzzing_program_callee, fuzzing_program_caller],            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-0-21)             &[]        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-0-22)         ).unwrap(); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-0-23)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-0-24)     let _ = fuzz_data.run_with_runtime(&mut client); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-0-25) }`

### SBF[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#sbf "Permanent link")

In case of SBF targets, compiled or dumped from whatever cluster. You can also use these within the Fuzz Tests.

Tip

If you want to obtain Program from Mainnet use

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-1-1) # -u m specifies to dump from mainnet [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-1-2) solana program dump -u m <PROGRAM_ID> <PROGRAM_NAME>.so`

Important

*   To include the SBF target in the Fuzz Test for CPI, specify address and path to the program in the `Trident.toml`.
    
*   Including these types of programs will lead to performance decline of Trident.
    

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-2-1) [[fuzz.programs]] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-2-2) address = "metaqbxxUerdq28cj1RbAWkYQm3ybzjb6a8bt518x1s" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-2-3) program = "metaplex-program/metaplex-token-metadata.so"`

Genesis Accounts[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#genesis-accounts "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Trident allows you to include Accounts with data in base64 format.

Tip

If you want to obtain Account with `base64` data format, use

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-3-1) # -u m specifies to dump from mainnet [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-3-2) solana account -u m <ADDRESS> --output json`

Important

To include desired accounts in the fuzz testing environment, add then using the `Trident.toml`.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-4-1) [[fuzz.accounts]] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-4-2) address = "6YG3J7PaxyMnnbU67ifyrgF3BzNzc7cD8hPkqK6ATweE" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/genesis-accounts/#__codelineno-4-3) filename = "tests/accounts/core_bridge_mainnet/guardian_set_5_mock.json"`

Tip

Consider checking the [Examples](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/examples/examples/)
 section for more tips.

Back to top

# Error Handler - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/error-handlers/#error-handler)

Error Handler[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/error-handlers/#error-handler "Permanent link")

===============================================================================================================

Trident allows you to specify custom error handler for each Instruction.

This can be particularly helpful:

*   If Transaction returns Error, you can specify to omit this error and continue with the fuzzing instruction.
*   Using the `tx_error_handler` you can check if the error returned is desired based on the Accounts and Input data that were used.

Tip

The default behavior of the function is that the error is returned.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-0-1) /// default implementation [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-0-2) fn tx_error_handler(     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-0-3)     &self,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-0-4)     e: FuzzClientErrorWithOrigin,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-0-5)     ix_data: Self::IxData,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-0-6)     pre_ix_acc_infos: &[SnapshotAccount],, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-0-7) ) -> Result<(), FuzzClientErrorWithOrigin> {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-0-8)     Err(e) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-0-9) }`

To omit the Error and continue with the next Instruction in the iteration, you can do

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-1-1) /// default implementation [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-1-2) fn tx_error_handler(     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-1-3)     &self,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-1-4)     e: FuzzClientErrorWithOrigin,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-1-5)     ix_data: Self::IxData,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-1-6)     pre_ix_acc_infos: &'info mut [Option<AccountInfo<'info>>], [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-1-7) ) -> Result<(), FuzzClientErrorWithOrigin> {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-1-8)     Ok(()) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-1-9) }`

Back to top
