# Fuzz Instructions - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#fuzz-instructions)

Fuzz Instructions[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#fuzz-instructions "Permanent link")

==========================================================================================================================

Trident defines `FuzzInstruction` enum containing all available **Instructions** within your program.

The enum variants additionally contains their corresponding structures for **Accounts** and **Input** arguments.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-1) #[derive(Arbitrary, DisplayIx, FuzzTestExecutor, FuzzDeserialize)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-2) pub enum FuzzInstruction {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-3)     Initialize(Initialize),    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-4)     Update(Update), [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-5) } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-6) #[derive(Arbitrary, Debug)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-7) pub struct Initialize {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-8)     pub accounts: InitializeAccounts,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-9)     pub data: InitializeData, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-10) } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-11) #[derive(Arbitrary, Debug)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-12) pub struct Update {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-13)     pub accounts: UpdateAccounts,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-14)     pub data: UpdateData, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-15) } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-16) // ...`

Instruction behavior[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#instruction-behavior "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each Instruction variant has to define `IxOps` trait containing the following methods:

*   [`get_program_id()`](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#get_program_id)
     (automatically implemented)
*   [`get_data()`](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#get_data)
     (required)
*   [`get_accounts()`](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#get_accounts)
     (required)
*   [`check()`](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#check)
     (optional)
*   [`tx_error_handler()`](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#tx_error_handler)
     (optional)
*   `deserialize_accounts()` (automatically implemented)

`get_program_id()`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#get_program_id "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This method specifies **program ID** to which the Instruction corresponds.

In case you have only one program in the Anchor Workspace it is not really important. The importance occurs when you have multiple programs in the Workspace and you want to call Instructions of every Program. In that case each Instruction Variant corresponds to its program by the Program ID.

`get_data()`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#get_data "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This method specifies what the Instruction Input Data should look like. You can use completely random data generated by the fuzzer, such as:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-1-1) fn get_data(     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-1-2)     &self,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-1-3)     _client: &mut impl FuzzClient,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-1-4)     _fuzz_accounts: &mut FuzzAccounts, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-1-5) ) -> Result<Self::IxData, FuzzingError> {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-1-6)     let data = hello_world::instruction::InitializeFn {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-1-7)         input: self.data.input,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-1-8)     };    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-1-9)     Ok(data) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-1-10) }`

You can also use always constant values

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-2-1) fn get_data(     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-2-2)     &self,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-2-3)     _client: &mut impl FuzzClient,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-2-4)     _fuzz_accounts: &mut FuzzAccounts, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-2-5) ) -> Result<Self::IxData, FuzzingError> {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-2-6)     let data = hello_world::instruction::InitializeFn {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-2-7)         input: 5,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-2-8)     };    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-2-9)     Ok(data) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-2-10) }`

Or you can customize the Data using the Arbitrary crate. Check [Arbitrary Data](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/)
.

### Custom Data Types[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#custom-data-types "Permanent link")

If you use Custom Types as Instruction data arguments, you may encounter a problem that the Custom Type does not implement

*   [Debug](https://doc.rust-lang.org/std/fmt/trait.Debug.html)
     trait
*   [Arbitrary](https://docs.rs/arbitrary/latest/arbitrary/trait.Arbitrary.html)
     trait

### Derive Debug and Arbitrary traits inside the Fuzz Test[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#derive-debug-and-arbitrary-traits-inside-the-fuzz-test "Permanent link")

You can redefine the custom type within the `fuzz_instructions.rs` file, along with all the necessary traits.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-3-1) // Redefine the Custom Type inside the fuzz_instructions.rs, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-3-2) // but this time with all of the required traits. [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-3-3) #[derive(Arbitrary,Debug, Clone, Copy)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-3-4) pub enum CustomEnumInputFuzz {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-3-5)     InputVariant1,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-3-6)     InputVariant2,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-3-7)     InputVariant3, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-3-8) }`

Then, you would also need to implement the [`std::convert::From<T>`](https://doc.rust-lang.org/std/convert/trait.From.html)
 trait to enable conversion between the newly defined Custom Type and the Custom Type used within your program.

Tip

Consider checking the [Examples](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/examples/examples/)
 section for more tips.

`get_accounts()`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#get_accounts "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This method specifies how the **Accounts** for the corresponding Instruction should be resolved. You can use accounts stored within the **FuzzAccounts Account Storages**, or you can define custom Account using the **client**.

There are two main functions to use within the `get_accounts()`:

*   [`get_or_create_account()`](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#get_or_create_account)
    
*   [`get()`](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#get)
    
*   [`set_custom()`](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#set_custom)
    

### `get_or_create_account()`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#get_or_create_account "Permanent link")

Insert a new record into AccountsStorage based on the `account_id`. If a record with the entered `account_id` already exists, it is returned, and no insertion is performed.

Tip

*   This function is particularly useful for instructions that initialize accounts.

Example:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-4-1) let hello_world_account = fuzz_accounts.hello_world_account.get_or_create_account(     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-4-2)     self.accounts.hello_world_account,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-4-3)     client,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-4-4)     &[b"hello_world_seed"],    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-4-5)     &hello_world::ID, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-4-6) );`

The code above will return the PDA from `hello_world`'s AccountsStorage if a record for the entered `account_id` exists. If not, the function will create a new record corresponding to the PDA derived from the provided seeds and return the PDA.

### `get()`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#get "Permanent link")

Retrieves a record from AccountsStorage based on the entered `account_id`. If no record exists for the `account_id`, a random public key is returned.

Tip

*   This function is particularly useful for instructions other than those that perform initialization.
    
    Example:
    

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-5-1) let hello_world_account = fuzz_accounts         [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-5-2)         .hello_world_account        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-5-3)         .get(self.accounts.hello_world_account);`

The code above will return the PDA from `hello_world`'s AccountsStorage if a record for the entered `account_id` exists. If not, the function will return a random public key.

### `set_custom()`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#set_custom "Permanent link")

If the previous two functions are insufficient, you can use `set_custom()` to manually set an account with data you select. This function accepts `account_id`, which specifies the record in the corresponding AccountsStorage; `client`, which handles the insertion of AccountSharedData; the account's `address` (particularly helpful if a predefined address is needed); and `AccountSharedData`, which you can configure as needed.

Tip

`Example:`

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-6-1) let address = Keypair::new(); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-6-2) fuzz_accounts.hello_world_account.set_custom(     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-6-3)     self.accounts.hello_world_account,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-6-4)     client,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-6-5)     address.pubkey(),    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-6-6)     AccountSharedData::new(10 * LAMPORTS_PER_SOL, 0, &solana_sdk::system_program::ID), [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-6-7) );`

The code above will generate a new random keypair. The `set_account` function will insert the specified `AccountSharedData` into the client and create a record in the corresponding AccountsStorage based on the entered `account_id`.

`check()`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#check "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This method provides Invariant Check for the corresponding Instruction. Check [Invariant Checks](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/invariant-checks/)
.

`tx_error_handler()`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#tx_error_handler "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This method provides Tx Error Handler for the corresponding Instruction. Check [Error Handler](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/error-handlers/)
.

Example[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#example "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Tip

Consider checking the [Examples](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/examples/examples/)
 section for more tips.

# Current limitations - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/limitations/#current-limitations)

Current limitations[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/limitations/#current-limitations "Permanent link")

========================================================================================================================

This section summarizes some known limitations in the current development stage. Further development will be focused on resolving these limitations.

*   Remaining accounts in check methods are not supported.
*   Composite accounts are not supported.

# Arbitrary Data - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#arbitrary-data)

Arbitrary Data[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#arbitrary-data "Permanent link")

=================================================================================================================

Trident allows you to customize Instruction Data to provide structure.

For example your Initialize Instruction expects two arguments `start_at` and `end_at` you know that in order for the Instruction to make sense, it is required that the `start_at` < `end_at`. Moreover, there should be significant difference between these two. This can be utilized with the **Arbitrary crate**.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-0-1) #[derive(Arbitrary, Debug)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-0-2) pub struct InitVestingData {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-0-3)     pub recipient: AccountId,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-0-4)     #[arbitrary(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-0-5)         with = |u: &mut arbitrary::Unstructured| u.int_in_range(1..=1_000_000)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-0-6)     )]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-0-7)     pub amount: u64,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-0-8)     // we want start_at smaller than end_at    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-0-9)     // and for testing purposes we can run tests with times from the past    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-0-10)     #[arbitrary(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-0-11)         with = |u: &mut arbitrary::Unstructured| u.int_in_range(0..=1_000_000)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-0-12)     )]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-0-13)     pub start_at: u64,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-0-14)     #[arbitrary(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-0-15)         with = |u: &mut arbitrary::Unstructured| u.int_in_range(1_001_001..=1_050_000)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-0-16)     )]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-0-17)     pub end_at: u64,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-0-18)     #[arbitrary(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-0-19)         with = |u: &mut arbitrary::Unstructured| u.int_in_range(1..=1000)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-0-20)     )]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-0-21)     pub interval: u64, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-0-22) }`

Implement Arbitrary[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#implement-arbitrary "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are macros available to use with Arbitrary, however, it is possible to Implement the arbitrary function by yourself.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-1) // ------------------------------------------------------------------- [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-2) // ------------------------------------------------------------------- [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-3) // Implement Arbitrary [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-4) impl<'a> Arbitrary<'a> for InitVestingData {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-5)     fn arbitrary(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-6)         u: &mut arbitrary::Unstructured<'a>    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-7)     ) -> arbitrary::Result<Self> {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-8)         // obtain AccountId        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-9)         let recipient = AccountId::arbitrary(u)?; [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-10)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-11)         // limit the generated amount to the 1_000_000        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-12)         let amount = u.int_in_range(1..=1_000_000)?; [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-13)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-14)         // now we want to obtain        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-15)         // - start_at        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-16)         // - end_at        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-17)         // - interval        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-18)         // however we want to limit the data such that:        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-19)         // - start_at < end_at        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-20)         // - end_at - start_at > interval        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-21)         // - interval has lower limit of 500 and upper limit of 1000. [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-22)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-23)         let start_at: u64 = u.int_in_range(1_000_000..=5_000_000)?;        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-24)         let end_at: u64 = u.int_in_range(1_000_000..=5_000_000)?;        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-25)         let interval: u64 = u.int_in_range(500..=1000)?; [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-26)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-27)         // ensure that start_at < end_at        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-28)         if start_at >= end_at {            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-29)             return Err(arbitrary::Error::IncorrectFormat);        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-30)         } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-31)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-32)         // ensure that end_at - start_at > interval        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-33)         match end_at.checked_sub(start_at) {            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-34)             Some(diff) => {                [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-35)                 if diff <= interval {                    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-36)                     return Err(arbitrary::Error::IncorrectFormat);                [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-37)                 }            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-38)             }            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-39)             None => return Err(arbitrary::Error::IncorrectFormat),        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-40)         } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-41)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-42)         Ok(InitVestingData {            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-43)             recipient,            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-44)             amount,            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-45)             start_at,            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-46)             end_at,            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-47)             interval,        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-48)         })    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-49)     }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-50)     // -------------------------------------------------------------------    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-51)     // ------------------------------------------------------------------- [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/arbitrary-data/#__codelineno-1-52) }`

Tip

Consider checking the [Examples](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/examples/examples/)
 section for more tips.

# Trident by Examples - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/examples/examples/#trident-by-examples)

Trident by Examples[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/examples/examples/#trident-by-examples "Permanent link")

=====================================================================================================================

*   **Hello World!**
    
    * * *
    
    Hello World example with Trident.
    
    [Hello World!](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/tree/0.9.1/examples/hello_world)
    
*   **Possible vulnerabilities and bugs**
    
    * * *
    
    Check the possible attack vectors and bugs that can be detected using Trident.
    
    [Unchecked Arithmetic](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/tree/0.9.1/examples/common_issues/unchecked-arithmetic-0)
    
    [Incorrect Instruction Sequence](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/tree/0.9.1/examples/common_issues/incorrect-ix-sequence-1)
    
    [Unauthorized Access](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/tree/0.9.1/examples/common_issues/unauthorized-access-2)
    
    [Incorrect Integer Arithmetic](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/tree/0.9.1/examples/common_issues/incorrect-integer-arithmetic-3)
    
*   **Customize with Arbitrary**
    
    * * *
    
    You can use Arbitrary crate to your advantage and limit or customize the data that are sent to the instructions.
    
    [Custom Data Types](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/tree/0.9.1/examples/common_issues/arbitrary-custom-types-4)
    
    [Limiting Instructions Inputs](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/tree/0.9.1/examples/common_issues/arbitrary-limit-inputs-5)
    
*   **Cross-Program Invocation**
    
    * * *
    
    Trident supports Cross-Program Invocation, you can fuzz your programs and create NFTs at the same time.
    
    [Simple CPI](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/tree/0.9.1/examples/cpi/simple-cpi-6)
    
    [CPI with Metaplex Metadata Program](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/tree/0.9.1/examples/cpi/cpi-metaplex-7)
    
*   **Benchmarking**
    
    * * *
    
    Trident contains benchmarks of [Daedaluzz: A Benchmark Generator for Smart-Contract Fuzzers](https://github.com/Consensys/daedaluzz)
     rewritten in Rust.
    
    [Trident Benchmark](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/tree/0.9.1/examples/trident-benchmark)
    

Back to top

---

# Commands - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#trident-init)

Commands
========

* * *

trident init[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#trident-init "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-0-1) trident init`

*   This command Initializes Trident Workspace and generates new Fuzz Test Template.
    
*   The command will generate the following folder structure:
    
    `[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-1-1) project-root [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-1-2) ├── trident-tests [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-1-3) │   ├── fuzz_tests # fuzz tests folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-1-4) │   │   ├── fuzz_0 # particular fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-1-5) │   │   │   ├── test_fuzz.rs # the binary target of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-1-6) │   │   │   └── fuzz_instructions.rs # the definition of your fuzz test [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-1-7) │   │   ├── fuzz_1 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-1-8) │   │   ├── fuzz_X # possible multiple fuzz tests [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-1-9) │   │   ├── fuzzing # compilations and crashes folder [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-1-10) │   │   └── Cargo.toml [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-1-11) ├── Trident.toml [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-1-12) └── ...`
    

* * *

trident how[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#trident-how "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-2-1) trident how`

*   Print How To message about how to start writting fuzz tests.

* * *

trident fuzz[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#trident-fuzz "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-3-1) trident fuzz <subcommand>`

*   Behavior depends on the subcommands.

### trident fuzz run-afl[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#trident-fuzz-run-afl "Permanent link")

Warning

To execute and debug fuzz tests, navigate to the `trident-tests` directory.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-4-1) trident fuzz run-afl <fuzz_target>`

*   Run AFL on the specified Fuzz Target (i.e. the Fuzz Template, for example fuzz\_0).

#### Output[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#output "Permanent link")

TBD

### trident fuzz run-hfuzz[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#trident-fuzz-run-hfuzz "Permanent link")

Warning

To execute and debug fuzz tests, navigate to the `trident-tests` directory.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-5-1) trident fuzz run-hfuzz <fuzz_target>`

*   Run Honggfuzz on the specified Fuzz Target (i.e. the Fuzz Template, for example fuzz\_0).

#### Output[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#output_1 "Permanent link")

Important

The output provided by Honggfuzz is as follows:

1.  Number of Fuzzing Iterations.
2.  Feedback Driven Mode = Honggfuzz generates data based on the feedback (i.e. feedback based on Coverage progress).
3.  Average Iterations per second.
4.  Number of crashes it found (**panics** or failed **invariant checks**).

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-6-1) ------------------------[  0 days 00 hrs 00 mins 01 secs ]----------------------   [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-6-2)   Iterations : 688 (out of: 1000 [68%]) # -- 1. --  [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-6-3)   Mode [3/3] : Feedback Driven Mode # -- 2. --      [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-6-4)       Target : trident-tests/fuzz_tests/fuzzing.....wn-linux-gnu/release/fuzz_0     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-6-5)      Threads : 16, CPUs: 32, CPU%: 1262% [39%/CPU]       [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-6-6)        Speed : 680/sec [avg: 688] # -- 3. --     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-6-7)      Crashes : 1 [unique: 1, blocklist: 0, verified: 0] # -- 4. --    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-6-8)     Timeouts : 0 [10 sec] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-6-9)  Corpus Size : 98, max: 1048576 bytes, init: 0 files  [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-6-10)   Cov Update : 0 days 00 hrs 00 mins 00 secs ago    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-6-11)     Coverage : edge: 10345/882951 [1%] pc: 163 cmp: 622547 [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-6-12) ---------------------------------- [ LOGS ] ------------------/ honggfuzz 2.6 /-`

### trident fuzz debug-afl[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#trident-fuzz-debug-afl "Permanent link")

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-7-1) trident fuzz debug-afl <fuzz_target> <crash_file_path>`

*   Run AFL debug on the specified Fuzz Target (i.e. the Fuzz Template, for example fuzz\_0), with specified crash file, to see where the crash file found an issue.

#### Output[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#output_2 "Permanent link")

TBD

### trident fuzz debug-hfuzz[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#trident-fuzz-debug-hfuzz "Permanent link")

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-8-1) trident fuzz debug-hfuzz <fuzz_target> <crash_file_path>`

*   Run Honggfuzz debug on the specified Fuzz Target (i.e. the Fuzz Template, for example fuzz\_0), with specified crash file, to see where the crash file found an issue.

#### Output[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#output_3 "Permanent link")

Important

The debug output is at current development stage really verbose and contains lldb parts. We are working on improving this experience. In the picture below you can see an example of provided debug output.

1.  Series of Transaction Logs
2.  Structures of data send within the Instructions
3.  **Panic** or **Crash**, based on if the Fuzzing panicked within the Solana Program or Invariant Check failed.

![alt text](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/images/run-debug.png)

### trident fuzz add[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#trident-fuzz-add "Permanent link")

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-9-1) trident fuzz add`

*   Adds new Fuzz Test Template.

* * *

trident clean[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#trident-clean "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/#__codelineno-10-1) trident clean`

*   Calls `anchor clean` and cleans targets created by the underlying Honggfuzz. Crashfiles and Fuzzing Inputs are preserved.

Back to top

# Trident Manifest - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#trident-manifest)

Trident Manifest[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#trident-manifest "Permanent link")

=======================================================================================================================

You can pass supported parameters via the **Trident.toml** configuration file:

\[fuzz\][#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#fuzz "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### programs[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#programs "Permanent link")

*   Trident allows you to specify genesis programs (SBF targets) that will be included in the fuzzing environment in order to perform all desired Cross-Program-Invocations.
    
*   Including these types of programs will lead to performance decline of Trident.
    

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-0-1) [[fuzz.programs]] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-0-2) address = "metaqbxxUerdq28cj1RbAWkYQm3ybzjb6a8bt518x1s" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-0-3) program = "metaplex-program/metaplex-token-metadata.so"`

* * *

#### accounts[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#accounts "Permanent link")

*   Trident allwos you to specify genesis accounts to inlcude in the fuzzing environment. In most cases it is helpful to dump some accounts from mainnet and use then during testing.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-1-1) [[fuzz.accounts]] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-1-2) address = "6YG3J7PaxyMnnbU67ifyrgF3BzNzc7cD8hPkqK6ATweE" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-1-3) filename = "tests/accounts/core_bridge_mainnet/guardian_set_5_mock.json"`

* * *

#### allow\_duplicate\_txs[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#allow_duplicate_txs "Permanent link")

*   Allow processing of duplicate transactions. Setting to true might speed up fuzzing but can cause false positive crashes (default: false)

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-1) [fuzz] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-2) # Allow processing of duplicate transactions. [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-3) # Setting to true might speed up fuzzing but can cause [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-4) # false positive crashes (default: false) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-5) allow_duplicate_txs = false`

* * *

#### fuzzing\_with\_stats[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#fuzzing_with_stats "Permanent link")

*   Trident will show statistics after the fuzzing session. This option forces use of honggfuzz parameter `keep_output` as true in order to be able to catch fuzzer stdout. (default: false)

``[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-3-1) [fuzz] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-3-2) # Trident will show statistics after the fuzzing session. [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-3-3) # This option forces use of honggfuzz parameter [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-3-4) # `keep_output` as true in order to be able to catch fuzzer stdout. [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-3-5) # (default: false) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-3-6) fuzzing_with_stats = true``

* * *

\[honggfuzz\][#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#honggfuzz "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### timeout[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#timeout "Permanent link")

*   Timeout in seconds (default: 10)

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-4-1) [honggfuzz] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-4-2) # Timeout in seconds (default: 10) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-4-3) timeout = 10`

* * *

#### iterations[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#iterations "Permanent link")

*   Number of fuzzing iterations (default: 0 \[no limit\])

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-5-1) [honggfuzz] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-5-2) # Number of fuzzing iterations (default: 0 [no limit]) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-5-3) iterations = 0`

* * *

#### threads[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#threads "Permanent link")

*   Number of concurrent fuzzing threads (default: 0 \[number of CPUs / 2\])

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-6-1) [honggfuzz] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-6-2) # Number of concurrent fuzzing threads (default: 0 [number of CPUs / 2]) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-6-3) threads = 0`

* * *

#### keep\_output[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#keep_output "Permanent link")

*   Don't close children's stdin, stdout, stderr; can be noisy (default: false)

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-1) [honggfuzz] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-2) # Don't close children's stdin, stdout, stderr; can be noisy (default: false) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-7-3) keep_output = false`

* * *

#### verbose[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#verbose "Permanent link")

*   Disable ANSI console; use simple log output (default: false)

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-8-1) [honggfuzz] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-8-2) # Disable ANSI console; use simple log output (default: false) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-8-3) verbose = false`

* * *

#### exit\_upon\_crash[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#exit_upon_crash "Permanent link")

*   Exit upon seeing the first crash (default: false)

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-9-1) [honggfuzz] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-9-2) # Exit upon seeing the first crash (default: false) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-9-3) exit_upon_crash = false`

* * *

#### mutations\_per\_run[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#mutations_per_run "Permanent link")

*   Maximal number of mutations per one run (default: 6)

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-10-1) [honggfuzz] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-10-2) # Maximal number of mutations per one run (default: 6) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-10-3) mutations_per_run = 6`

* * *

#### cargo\_target\_dir[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#cargo_target_dir "Permanent link")

*   Target compilation directory, (default: "" \["trident-tests/fuzz\_tests/fuzzing/honggfuzz/hfuzz\_target"\]).
*   To not clash with cargo build's default target directory.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-11-1) [honggfuzz] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-11-2) # Target compilation directory, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-11-3) # (default: "" ["trident-tests/fuzz_tests/fuzzing/honggfuzz/hfuzz_target"]). [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-11-4) # To not clash with cargo build's default target directory. [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-11-5) cargo_target_dir = ""`

* * *

#### hfuzz\_workspace[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#hfuzz_workspace "Permanent link")

*   Honggfuzz working directory, (default: "" \["trident-tests/fuzz\_tests/fuzzing/honggfuzz/hfuzz\_workspace"\]).

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-12-1) [honggfuzz] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-12-2) # Honggfuzz working directory, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-12-3) # (default: "" ["trident-tests/fuzz_tests/fuzzing/honggfuzz/hfuzz_workspace"]). [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-12-4) hfuzz_workspace = ""`

* * *

#### crashdir[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#crashdir "Permanent link")

*   Directory where crashes are saved to (default: "" \[workspace directory\])

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-13-1) [honggfuzz] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-13-2) # Directory where crashes are saved to (default: "" [workspace directory]) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-13-3) crashdir = ""`

* * *

#### extension[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#extension "Permanent link")

*   Input file extension (e.g. 'swf'), (default: "" \['fuzz'\])

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-14-1) [honggfuzz] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-14-2) # Input file extension (e.g. 'swf'), (default: "" ['fuzz']) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-14-3) extension = ""`

* * *

#### run\_time[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#run_time "Permanent link")

*   Number of seconds this fuzzing session will last (default: 0 \[no limit\])

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-15-1) [honggfuzz] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-15-2) # Number of seconds this fuzzing session will last (default: 0 [no limit]) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-15-3) run_time = 0`

* * *

#### max\_file\_size[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#max_file_size "Permanent link")

*   Maximal size of files processed by the fuzzer in bytes (default: 1048576 = 1MB)

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-16-1) [honggfuzz] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-16-2) # Maximal size of files processed by the fuzzer in bytes [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-16-3) # (default: 1048576 = 1MB) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-16-4) max_file_size = 1048576`

* * *

#### save\_all[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#save_all "Permanent link")

*   Save all test-cases (not only the unique ones) by appending the current time-stamp to the filenames (default: false)

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-17-1) [honggfuzz] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-17-2) # Save all test-cases [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-17-3) # (not only the unique ones) by appending the current [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-17-4) # time-stamp to the filename (default: false) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-17-5) save_all = false`

Tip

Consider checking the [Examples](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/examples/examples/)
 section for more tips.

Back to top

# FAQ - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/faq/faq/#faq)

FAQ[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/faq/faq/#faq "Permanent link")

===========================================================================

### Is Trident supported only with Anchor ?[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/faq/faq/#is-trident-supported-only-with-anchor "Permanent link")

*   Currently yes, Trident under the hood obtains data from the IDL generated by Anchor.

### I created the Fuzz Test what should I do next ?[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/faq/faq/#i-created-the-fuzz-test-what-should-i-do-next "Permanent link")

*   Start here [Writing Fuzz Tests](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/)
    . For additional features check [Features](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/features/)
    . If you are not sure about anything check [Get Help](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/get-help/get-help/)
    

### My program Instruction contains custom type such as Struct or Enum on its input, but it does not derive Arbitrary.[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/faq/faq/#my-program-instruction-contains-custom-type-such-as-struct-or-enum-on-its-input-but-it-does-not-derive-arbitrary "Permanent link")

*   In this case you need to specify same type in the Fuzz Test (with the same fields). And implement From Trait to convert to your type. Check [Custom Data Types](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/)
     or [Examples of Arbitrary](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/examples/examples/)
    .

### Is Trident open-source ?[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/faq/faq/#is-trident-open-source "Permanent link")

*   Yes, here [Trident](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident)
    

### I would like to report Issue with Trident, what should I do ?[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/faq/faq/#i-would-like-to-report-issue-with-trident-what-should-i-do "Permanent link")

*   Write Issue [Issues](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/issues)
    

### Is Trident deployed on Mainnet / Devnet / Testenet ?[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/faq/faq/#is-trident-deployed-on-mainnet-devnet-testenet "Permanent link")

*   No, Trident is Fuzz Testing Framework, not Solana Program.

### What type of Fuzzer Trident is ?[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/faq/faq/#what-type-of-fuzzer-trident-is "Permanent link")

*   Currently, we refer to it as _"coverage guided gray box fuzzer"_.

Back to top

---

# Writing fuzz test - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#initialize-trident)

Writing fuzz test
=================

Initialize Trident[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#initialize-trident "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Initialize Trident in the Anchor-based workspace.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-0-1) trident init`

Info

Trident under the hood

*   Builds the Anchor-based project.
*   Reads the generated IDL.
*   Based on the IDL creates the fuzzing template.

Tip

If you have Trident already initialized, you can add a new fuzz test using `trident fuzz add`.

Fill the Fuzz test Template[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#fill-the-fuzz-test-template "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Define Fuzz Accounts[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#define-fuzz-accounts "Permanent link")

Define `AccountsStorage` type for each Account you would like to use.

Important

Keep in mind:

*   You do not need to specify every `AccountStorage`; some accounts do not necessarily need to be stored in their corresponding storage.
    *   For example, `System Program` does not need to be stored and can be used from the `solana_sdk`.
*   You can rename `FuzzAccounts` fields to whatever you want. The default names were generated based on the Program's `IDL`.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-1-1) #[doc = r" Use AccountsStorage<T> where T can be one of:"] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-1-2) #[doc = r" Keypair, PdaStore, TokenStore, MintStore, ProgramStore"] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-1-3) #[derive(Default)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-1-4) pub struct FuzzAccounts {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-1-5)     author: AccountsStorage<KeypairStore>,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-1-6)     hello_world_account: AccountsStorage<PdaStore>,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-1-7)     // No need to fuzz system_program    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-1-8)     // system_program: AccountsStorage<todo!()>, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-1-9) }`

Tip

For more details about the `AccountsStorage`, check [AccountsStorage](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/account-storages/)
.

### Implement Fuzz Instructions[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#implement-fuzz-instructions "Permanent link")

Each Instruction in the Fuzz Test must define the following functions:

*   `get_discriminator`
    *   Defines Instruction Discriminator, which is used to identify the Instruction.
*   `get_program_id()`
    *   Specifies to which program the Instruction belongs. This function is **automatically defined** and should not need any updates. The importance is such that if you have multiple programs in your workspace, Trident can generate Instruction Sequences corresponding to different programs.
*   `get_data()`
    *   Specifies what Instruction inputs are sent to the Program Instructions.
*   `get_accounts()`
    *   Specifies what Accounts are sent to the Program Instructions.

Tip

*   For more info about how to write these functions, check the [Fuzz Instructions](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/)
    .
*   For examples of how to write these functions, check the [Examples](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/examples/examples/)
    .

Execute[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#execute "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Warning

To execute and debug fuzz tests, navigate to the `trident-tests` directory.

### Run Fuzz Test[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#run-fuzz-test "Permanent link")

In principle there are two possible fuzzing engines that the Trident supports, [Honggfuzz](https://github.com/google/honggfuzz)
 and [AFL](https://aflplus.plus/)
.

To execute the desired fuzz test using the Honggfuzz, run the following command from the `trident-tests` directory:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-2-1) # Replace <TARGET_NAME> with the name of particular [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-2-2) # fuzz test (for example: "fuzz_0") [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-2-3) trident fuzz run-hfuzz <TARGET_NAME>`

To execute the desired fuzz test using the AFL, run the following command from the `trident-tests` directory:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-3-1) # Replace <TARGET_NAME> with the name of particular [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-3-2) # fuzz test (for example: "fuzz_0") [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-3-3) trident fuzz run-afl <TARGET_NAME>`

### Debug Fuzz Test[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#debug-fuzz-test "Permanent link")

To debug your program using Honggfuzz with values from a crash file, run the following command from the `trident-tests` directory:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-4-1) # The fuzzer will run the <TARGET_NAME> with the specified <CRASH_FILE_PATH> [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-4-2) trident fuzz debug-hfuzz <TARGET_NAME> <CRASH_FILE_PATH>`

To debug your program using AFL with values from a crash file, run the following command from the `trident-tests` directory:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-5-1) # The fuzzer will run the <TARGET_NAME> with the specified <CRASH_FILE_PATH> [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/writing-fuzz-test/writing-fuzz-test/#__codelineno-5-2) trident fuzz debug-afl <TARGET_NAME> <CRASH_FILE_PATH>`

Tip

By default, the crash files are stored in:

*   `trident-tests/fuzzing/honggfuzz/hfuzz_workspace/<FUZZ_TARGET>` for Honggfuzz and
*   `trident-tests/fuzzing/afl/afl_workspace/out/default/crashes` for AFL.

Tip

For more info about the fuzzing outputs, check the [Commands](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/commands/commands/)
.

Back to top

---

# Trident Features - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/features/#trident-features)

Trident Features[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/features/#trident-features "Permanent link")

===============================================================================================================

Trident contains multiple features to enhance the fuzzing experience and increase ability to discover bugs.

*   **AccountStorages**
    
    * * *
    
    Initialize, store and re-use random Accounts.
    
    [**AccountStorages**](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/account-storages/)
    
*   **FuzzInstructions**
    
    * * *
    
    All available Program Instructions as FuzzInstructions Variants.
    
    [**FuzzInstructions**](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/)
    
*   **Custom Instruction Sequences**
    
    * * *
    
    Specify Instruction Sequqnces you would like to executed instead of completely random execution order.
    
    [**Custom Instruction Sequences**](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/)
    
*   **Invariant Checks**
    
    * * *
    
    Allows to compare Account contents before and after the Instruction was successfully executed.
    
    [**Invariant Checks**](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/invariant-checks/)
    
*   **Programs and Accounts**
    
    * * *
    
    Include programs and accounts from the desired cluster (Mainnet, Devnet, etc.).
    
    [**Programs and Accounts**](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/)
    
*   **Fuzzing Statistics**
    
    * * *
    
    Show Fuzzing Statistics after the Fuzzing Session ended.
    
    [**Fuzzing Statistics**](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzzing-statistics/)
    
*   **Customize Instruction Data**
    
    * * *
    
    Customize Instruction data, for example, to use integers from specific range.
    
    [**Customize Instruction Data**](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/)
    
*   **Trident Manifest**
    
    * * *
    
    Customize Fuzzing experience with the Trident Manifest.
    
    [**Trident Manifest**](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/)
    
*   **Custom Error Handlers**
    
    * * *
    
    Continue Instruction Sequence in case of Instruction Error was returned or specify custom behavior based on the returned error.
    
    [**Custom Error Handlers**](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/error-handlers/)
    

Back to top

---

# Account Storages - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/account-storages/#account-storages)

Account Storages[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/account-storages/#account-storages "Permanent link")

=======================================================================================================================

Trident allows developers to generate random accounts for fuzzing.

However, the fuzzer cannot generate account addresses completely randomly, as the address has 32 bytes; this means that the fuzzer will, in most cases, generate incorrect addresses.

Thus, Trident generates random **AccountIDs** which are indexes to **Account Storages**. Each unique account contained within the Anchor-generated IDL has its own AccountStorage. The FuzzAccounts containing the Account Storages are global to all instructions.

Important

There are two types of Account Storages:

*   KeypairStore (dedicated for Keypairs)
*   PdaStore (dedicated for Program Derived Addresses)

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/account-storages/#__codelineno-0-1) pub struct FuzzAccounts {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/account-storages/#__codelineno-0-2)     signer: AccountsStorage<KeypairStore>,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/account-storages/#__codelineno-0-3)     some_pda: AccountsStorage<PdaStore>,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/account-storages/#__codelineno-0-4)     // ... [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/account-storages/#__codelineno-0-5) }`

Tip

Keep in mind:

*   You do not need to specify every `AccountStorage`; some accounts do not necessarily need to be stored in their corresponding storage.
    *   For example, the `System Program` does not need to be stored and can be used from the `solana_sdk` as a constant account address.
*   If you are going to initialize an `Associated Token Account` in your Solana Program, use `PdaStore`.
*   You can rename fields of `FuzzAccounts` to whatever you want. The default names are generated based on the Program's `IDL`.

Account Storage Methods[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/account-storages/#account-storage-methods "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are multiple methods to interact with Account Storages.

### `get_or_create_account()`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/account-storages/#get_or_create_account "Permanent link")

Retrieves a record from AccountsStorage based on the entered `account_id`. If no record exists for the `account_id`, a new **empty** account is created.

### `get()`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/account-storages/#get "Permanent link")

Retrieves a record from AccountsStorage based on the entered `account_id`. If no record exists for the `account_id`, a random public key is returned.

### `get_or_create_token_account()`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/account-storages/#get_or_create_token_account "Permanent link")

Retrieves a record from AccountsStorage based on the entered `account_id`. If no record exists for the `account_id`, a new Token account is created.

### `get_or_create_mint_account()`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/account-storages/#get_or_create_mint_account "Permanent link")

Retrieves a record from AccountsStorage based on the entered `account_id`. If no record exists for the `account_id`, a new Mint account is created.

### `get_or_create_delegated_account()`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/account-storages/#get_or_create_delegated_account "Permanent link")

Retrieves a record from AccountsStorage based on the entered `account_id`. If no record exists for the `account_id`, a new Delegated account is created.

### `get_or_create_initialized_account()`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/account-storages/#get_or_create_initialized_account "Permanent link")

Retrieves a record from AccountsStorage based on the entered `account_id`. If no record exists for the `account_id`, a new Initialized account is created.

### `get_or_create_vote_account()`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/account-storages/#get_or_create_vote_account "Permanent link")

Retrieves a record from AccountsStorage based on the entered `account_id`. If no record exists for the `account_id`, a new Vote account is created.

Tip

Consider checking the [Examples](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/examples/examples/)
 section for more tips.

Back to top

---

# Changelog - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/CHANGELOG/#changelog)

Changelog[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/CHANGELOG/#changelog "Permanent link")

=========================================================================================

All notable changes to this project will be documented in this file.

The format is based on [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.0.0/)
, and this project adheres to [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html)
 (SemVer).

**Note**: Version 0 of Semantic Versioning is handled differently from version 1 and above. The minor version will be incremented upon a breaking change and the patch version will be incremented for features.

\[dev\] - Unreleased[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/CHANGELOG/#dev-unreleased "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

\[0.9.1\] - 2025-02-03[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/CHANGELOG/#091-2025-02-03 "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   added warp to time manipulation ([259](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/259)
    )
*   added methods to check if account storage is empty ([258](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/258)
    )
*   added support for post-instruction behavior ([257](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/257)
    )

**Removed**

**Changed**

\[0.9.0\] - 2025-01-15[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/CHANGELOG/#090-2025-01-15 "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   added support for composite accounts ([245](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/245)
    )
*   Trident SVM + AFL (see the PR for more details) ([234](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/234)
    )

**Removed**

*   removed fuzz\_iteration from test\_fuzz.rs ([243](https://github.com/Ackee-Blockchain/trident/pull/243)

*   Implemented Anchor Client logic was not able to work with newer version of Anchor. Fixed with `async_rpc` and `async` feature.
*   Trident init IDL Parse Error on newer version of Rust, fixed with updated `accounts` token.

\[0.3.0\] - 2022-09-23[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/CHANGELOG/#030-2022-09-23 "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Changed**

*   Upgrade Solana (`~1.10`) and Anchor framework (`~0.25`) versions

**Added**

*   Custom Solana RPC error reporter. If the Solana RPC error is thrown, the error code, message and data (logs) are reported to the output.
*   Custom imports in the `.program_client`. User is able to import custom types and structures into program client. The import part of the code would not be re-generated.

\[0.2.0\] - 2022-07-27[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/CHANGELOG/#020-2022-07-27 "Permanent link")

-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Added**

*   Trident is now configurable. This requires `Trident.toml` file to exist in the project's root directory - without this file the execution will fail. To solve this re-run `trident init` or just create an empty `Trident.toml` file in the project's root directory.

# Instructions Sequences - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#instructions-sequences)

Instructions Sequences[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#instructions-sequences "Permanent link")

=========================================================================================================================================

Trident allows you to specify **custom instruction sequences** that you would like to execute.

Possible instruction sequences are divided into three parts:

*   **Pre-Instructions**
*   **Instructions**
*   **Post-Instructions**

For example, if your program requires an Initialization instruction at the start, you can specify it using the `pre_sequence()` macro, as shown in the source code below.

``[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-1) // test_fuzz.rs [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-2)[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-3) /// ... [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-4)[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-5) struct InstructionsSequence; [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-6) /// Define instruction sequences for invocation. [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-7) /// `pre` runs at the start, `middle` in the middle, and `post` at the end. [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-8) /// For example, to call `InitializeFn`, `UpdateFn` and then `WithdrawFn` during [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-9) /// each fuzzing iteration: [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-10) /// ``` [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-11) /// impl FuzzDataBuilder<FuzzInstruction> for InstructionsSequence { [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-12) ///     pre_sequence!(InitializeFn,UpdateFn); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-13) ///     middle_sequence!(WithdrawFn); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-14) ///} [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-15) /// ``` [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-16) /// For more details, see: [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-17) /// https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/dev/features/instructions-sequences/#instructions-sequences [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-18) impl FuzzDataBuilder<FuzzInstruction> for InstructionsSequence {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-19)     pre_sequence!(InitializeFn);    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-20)     middle_sequence!();    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-21)     post_sequence!(); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-22) } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-23)[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-0-24) /// ...``

Tip

*   The arguments to the macro are variants of `FuzzInstruction` specified in `fuzz_instructions.rs`.
*   Empty macro parameters (such as `middle_sequence!()`) will skip that section, meaning no instructions will be executed during that phase.
*   If no macro is defined for a section, a random instruction sequence will be generated for that section.

Manual Trait Override[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#manual-trait-override "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

It is not necessary to use the macro as explained above. The trait implementation (i.e., the methods) can be implemented manually, allowing for greater customization if needed. The rules are the same as described above.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-1) // test_fuzz.rs [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-2)[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-3) // Do not forget to include the required structures [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-4) use fuzz_instructions::InitVesting; [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-5) use fuzz_instructions::WithdrawUnlocked; [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-6)[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-7) impl FuzzDataBuilder<FuzzInstruction> for MyFuzzData {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-8)     fn pre_ixs(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-9)         u: &mut arbitrary::Unstructured    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-10)     ) -> arbitrary::Result<Vec<FuzzInstruction>> {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-11)         let init_ix =            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-12)             FuzzInstruction::InitVesting(InitVesting::arbitrary(u)?); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-13)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-14)         Ok(vec![init_ix])    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-15)     }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-16)     fn ixs(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-17)         u: &mut arbitrary::Unstructured    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-18)     ) -> arbitrary::Result<Vec<FuzzInstruction>> {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-19)         let withdraw_ix =            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-20)             FuzzInstruction::WithdrawUnlocked(WithdrawUnlocked::arbitrary(u)?); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-21)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-22)         Ok(vec![withdraw_ix])    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-23)     }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-24)     fn post_ixs(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-25)         _u: &mut arbitrary::Unstructured    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-26)     ) -> arbitrary::Result<Vec<FuzzInstruction>> {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-27)         Ok(vec![])    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-28)     } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/instructions-sequences/#__codelineno-1-29) }`

Tip

Consider checking the [Examples](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/examples/examples/)
 section for more tips on implementing instruction sequences effectively.
