# Fuzzing Statistics - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzzing-statistics/#fuzzing-statistics)

Fuzzing Statistics[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzzing-statistics/#fuzzing-statistics "Permanent link")

=============================================================================================================================

Trident allows you to see statistics after the fuzzing session ended.

Important

In order to show statistics set `fuzzing_with_stats` within the `Trident.toml` to `true`.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzzing-statistics/#__codelineno-0-1) [fuzz] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzzing-statistics/#__codelineno-0-2) # ... [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzzing-statistics/#__codelineno-0-3) fuzzing_with_stats = true [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzzing-statistics/#__codelineno-0-4) # ...`

Available Statistics[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzzing-statistics/#available-statistics "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Simple[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzzing-statistics/#simple "Permanent link")

*   Number of invocations of each instruction during the fuzzing session.
*   Number of successful invocations of each instruction during the fuzzing session.
*   Number of failed invariants checks for each instruction during the fuzzing session.

Note

Keep in mind that the number of fuzz iterations does not directly correspond to the total number of invocations. In one fuzz iteration, the fuzzer might be unable to deserialize fuzz data into instructions, causing the entire iteration to be skipped.

On the other hand, this is expected behavior as the underlying data are randomly (with coverage feedback) generated, so the Honggfuzz will not necessarily find appropriate data each iteration.

Tip

Consider checking the [Examples](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/examples/examples/)
 section for more tips.

Back to top

---

# Invariant Checks - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/invariant-checks/#invariant-checks)

Invariant Checks[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/invariant-checks/#invariant-checks "Permanent link")

=======================================================================================================================

Trident allows you to (optionally) specify invariant checks for each Instruction.

The invariant check will be called after the Instruction has been successfully invoked. Within the invariant check, you can compare the contents of accounts before and after the Instruction.

Important

Returning an error in the Invariant Check is considered a detection of undesired behavior (i.e., issue/crash detected).

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-1) fn check(     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-2)     &self,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-3)     pre_ix: &[SnapshotAccount],    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-4)     post_ix: &[SnapshotAccount],    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-5)     ix_data: Vec<u8>, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-6) ) -> Result<(), FuzzingError> {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-7)     if let Ok(hello_world_account) =        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-8)         StoreHelloWorld::deserialize(&mut post_ix[1].data_no_discriminator())    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-9)     {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-10)         if hello_world_account.input == 253 {            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-11)             return Err(FuzzingError::Custom(1));        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-12)         }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-13)     }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-14)     Ok(()) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-0-15) }`

Important

The order of accounts within the array is the same as the order of accounts in the instruction input of your program.

Account Deserialization[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/invariant-checks/#account-deserialization "Permanent link")

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `SnapshotAccount` provides methods to obtain parts of the account (e.g., address, its data, owner, etc.).

If you want to deserialize data into a struct defined within your program, ensure that the struct is present in the fuzz test template and has derived the `BorshDeserialize` and `BorshSerialize` traits, as shown in the example below:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-1-1) #[derive(Debug, BorshDeserialize, BorshSerialize, Clone)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-1-2) pub struct StoreHelloWorld {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-1-3)     recipient: Pubkey,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-1-4)     input: u8, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/invariant-checks/#__codelineno-1-5) }`

Tip

Consider checking the [Examples](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/examples/examples/)
 section for more tips.

Back to top

---

# Programs and Accounts - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#programs-and-accounts)

Programs and Accounts[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#programs-and-accounts "Permanent link")

====================================================================================================================================

Trident allows for usage of programs and accounts from the desired cluster (Mainnet, Devnet, etc.).

### Include Mainnet Programs[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#include-mainnet-programs "Permanent link")

In case you want to include programs from Mainnet, you can do so by specifying the address and path to the program in the `Trident.toml`.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-0-1) [[fuzz.programs]] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-0-2) address = "metaqbxxUerdq28cj1RbAWkYQm3ybzjb6a8bt518x1s" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-0-3) program = "metaplex-program/metaplex-token-metadata.so"`

Tip

If you want to dump a program from Mainnet, use

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-1-1) # -u m specifies to dump from mainnet [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-1-2) solana program dump -u m <PROGRAM_ID> <PROGRAM_NAME>.so`

### Include Mainnet Accounts[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#include-mainnet-accounts "Permanent link")

In case you want to include accounts from Mainnet, you can do so by specifying the address and path to the account in the `Trident.toml`.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-2-1) [[fuzz.accounts]] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-2-2) address = "6YG3J7PaxyMnnbU67ifyrgF3BzNzc7cD8hPkqK6ATweE" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-2-3) filename = "tests/accounts/core_bridge_mainnet/guardian_set_5_mock.json"`

Tip

If you want to obtain an account with `base64` data format, use

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-3-1) # -u m specifies to dump from mainnet [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-3-2) solana account -u m <ADDRESS> --output json`

### Include Programs Through the Entrypoint[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#include-programs-through-the-entrypoint "Permanent link")

There is another way to include programs in the Fuzz Test Environment. Including programs through the entrypoint is better for fuzzing, as the program is built together with the fuzz test, so that it will contain instrumentation which helps the fuzzer to better cover all possible program branches. However, the source code is required to do so.

You can include additional programs using the program entrypoint, as shown in the example below:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-1) // test_fuzz.rs [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-2)[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-3) use callee::entry as entry_callee; [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-4) use caller::entry as entry_caller; [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-5)[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-6) // ... [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-7)[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-8) fn main() {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-9)     // Program 1    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-10)     let program_callee = ProgramEntrypoint::new(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-11)         pubkey!("HJR1TK8bgrUWzysdpS1pBGBYKF7zi1tU9cS4qj8BW8ZL"),        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-12)         None,        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-13)         processor!(entry_callee),    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-14)     ); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-15)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-16)     // Program 2    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-17)     let program_caller = ProgramEntrypoint::new(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-18)         pubkey!("FWtSodrkUnovFPnNRCxneP6VWh6JH6jtQZ4PHoP8Ejuz"),        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-19)         None,        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-20)         processor!(entry_caller),    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-21)     );    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-22)     let config = Config::new(); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-23)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-24)     let mut client = TridentSVM::new_client(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-25)         &[program_callee, program_caller],        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-26)         &config    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-27)     ); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-28)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-29)     fuzz_trident !        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-30)         (fuzz_ix : FuzzInstruction , | fuzz_data : InstructionsSequence |            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-31)             { fuzz_iteration (fuzz_data , & config , & mut client) ; }); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/programs-n-accounts/#__codelineno-4-32) }`

Tip

Consider checking the [Examples](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/examples/examples/)
 section for more tips.

Back to top

# Error Handler - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/error-handlers/#error-handler)

Error Handler[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/error-handlers/#error-handler "Permanent link")

===============================================================================================================

Trident allows you to specify a custom error handler for each instruction.

This can be particularly helpful in the following scenarios:

*   If a transaction returns an error, you can choose to omit this error and continue the fuzzing process.
*   Using the `tx_error_handler`, you can check if the returned error is desired based on the accounts and input data that were used.

Tip

By default, transaction errors are propagated, meaning that if the transaction fails, the fuzzing iteration is stopped, and a new fuzzing iteration is started.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-0-1) /// Default implementation [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-0-2) fn tx_error_handler(     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-0-3)     &self,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-0-4)     e: TransactionError,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-0-5)     ix_data: Vec<u8>,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-0-6)     pre_ix_acc_infos: &[SnapshotAccount], [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-0-7) ) -> Result<(), TransactionError> {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-0-8)     Err(e) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-0-9) }`

To omit the error and continue with the next instruction in the iteration, you can use the following implementation:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-1-1) /// Custom implementation [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-1-2) fn tx_error_handler(     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-1-3)     &self,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-1-4)     e: TransactionError,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-1-5)     ix_data: Vec<u8>,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-1-6)     pre_ix_acc_infos: &[SnapshotAccount], [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-1-7) ) -> Result<(), TransactionError> {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-1-8)     Ok(()) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/error-handlers/#__codelineno-1-9) }`

Back to top

---

# Account Storages - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/account-storages/#account-storages)

Account Storages[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/account-storages/#account-storages "Permanent link")

=======================================================================================================================

Trident allows developers to generate random accounts for fuzzing.

However, the Accounts are not completely random, and neither are the Account addresses.

Instead, Trident generates random **AccountIDs** which are indexes to **Account Storages**. Each unique Account contained within the Anchor generated IDL has its own AccountStorage. The FuzzAccounts containing the Accounts Storages is global to all Instructions to use.

Note

**Details:**

Always generating only random accounts would **in most cases lead to a situation where the fuzzer would be stuck because the accounts would be almost every time rejected by your Anchor program**. Therefore it is necessary to specify, what accounts should be used and also limit the number of newly created accounts to reduce the space complexity.

Important

Currently, supported types of Account Storages:

*   Signer (KeypairStore)
*   Program Derived Address (PdaStore)
*   Token Account (TokenStore)
*   Mint Account (MintStore)
*   Program Account (ProgramStore)
*   Stake Account (StakeStore)
*   Vote Account (VoteStore)

Then use the corresponding AccountsStorage.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/account-storages/#__codelineno-0-1) pub struct FuzzAccounts {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/account-storages/#__codelineno-0-2)     signer: AccountsStorage<KeypairStore>,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/account-storages/#__codelineno-0-3)     some_pda: AccountsStorage<PdaStore>,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/account-storages/#__codelineno-0-4)     token_vault: AccountsStorage<TokenStore>,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/account-storages/#__codelineno-0-5)     mint: AccountsStorage<MintStore>,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/account-storages/#__codelineno-0-6)     // ... [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/account-storages/#__codelineno-0-7) }`

Tip

Keep in mind:

*   You do not need to specify every `AccountStorage`, some accounts do not necessarily need to be stored in their corresponding storage.
    *   For example `System Program` does not need to be stored, rather can be used from the `solana_sdk`.
*   If you are about to Initialize `Mint` or `Token Account` in your Solana Program.
    *   use `Keypair` or `PdaStore` (not `MintStore` or `TokenStore`).
*   If you are going to initialize `Associated Token Account` in your Solana Program.
    *   use `PdaStore`.
*   You can rename fields of `FuzzAccounts` to whatever you want. The default names are generated based on the Program's `IDL`.

Tip

Consider checking the [Examples](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/examples/examples/)
 section for more tips.

Back to top

---

# Installation - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/installation/installation/#installation)

Installation[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/installation/installation/#installation "Permanent link")

===============================================================================================================

Prerequisites

Before proceeding, ensure you have installed:

*   [Rust](https://www.rust-lang.org/tools/install)
     (stable version)
*   [Solana CLI](https://solana.com/docs/intro/installation)
    
*   [Anchor](https://www.anchor-lang.com/docs/installation)
    

Check out [supported versions](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/installation/installation/#supported-versions)
 for version compatibility.

Install system dependencies[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/installation/installation/#install-system-dependencies "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Update your package list:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-0-1) sudo apt update [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-0-2) sudo apt upgrade`

Install the required packages:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-1-1) sudo apt install build-essential [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-1-2) sudo apt-get install binutils-dev [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-1-3) sudo apt-get install libunwind-dev`

Install Trident[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/installation/installation/#install-trident "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-2-1) cargo install trident-cli`

You can also use the `version` flag to install a specific version:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-3-1) cargo install trident-cli --version x.y.z`

Install Hongfuzz and AFL[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/installation/installation/#install-hongfuzz-and-afl "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-4-1) cargo install honggfuzz [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-4-2) cargo install cargo-afl`

To install a specific version use the following commands:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-5-1) cargo install honggfuzz --version x.y.z [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/installation/installation/#__codelineno-5-2) cargo install cargo-afl --version x.y.z`

Supported versions[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/installation/installation/#supported-versions "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| **_Trident CLI_** | **_Anchor_** | **_Solana_** | **_Rust_** | **_Honggfuzz_** | **_AFL_** |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **_`develop`_** | `>=0.29.0` | `>=1.17.3` | `nightly` | `0.5.56` | `0.15.11` |
| **_`0.9.0`_** | `>=0.29.0` | `>=1.17.3` | `nightly` | `0.5.56` | `0.15.11` |
| **_`0.8.*`_** | `0.30.1` | `^1.17.4` | `nightly` | `0.5.56` | \-  |
| **_`0.7.0`_** | `>=0.29.*` | `^1.17.4` | `nightly` | `0.5.56` | \-  |
| **_`0.6.0`_** | `>=0.29.*` | `^1.17` | `nightly` | `0.5.55` | \-  |
| **_`0.5.0`_** | `~0.28.*` | `=1.16.6` | \-  | \-  | \-  |
| **_`0.4.0`_** | `~0.27.*` | `>=1.15` | \-  | \-  | \-  |
| **_`0.3.0`_** | `~0.25.*` | `>=1.10` | \-  | \-  | \-  |

# Fuzz Instructions - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#fuzz-instructions)

Fuzz Instructions[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#fuzz-instructions "Permanent link")

==========================================================================================================================

Trident defines the `FuzzInstruction` enum, which contains all available **Instructions** within your program. Each enum variant corresponds to one instruction within your program. This enum is crucial for defining how different instructions behave during fuzz testing.

The enum variants additionally contain their corresponding structures for **Accounts** and **Input** arguments.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-1) #[derive(Arbitrary, DisplayIx, FuzzTestExecutor)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-2) pub enum FuzzInstruction {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-3)     Initialize(Initialize),    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-4)     Update(Update), [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-5) } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-6) #[derive(Arbitrary, Debug)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-7) pub struct Initialize {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-8)     pub accounts: InitializeAccounts,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-9)     pub data: InitializeData, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-10) } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-11) #[derive(Arbitrary, Debug)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-12) pub struct Update {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-13)     pub accounts: UpdateAccounts,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-14)     pub data: UpdateData, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-15) } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-0-16) // ...`

Instruction Behavior[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#instruction-behavior "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each Instruction variant must define the `IxOps` trait, which contains the following methods:

*   [`get_discriminator()`](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#get_discriminator)
     (automatically implemented)
*   [`get_program_id()`](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#get_program_id)
     (automatically implemented)
*   [`get_data()`](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#get_data)
     (required)
*   [`get_accounts()`](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#get_accounts)
     (required)
*   [`check()`](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#check)
     (optional)
*   [`tx_error_handler()`](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#tx_error_handler)
     (optional)

`get_discriminator()`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#get_discriminator "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This method specifies the **discriminator** of the instruction.

Tip

*   The IDL created by Anchor 0.29.0 and lower does not contain the discriminator. In that case, the **discriminator** is generated automatically.
*   If you are experiencing errors with the wrong **discriminator**, you can specify it manually by hashing `global:<instruction_name>` with SHA256 and taking the first 8 bytes.

`get_program_id()`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#get_program_id "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This method specifies the **program ID** to which the Instruction corresponds.

`get_data()`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#get_data "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This method specifies what the Instruction Input Data should look like. You can use completely random data generated by the fuzzer, such as:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-1-1) fn get_data(     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-1-2)     &self,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-1-3)     client: &mut impl FuzzClient,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-1-4)     fuzz_accounts: &mut FuzzAccounts, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-1-5) ) -> Result<Vec<u8>, FuzzingError> {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-1-6)     let mut args: Vec<u8> = self.get_discriminator();    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-1-7)     {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-1-8)         args.extend(borsh::to_vec(&self.data.input).unwrap());    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-1-9)     }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-1-10)     Ok(args) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-1-11) }`

You can also use always constant values:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-2-1) fn get_data(     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-2-2)     &self,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-2-3)     client: &mut impl FuzzClient,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-2-4)     fuzz_accounts: &mut FuzzAccounts, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-2-5) ) -> Result<Vec<u8>, FuzzingError> {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-2-6)     let mut args: Vec<u8> = self.get_discriminator();    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-2-7)     {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-2-8)         // The constant value 5 is used as an example        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-2-9)         args.extend(borsh::to_vec(5).unwrap());    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-2-10)     }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-2-11)     Ok(args) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-2-12) }`

Additionally, you can limit the range of the data generated using the `Arbitrary` crate. Check [Arbitrary Data](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/)
.

`get_accounts()`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#get_accounts "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This method specifies the **Accounts** that will be used for the corresponding Instruction. To use multiple combinations of accounts, Trident utilizes the **AccountStorage**, where accounts are stored across the fuzzing process.

There are three main functions to use within the `get_accounts()`:

*   [`get_or_create_account()`](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#get_or_create_account)
    
*   [`get()`](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#get)
    
*   [`set_account_custom()`](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#set_account_custom)
    

For additional methods, check [Account Storage Methods](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/account-storages/#account-storage-methods)
.

### `get_or_create_account()`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#get_or_create_account "Permanent link")

Retrieves a record from AccountsStorage based on the entered `account_id`. If no record exists for the `account_id`, a new empty account is created.

Tip

*   This function is particularly useful for instructions that initialize accounts.

Example:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-3-1) let hello_world_account = fuzz_accounts.hello_world_account.get_or_create_account(     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-3-2)     self.accounts.hello_world_account,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-3-3)     client,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-3-4)     &[b"hello_world_seed"],    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-3-5)     &hello_world::ID, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-3-6) );`

### `get()`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#get "Permanent link")

Retrieves a record from AccountsStorage based on the entered `account_id`. If no record exists for the `account_id`, a **random public key** is returned.

Tip

*   This function is particularly useful for instructions other than those that perform initialization.

Example:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-4-1) let hello_world_account = fuzz_accounts         [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-4-2)         .hello_world_account        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-4-3)         .get(self.accounts.hello_world_account);`

### `set_account_custom()`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#set_account_custom "Permanent link")

If the previous two functions are insufficient, you can use `set_account_custom()` to manually set an account with data you select.

Tip

Example:

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-5-1) let author = fuzz_accounts.author_hello_world.get_or_create_account(     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-5-2)     self.accounts.author,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-5-3)     client,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-5-4)     500 * LAMPORTS_PER_SOL, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-5-5) ); [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-5-6) client.set_account_custom(     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-5-7)     &author.pubkey(),    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-5-8)     &AccountSharedData::create(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-5-9)         10 * LAMPORTS_PER_SOL,        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-5-10)         vec![1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7, 8, 9],        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-5-11)         solana_sdk::system_program::ID,        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-5-12)         false,        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-5-13)         0,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-5-14)     ), [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#__codelineno-5-15) );`

`check()`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#check "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This method provides an Invariant Check for the corresponding Instruction. Check [Invariant Checks](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/invariant-checks/)
.

`tx_error_handler()`[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#tx_error_handler "Permanent link")

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This method provides a Tx Error Handler for the corresponding Instruction. Check [Error Handler](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/error-handlers/)
.

Example[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/fuzz-instructions/#example "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Tip

Consider checking the [Examples](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/examples/examples/)
 section for more tips.

# Customize Instruction Data - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#customize-instruction-data)

Customize Instruction Data[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#customize-instruction-data "Permanent link")

============================================================================================================================================

Trident allows you to customize instruction data.

Trident by default generates random data for instructions, however, you can customize the data to select specific values.

For example, your Initialize Instruction expects two arguments: `start_at` and `end_at`. You know that in order for the Instruction to make sense, it is required that `start_at` < `end_at`. Moreover, there should be a significant difference between these two. This can be utilized with the **Arbitrary crate**.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-0-1) #[derive(Arbitrary, Debug)] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-0-2) pub struct InitVestingData {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-0-3)     pub recipient: AccountId,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-0-4)     #[arbitrary(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-0-5)         with = |u: &mut arbitrary::Unstructured| u.int_in_range(1..=1_000_000)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-0-6)     )]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-0-7)     pub amount: u64,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-0-8)     // we want start_at smaller than end_at    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-0-9)     // and for testing purposes we can run tests with times from the past    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-0-10)     #[arbitrary(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-0-11)         with = |u: &mut arbitrary::Unstructured| u.int_in_range(0..=1_000_000)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-0-12)     )]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-0-13)     pub start_at: u64,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-0-14)     #[arbitrary(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-0-15)         with = |u: &mut arbitrary::Unstructured| u.int_in_range(1_001_001..=1_050_000)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-0-16)     )]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-0-17)     pub end_at: u64,    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-0-18)     #[arbitrary(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-0-19)         with = |u: &mut arbitrary::Unstructured| u.int_in_range(1..=1000)    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-0-20)     )]    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-0-21)     pub interval: u64, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-0-22) }`

Implement Arbitrary[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#implement-arbitrary "Permanent link")

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are macros available to use with Arbitrary, however, it is possible to Implement the arbitrary function by yourself.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-1) // ------------------------------------------------------------------- [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-2) // ------------------------------------------------------------------- [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-3) // Implement Arbitrary [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-4) impl<'a> Arbitrary<'a> for InitVestingData {     [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-5)     fn arbitrary(        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-6)         u: &mut arbitrary::Unstructured<'a>    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-7)     ) -> arbitrary::Result<Self> {        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-8)         // obtain AccountId        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-9)         let recipient = AccountId::arbitrary(u)?; [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-10)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-11)         // limit the generated amount to the 1_000_000        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-12)         let amount = u.int_in_range(1..=1_000_000)?; [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-13)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-14)         // now we want to obtain        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-15)         // - start_at        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-16)         // - end_at        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-17)         // - interval        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-18)         // however we want to limit the data such that:        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-19)         // - start_at < end_at        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-20)         // - end_at - start_at > interval        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-21)         // - interval has lower limit of 500 and upper limit of 1000. [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-22)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-23)         let start_at: u64 = u.int_in_range(1_000_000..=5_000_000)?;        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-24)         let end_at: u64 = u.int_in_range(1_000_000..=5_000_000)?;        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-25)         let interval: u64 = u.int_in_range(500..=1000)?; [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-26)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-27)         // ensure that start_at < end_at        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-28)         if start_at >= end_at {            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-29)             return Err(arbitrary::Error::IncorrectFormat);        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-30)         } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-31)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-32)         // ensure that end_at - start_at > interval        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-33)         match end_at.checked_sub(start_at) {            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-34)             Some(diff) => {                [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-35)                 if diff <= interval {                    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-36)                     return Err(arbitrary::Error::IncorrectFormat);                [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-37)                 }            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-38)             }            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-39)             None => return Err(arbitrary::Error::IncorrectFormat),        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-40)         } [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-41)        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-42)         Ok(InitVestingData {            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-43)             recipient,            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-44)             amount,            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-45)             start_at,            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-46)             end_at,            [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-47)             interval,        [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-48)         })    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-49)     }    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-50)     // -------------------------------------------------------------------    [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-51)     // ------------------------------------------------------------------- [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/customize-ix-data/#__codelineno-1-52) }`

Tip

Consider checking the [Examples](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/examples/examples/)
 section for more tips.

# Trident Manifest - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#trident-manifest)

Trident Manifest[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#trident-manifest "Permanent link")

=======================================================================================================================

You can pass supported parameters via the **Trident.toml** configuration file:

\[fuzz\][#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#fuzz "Permanent link")

---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### programs[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#programs "Permanent link")

*   Use dumped program from desired cluster, during fuzzing.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-0-1) [[fuzz.programs]] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-0-2) address = "metaqbxxUerdq28cj1RbAWkYQm3ybzjb6a8bt518x1s" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-0-3) program = "metaplex-program/metaplex-token-metadata.so"`

* * *

#### accounts[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#accounts "Permanent link")

*   Use dumped accounts from desired cluster, during fuzzing.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-1-1) [[fuzz.accounts]] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-1-2) address = "6YG3J7PaxyMnnbU67ifyrgF3BzNzc7cD8hPkqK6ATweE" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-1-3) filename = "tests/accounts/core_bridge_mainnet/guardian_set_5_mock.json"`

* * *

#### allow\_duplicate\_txs[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#allow_duplicate_txs "Permanent link")

*   Allow processing of duplicate transactions. Setting to true might speed up fuzzing but can cause false positive crashes (default: false).

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-1) [fuzz] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-2) # Allow processing of duplicate transactions. [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-3) # Setting to true might speed up fuzzing but can cause [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-4) # false positive crashes (default: false) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-2-5) allow_duplicate_txs = false`

* * *

#### fuzzing\_with\_stats[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#fuzzing_with_stats "Permanent link")

*   Trident will show statistics after the fuzzing session. This option forces use of honggfuzz parameter `keep_output` as true in order to be able to catch fuzzer stdout. (default: false)

``[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-3-1) [fuzz] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-3-2) # Trident will show statistics after the fuzzing session. [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-3-3) # This option forces use of honggfuzz parameter [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-3-4) # `keep_output` as true in order to be able to catch fuzzer stdout. [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-3-5) # (default: false) [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-3-6) fuzzing_with_stats = true``

#### seeds[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#seeds "Permanent link")

*   Predefined inputs to the AFL
*   You can specify multiple input seeds.

Important

`bytes_count` has precedence before `seed`, in that case if both are specified. Seed is generated as random array of `bytes_count` bytes.

`[](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-23-1) [[afl.seeds]] [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-23-2) # Filename under which the test input is generated. [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-23-3) # The location of file is afl_workspace_in directory. [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-23-4) # (default: "" ["trident-seed"]). [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-23-5) file_name = "" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-23-6) # String used as seed. [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-23-7) # (default: "" ["trident"]). [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-23-8) seed = "" [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-23-9) # If the file already exists at specific location, [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-23-10) # select if override. [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-23-11) # (default: false). [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-23-12) override_file = true [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-23-13) # Number of randomly generated bytes. [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-23-14) # (default: 0). [](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/trident-manifest/#__codelineno-23-15) bytes_count = 20`

# Fuzz Test Lifecycle - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/lifecycle/#fuzz-test-lifecycle)

Fuzz Test Lifecycle[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/lifecycle/#fuzz-test-lifecycle "Permanent link")

======================================================================================================================

In the sequence diagram below you can see a simplified fuzz test lifecycle.

Some diagram states are labeled with emojis:

*   ⚡ Mandatory methods that must be implemented by the user.
*   👤 Optional methods that can be implemented by the user.

Lifecycle[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.8.1/features/lifecycle/#lifecycle "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  The fuzzer is running until:
    1.  The maximal number of iterations is reached (if specified).
    2.  A crash was detected and the `exit_upon_crash` parameter was set.
    3.  User interrupted the test manually (for example by hitting `CTRL+C`).
2.  In each iteration, the fuzzer generates a sequence of random instructions to execute.
    1.  User can optionally customize how the instructions are generated and can specify the instructions that should be executed at the beginning (`pre_ixs`), in the middle (`ixs`) and at the end (`post_ixs`) of each iteration. This can be useful for example if your program needs an initialization or you want to fuzz some specific program state.
3.  For each instruction:
    1.  User defined mandatory method `get_accounts()` is called to collect necessary instruction accounts.
    2.  User defined mandatory method `get_data()` is called to collect instruction data.
    3.  A snapshot of all instruction accounts before the instruction execution is saved.
    4.  The instruction is executed.
    5.  A snapshot of all instruction accounts after the instruction execution is saved.
    6.  User defined optional method `check()` is called to check accounts data and evaluate invariants.

fuzzer\_iterations = 0

fuzzer\_iterations = 0

fuzzer\_iterations < 

max\_iterations

fuzzer\_iterations <...

done

done

create pre-instruction 

accounts snapshots

create pre-instruction...

execute instruction

execute instruction

create post-instruction 

accounts snapshots

create post-instruction...

check invariants 👤

check invariants 👤

fuzzer\_iterations++

fuzzer\_iterations++Generate instructions

pre\_ixs 👤

pre\_ixs 👤

ixs 👤

ixs 👤

post\_ixs 👤

post\_ixs 👤

end

end

for ix in instructions

for ix in instructions

get instruction accounts ⚡

get instruction accounts ⚡

get instruction data ⚡

get instruction data ⚡

next ix

# Fuzz Test Lifecycle - Trident

 

[Skip to content](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/lifecycle/#fuzz-test-lifecycle)

Fuzz Test Lifecycle[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/lifecycle/#fuzz-test-lifecycle "Permanent link")

======================================================================================================================

In the sequence diagram below you can see a simplified fuzz test lifecycle.

Some diagram states are labeled with emojis:

*   ⚡ Mandatory methods that must be implemented by the user.
*   👤 Optional methods that can be implemented by the user.

Lifecycle[#](https://ackee.xyz/trident/docs/0.9.1/features/lifecycle/#lifecycle "Permanent link")

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  The fuzzer is running until:
    1.  The maximal number of iterations is reached (if specified).
    2.  A crash was detected and the `exit_upon_crash` parameter was set.
    3.  User interrupted the test manually (for example by hitting `CTRL+C`).
2.  In each iteration, the fuzzer generates a sequence of random instructions to execute.
    1.  User can optionally customize how the instructions are generated and can specify the instructions that should be executed at the beginning (`pre_ixs`), in the middle (`ixs`) and at the end (`post_ixs`) of each iteration. This can be useful for example if your program needs an initialization or you want to fuzz some specific program state.
3.  For each instruction:
    1.  User defined mandatory method `get_accounts()` is called to collect necessary instruction accounts.
    2.  User defined mandatory method `get_data()` is called to collect instruction data.
    3.  A snapshot of all instruction accounts before the instruction execution is saved.
    4.  The instruction is executed.
    5.  A snapshot of all instruction accounts after the instruction execution is saved.
    6.  User defined optional method `check()` is called to check accounts data and evaluate invariants.
